[I,1,i_I,1,ii]	namaḥ buddhāya jayati sugataḥ kṛpā ātmā dharmaḥ nairyāṇikaḥ sadā jayati sakala tribhuvana pūjyaḥ prathita guṇaḥ jayati ca ārya gaṇaḥ param anugṛhṇan prāptaiḥ paratas api hi vastubhiḥ satām ślāghyaḥ labdhaiḥ anya mataiḥ api tat kartum para hitam yuktam tat atīva viprakīrṇāni ācāryāṇām matāni aśaknuvataḥ ālocayitum samyak janasya mattaḥ api manda mateḥ āhṛtya dharma kīrteḥ anyeṣām ca eva khalu matāt kiñcid tat darśitayā ca diśā svayam abhyūhya prayatnena udbhāvita artha tattva svādu rasaḥ ayam mayā upakārāya diś nāga nīti śāstra vyākhyāna karambakaḥ kriyate 
[I,1,iii]	pramāṇa bhūtāya ityādi yathā tvam meruḥ tvam samudraḥ asi nātha tvam kalpapādapaḥ tvam su vaidyaḥ pradīpaḥ tvam tvam eva paramaḥ plavaḥ iti atra iva śabda prayogam antareṇa api tad arthaḥ gamyate tathā iha api iti bhagavān pramāṇam iva pramāṇam yathā hi pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇam puruṣa artha upayoginaḥ anadhigatasya arthasya prakāśakam avisaṃvādakam ca tathā bhagavān api yatra paraḥ puruṣa arthaḥ pratibaddhaḥ catur ārya satya lakṣaṇe tattve tad viṣayam jñānam āsādya niḥśreyasa arthinām tasya anadhigatasya prakāśakaḥ avisaṃvādakaḥ ca tasmāt pramāṇa sādharmyāt pramāṇam bhūtaḥ jātaḥ utpannaḥ iti arthaḥ bhūta vacanam abhūtasya nityasya īśvara ādeḥ pramāṇasya para parikalpitasya pratiṣedha artham pramāṇam ca asau bhūtaḥ ca iti pramāṇa bhūtaḥ tasmai pramāṇa bhūtāya 
[I,2,i]	nanu ca dvitīyayā atra bhavitavyam yathā asya eva vivaraṇe evac guṇam śāstāram praṇamya iti satyam śiṣṭa prayoga anusāri tvāt vivakṣāyāḥ yadā karma kārakam vivakṣyate yadā tu prārthanā adhyavasāya kriyābhyām āptum iṣṭama tvāt labdha karma vyapadeśayā praṇati kriyayā abhipreyamāṇasya sampradāna tvam vivakṣyate tadā caturthī ā iva nyāyyā yathā tathiva prāpta karma sañjñena śayanena abhipreyamāṇa tvāt patyuḥ sampradāna vivakṣāyām patye śetaḥ iti atra caturthī ā iva bhavati tathā iha api iti adoṣaḥ 
[I,2,ii]	jagat hita eṣiṇaḥ iti jagat dhitam heya upādeyayoḥ sa abhyupāyayoḥ ātyantike hāna upādāne tad eṣaṇa śīlāya praṇamya iti manaḥ vāt lāyaiḥ praṇāmam kṛtvā asya ca samuccayaḥ kariṣyate iti anena sambandhaḥ etena praṇāmataḥ pūjā jihitā śāstre iti iṭaḥ atra abhāvaḥ tṛntṛcau śaṃsikṣat ādibhyaḥ sañjñāyām ca aniṭau bahulam anyatra api iti vacanāt duḥkha kṣaya upāya upadeśaḥ śāsanam tasya kartā śāstā iti ucyate phalau asthāyām iha tu tasya eva śāsanasya hetau mārga abhyāse phala upacārāt śāsana śabdaḥ vartate tad śāsanam kurvan bhagavān bodhisattva avasthāyām śastṛ śabdena uktaḥ 
[I,3,i_I,3,ii]	sugatāya iti suṣṭhu gataḥ prāptaḥ sarvathā sarva praheya prahāṇam iti sugataḥ tāyinaḥ iti tāyate anena iti tāyaḥ sa punar sva dṛṣṭa mārga upadeśaḥ saḥ asya asti iti tāyī sarva prekṣā pūrva kāriṇām ārambhasya prayojanena vyāpta tvāt tat nivartamānam ārambham api nivartayati tat ca asya na asti tasmāt na ārabdhavyam idam yasya prayojanam na asti na tat prekṣāvatārabdhavyam tat yathā ananuṣṭheya viṣaya jñāna parīkṣaṇam upadeṣṭari na asti ca asya tat vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ asya asiddhim udbhāvitum āha pramāṇa siddhyā iti pramāṇa siddhiḥ pramāṇa vyutpattiḥ tad artham idam tasmāt ārabdhavyam yat sa prayojanam tat prekṣāvatārabdhavyam tat yathā anuṣṭheya viṣaya jñāna parīkṣaṇam upadeṣṭari sa prayojanam ca idam svabhāvaḥ 
[I,4,i^1]	yadi tarhi etat artham idam ārabhyate na ārabdhavyam pramāṇa siddheḥ nyāya mukha ādinā eva sva matena tvayā prāk eva sādhita tvāt yat sādhitam na tat siddhaye prekṣāvata ārambhaḥ kartavyaḥ tat yathā sādhitasya odanasya sādhitā ca pramāṇa siddhiḥ vyāpaka viruddhaḥ asya nirāsāya āha sva matāt viprasṛtāt iti hetau iyam pañcamī prasṛtam prasaraṇam vistaraḥ iti yāvat punar tantreṇa āvṛtteḥ aneka śakteḥ vā asya eva ayam aparaḥ arthaḥ sarve gati arthāḥ jñāna arthāḥ iti sṛtam avagamaḥ parijñānam prakṛṣṭam sṛtam prasṛtam vigatam prasṛtam yatas 
[I,4,i^2]	tat viprasṛtam sva matam nyāya mukha ādi vigata prasṛta pramāṇa vyutpattikam tathā hi tatra pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti asya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇasya na apavādaḥ kṛtaḥ tatas ca dvi candra ādi jñānasya api pratyakṣatā prasaṅgaḥ vigata vistaram ca tad saṅkṣiptam tena yaḥ eva uddhaṭita jñaḥ diś mātra darśanena api anuktam abhyūhitum artham samarthaḥ tasya eva vyutpattiḥ bhavati na itarasya tathā hi tatra eva mukha mātram idam sat arthanīteḥ iti ādeḥ ślokasya pūrva ardhena sudhiyaḥ eva saṅkṣipta ruceḥ upakārāya idam kṛtam iti sūcitam 
[I,4,i^3]	kusṛtīḥ ityādinā tu uttara ardhena na itareṣām anena anugrahaḥ bhavati iti tīrthya tarka bhramitāḥ manda dhiyaḥ vistareṇa pratipādyāḥ kṛsṛtīḥ apavidhya katham artha tattva bhājaḥ syuḥ na eva iti artha gateḥ kathaṃśabdena hi atra asambhavaḥ dyotyate ye tu uddhaṭita dhī viṣayam āsaṃsa artham vyācakṣate katham nāma uddhaṭita dhīviṣāḥ ku mārgam apāsya tīrthya tarka bhramitā bhūyāsūḥ artha tattva bhājaḥ iti teṣām tat ayuktam sthavīyāṃsaḥ hi doṣāḥ tīrthyataka arṇām te tathāvidhaiḥ sukham eva upalakṣyante ye anuktam api nāma duravabodham artham diś mātra darśanena svayam utprekṣitum kṣamāḥ te su upa lakṣya sthūlatara doṣaiḥ tīrthya tarkaiḥ unmārgeṇa tīyante iti asambhāvanīyam etat tat evam evaṃvidham yatas sva matam na tena sarveṣām pramāṇa vyutpattiḥ kṛtā tasmāt sva matāt saṅkṣiptāt akṛta prakṛṣṭa pramāṇa vyutpatteḥ hetoḥ manda dhiyām api vastara rucīnām upakārāya sa utsargaḥ sa apavādaḥ sa vistaraḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ pramāṇa vyutpattaye pramāṇa samuccayaḥ kariṣyate 
[I,5,i]	tat kim tatra eva nyāya mukha ādau ekaikasmin prakaraṇe apara grantha prakṣepeṇa samuccayaḥ kariṣyate iti praśna avasaraḥ āha iha ekatas iti iha asmin ekasmin prakaraṇe sukha avabodha artham samuccayaḥ kariṣyate viprakīrṇaḥ hi granthaḥ prakaraṇa bhedena na sukham ālocayitum śakyate ekatas iti ādi a ādi tvāt tasiḥ tathā hi śiṣṭa prayogaḥ caraka saṃhitāyām yāni iha karmāṇi uktāni visarpāṇām praśāntaye ekatas tāni sarvāṇi rakta mokṣaṇam ekatas iti 
[I,6,i]	atra iti śloke bhagavataḥ iti bhaga śabdaḥ ayam aiśvarya ādiṣu vartate yathā uktam aiśvaryasya samagrasya vairyasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ jñānasya atha prayatnasya eṇṇām bhagaḥ iti śrutiḥ iti etat ca samagram tathāgataḥ eva asti iti saḥ eva bhagavān māra catuṣṭayam vā bhagnavān iti bhagavān naiḥ uktena vidhinā tasya stotra abhidhānam stūyate anena iti stotram sat bhūta guṇa udbhāvana vacanam a abhidhānam iha vivakṣitasya arthasya śabdena pratyāyanam abhisaṃhitam stotreṇa abhidhānam stuti padena guṇavat tayā prakāśanam iti arthaḥ kena guṇena tathā aprakāśanam iti āha pramāṇa bhūta tvena iti sa punar guṇaḥ kena hetunā iti āha hetu phala sampattyā iti hetu phalayoḥ sampattiḥ prakarṣaḥ tena hetunā yat pramāṇa bhūta tvam asādhāraṇaḥ guṇaḥ tena karaṇena hetunā vā stotra abhidhānam stuti padena bhagavataḥ guṇavat tayā śrotṛbhyaḥ pratipādanam iti yāvat 
[I,7,i^1]	tat punar kim artham iti āha prakaraṇa ādau gaurava utpādana artham iti katham punar bhagavataḥ stotra abhidhānena prakaraṇa ārambhe gauravam bhavati yatas satsu api anyeṣu guṇeṣu prāmāṇyena guṇena stuvatā etat sūcitam ācāryeṇa yat etat pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa lakṣaṇam tat bhagavat upadeśāt eva siddham na idānīm savayam utprekṣya mayā vyavasthāpyate iti atas eva abhidharme api uktam iti uktam yuktam tāvat pratyakṣasya tatas siddhiḥ tad upadeśa darśanāt anupadiṣṭasya tu anumānasya katham tasya api prayoga darśanāt vihitam eva lakṣaṇam gamyate yathā yat kiñcid samudaya dharmakam 
[I,7,i^2]	tat nirodha dharmakam iti ādayaḥ anumāna prayogāḥ bhagavataḥ dṛśyante katham evam ucyamāne anumānasya lakṣaṇam uktam bhavati yasmāt anumānasya āśrayaḥ avinābhāvi liṅgam anena ca prayogena sādhyena nirodhena utpādasya liṅgasya sphuṭam eva avinābhāvaḥ uktaḥ bhagavatā atas anumāna lakṣaṇam api bhagavat upadeśāt eva siddham tasmāt bhagavat upadeśa asiddha pramāṇa lakṣaṇa anuvidhāyī etat prakaraṇam iti jāta niśccayānām prasiddha śāstṛkāṇām tatra gauravam jāyate tatas ca adyatya śravaṇa ādau pravartante 
[I,7,ii]	atha vā atra prakaraṇa ādau bhagavataḥ stotra abhidhānam stutye bhagavati gaurava utpādana artham katham anena tatra gauravam jāyate yasmāt anena ślokena sa upapatta ekam pramāṇa bhūta tvam bhagavataḥ guṇaḥ udbhāvitaḥ tasmāt prāk aprasiddha śāstṛkāṇām api tatra gauravam utpadyate kim punar itareṣām tat gauravāt ca upacita puṇya sambhārāṇām prakaraṇa udgrahaṇāya pravṛttānām na vinayakāḥ prabhavanti iti tat gauravam api sa prayojanam eva 
[I,8,i]	nanu ca kaiḥ cit tathāvidha puruṣa pratiṣedhāya puruṣa tva ādi sādhana anīkam prayuktam tat katham tatra stotra abhidhānena gauravam bhavati yatas tad agamakam pratikṣepa sāmānya sādhanayoḥ asambhavāt na hi atīndriyeṣu atat darśinaḥ pratikṣepaḥ sambhavati satām api eṣām ajñānāt atas eva virodha asiddheḥ avirodhinā ca sahabhāva avirodhāt na api itara puruṣa sāmānya siddhiḥ viśeṣa asambhavasya jñātum aśakya tvāt īdṛśeṣu ca anupalabdheḥ hetu tva ayogāt puṃstva ādi sāmānye api kasyacid medhā ādeḥ guṇa viśeṣasya darśanāt tadvat sati saṃskāre anyasya api sambhāvāt sambhavat viśeṣe ca sāmānya asiddheḥ tasmāt śeṣavat anumānam etat vyatirekasya sandehāt asamartham adarśane api vipakṣa vṛtteḥ na ca tasya tathāvidha jñā lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam asambhāvanīyam tad sādhana anuṣṭhāna sambhavāt yaḥ yat sādhanam aviparītam anutiṣṭhati tasya sambhavati tad prāptiḥ tat yathā ārogya sādhanam aviparītam anutiṣṭhavān ca bhagavān svabhāvaḥ 
[I,9,i^1]	yat sādhana anuṣṭhānāt ca prāmāṇya prāptiḥ sambhavati tat darśayan āha tatra hetuḥ āśaya prayoga sampad iti āśayam darśayati āśayaḥ jagat hita eṣitā iti sā punar sakala jagat ātyantika duḥkha viyoga prārthana ākārān alpa kalpa abhyāsena sa ātmībhūtā karuṇā śloke jagat hita eṣiṇaḥ iti anena darśitā tad yogāt dhi jagat hita eṣī bhavati abhyāsāt ca sa ātmībhāvaḥ tasyāḥ sambhavati ye manaḥ guṇāḥ te atyanta abhyāsa sambhave sati sātmībhavanti 
[I,9,i^2]	śrotriya joṭiṅganaiḥ ghṛṇya vat manoguṇaḥ ca karuṇā svabhāvaḥ sa tayā para artham prati preryamāṇaḥ svayam asākṣāt kṛtya na pāryate parebhyaḥ deśayitum duḥkha praśama upāyaḥ iti sva duḥkha uparama upāya bhāvanā artham tāvat prayujyate iti darśayan āha prayogaḥ jagat śāsanāt ityādi yasya yatra dayā sa tayā yathā tasya arthaḥ bhavati tathā prayujyate yathā mātuḥ putre dayā sā ca yathā tasya arthaḥ bhavati tathā prayujyate āsīt ca bhagavataḥ jagati dayā svabhāvaḥ jagat śāsanam mukhyam sva dṛṣṭa duḥkha upaśama upāya upadeśaḥ iha tu kāraṇe kārya upacāram kṛtvā upāya abhyāsaḥ jagat śāsana śabda ūna uktaḥ tasya sattva śāsana yogya upāya tvena tat anya upāya abhyāsāt viśiṣṭa tva jñāpana artham 
[I,10,i^1]	jagat śāsanāt iti lakṣṇa hetuḥ ayam tena yathā kāṭhinyāt pṛthivī iti ukte kāṭhinya svabhāvā pṛthivī iti gamyate tathā jagat śāsanāt śāstṛ tvam iti ukte tad svabhāvam śāstṛ tvam iti sa pañca upādāna skandha lakṣaṇam duḥkham kādācid katvena hetunā anityam atas eva ca anitya hetukam śakyam etat dhetu kṣayeṇa kṣapayityum nidāna kṣayeṇa vyādhiḥ iva na anyathā iti ca niścitya kaḥ asya hetuḥ iti vicārayan duḥkha hetum ātma snehavataḥ tṛṣṇām eva prādhānyena evam avagatavān yaḥ ananya satvaneyaḥ yābhiḥ ati pūrvakaḥ hīna sthāna parigrahaḥ 
[I,10,i^2]	saḥ ātma snehavataḥ duḥkha sukha tyāga āptivān chāpu urvakaḥ tat yathā makṣikāṇām abhirati pūrvakaḥ aśuci sthāna parigrahaḥ ananya sattva neyaḥ yābhiḥ ati pūrvakaḥ ca garbha ādi hīna sthāna parigrahaḥ prāṇinaḥ iti kāryam sā eva ca tṛṣṇā prādhānyena śāstre samudaya satyam iti ucyate prādhānyam punar tad samutthāpita prayatna vaśena utpatti deśa gamanāt ānantaryāt ca sati api hi ajñāne vān chāntareṇa pravṛtteḥ asambhavāt karmaṇaḥ api tṛṣṇā eva pradhānam tathā hi sat api karma yāvat avidyāpam su avacchāditam na bhavati tṛṣṇā sra iha abhiṣyanditam ca 
[I,10,i^3]	na tāvat phala vat bhavati yathārhatām tatas tasyāḥ api tṛṣṇāyāḥ tad anyeṣām ca doṣāṇām ātma darśanam eva prabhavam evam vyavasitavān na hi na aham na mama iti paśyataḥ parigraham antareṇa kvacid snehaḥ na ca asnehavataḥ kvacid dveṣaḥ ātmā ātmīya anuparodhini uparodha pratighātini ca tad abhāvāt tad samāna jātīya abhyāsa jam ātma darśanam ātmīya sreham prasūte sa dveṣa ādīn iti sat kāya darśana jāḥ sarve tṛṣṇā ādayaḥ doṣāḥ tat eva ca ajñānam iti ucyate jñāna vipakṣa tvāt tasya tat eva ātma darśanam yatas doṣa hetuḥ 
[I,10,i^4]	tatas sambhavati tad kṣayāt tṛṣṇāyāḥ tad anyeṣām ca doṣāṇām kṣayaḥ iti matvā ātma darśana pratipakṣam parīkṣate sma yat abhyāsena tat prahātavyam parīkṣamāṇaḥ ca ātma darśanasya tad viparīta ākāra tvāt nairātmya darśanam eva pratipakṣam evam avajagāma yaḥ yat viparīta svabhāvaḥ sa tasya pratipakṣaḥ tat yathā vāyu viparīta svabhāvam tailam vāyoḥ ātma darśana viparīta svabhāvam ca nairātmya darśanam iti svabhāvaḥ ātma darśana viruddham ca nairātmya darśanam tat pūrvakasya ātma sneha ādeḥ api doṣa gaṇasya viruddham eva iti evam ajñāsīt yaḥ yat nidāna viruddhaḥ sa tasya bādhakaḥ yathā vātikasya vyādheḥ tat nidāna viruddham tailam ātma sneha ādi nidāna ātma darśana viruddham ca nairātmya darśanam iti svabhāvaḥ evam jñātvā tasya tat nairātmya darśanam bahuśas bahudhā dīrgham ca kālam abhyasyataḥ tatra tad vipakṣe ca sarvathā guṇa doṣāḥ prakāśa tām īyuḥ yaḥ yat prājñaḥ bahuśas bahudhā dīrgham ca kālam 
[I,10,i^5]	abhyasyati tasya tatra tad vipakṣe ca guṇa doṣāḥ prakāśībhavanti tat yathā kasyacid prājñasya kvacid śilpa viśeṣe abhiyuktasya abhyasyataḥ abhyastavān ca bhagavān nairātmya darśanam bahuśas bahudhā dīrgham ca kālam svabhāvaḥ ayam eva ca upāya abhyāsaḥ mārga satyam iti ucyate tasya evaṃvidhāt upāya abhyāsāt ananya sādhāraṇāt duḥkha hetoḥ vāsanā api na avaśiṣyate ayam eva ca bhagavataḥ khaḍga ādeḥ viśeṣaḥ para artha pradhāna vṛttinā ca anena avaśyam evaṃvidhaḥ abhyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ aparijñāta sakala vipakṣa pratipakṣeṇa parebhyaḥ vipakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ upadeṣṭum aśakya tvāt iti ayam upāya abhyāsaḥ pūrva nirdiṣṭā ca karuṇā hetu sampad 
[I,12,i]	asyāḥ phalam sva para artha sampad tatra sva artha sampad yathā uktāt upāya abhyāsā duḥkha hetoḥ pūrvasya svarasam nirodhe nairātmya darśana sātmye avasthitasya uttara duḥkha hetu anutpatti lakṣṇaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ yasya nirodha satyam iti ākhyā saḥ eva viśeṣaṇa traya viśiṣṭam sugata tvam iti ucyate tām sva artha sampadam darśayan āha sva artha sampad su gata tvena ityādi su śabdaḥ ayam iha praśasta tva ādeḥ arthasya dyotakaḥ veditavyaḥ yat āha trividham artham upādāya ityādi 
[I,13,i_I,13,ii]	praśastam gataḥ prāptaḥ sugataḥ praśasta tvam punar duḥkhasya apunar āśraya tvena loke hi sukham tat anubandhi ca praśastam iti ucyate tat ca duḥkhān āśrayaṇam nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ su abhyasta tvāt atha vā anantara uktena upāyena yukti dṛṣṭena gamanāt praśastam gataḥ loke hi yaḥ yukti pūrvakam pravartate sa praśasyate apunarāvṛtti gamanāt sugataḥ apunarāvṛttiḥ tu janma doṣa an utpādaḥ sa ca tad hetoḥ pūrvakasya abhāvāt yasya ātma darśana snehau na staḥ na tasya janma rāga ādi doṣa utpādaḥ tat yathā ākāśasya na staḥ ca ātma darśana snehau sa ātmībhūta nairātmya darśanasya kāraṇa abhāvaḥ 
[I,13,iii]	niḥśeṣam gataḥ sugataḥ nirgatam śeṣam asya iti vigrahaḥ śeṣam punar kāya ādi vaiguṇyam tat punar yathākramam acāpale api abhyāsāt utplutya gamana ādi aham māna abhāve api vṛṣalī vāda ādi nitya asamādhānena asamāhita citta avasthānam ca atha vā tathāvidhasya mārga abhyāsasya abhāvena atyartham aparijñānāt mārga tad vipakṣayoḥ adhigatasya api mārgasya vibhajya aprakāśana pāṭavam śeṣam tat api bhagavataḥ prahīṇam iti atas asau sugataḥ 
[I,13,iv_I,14,i]	artha trayam ca etat ityādi tatra bāhya vīta rāgāḥ ātma darśana anupātena duḥkha āśrayeṇa mārgeṇa gamanāt tad vaśena eva punar duḥkham āśrayante na ca yukti dṛṣṭena mārgeṇa gatāḥ iti atas te na praśastam gatāḥ tathā hi loke yaḥ duḥkham āśrayati ayukti pūrvakam ca pravartate sa na praśasyate api tu nindyate eva śaikṣāḥ tu yadi api duḥkhān āśrayeṇa yukti niścitena ca mārgeṇa praśastam gatāḥ tathā api teṣām doṣāṇām janmanaḥ ca punar utpādaḥ iti te api na dvitīyena arthena sugatāḥ aśaikṣāḥ punar kāmam artha dvayena sugatāḥ na tu niḥśeṣa arthena yathā uktasya śeṣasya aprahāṇāt para artha sampad tāraṇa arthena iti anena tāya śabdasya artham ācaṣṭe tāryante saṃsāra sāgaram anena sattvāḥ iti tāraṇaḥ sva dṛṣṭa mārga upadeśaḥ saḥ eva arthaḥ arthyate mokṣa upāya kāmaiḥ iti kṛtvā saḥ asya asti iti tena arthena bhagavataḥ tāyi tvam ayam eva hi tāyateḥ paraḥ pālana arthaḥ yat uta saṃsāra sāgara tāraṇam 
[I,14,ii]	na ca tasya viparīta upadeśa tā sambhāvyate tad kāraṇa abhāvāt kṛpā ātmaka tvāt mārgasya ca su pratividdha tvāt rāga ādayaḥ hi doṣāḥ mithyā abhidhāna getavaḥ prayojanam vā kiñcid tat ca na asti sā ātmībhūta kṛpaḥ ca para artham eva duḥkha kṣaya upāyam sādhayitvā katham anyathā brūyāt yasya yadā anṛta vacana kāraṇāni na santi na sa tadā anṛtam vakti tat yathā anyaḥ kaścid satya vacana kāle na santi ca sugata avasthā kāle tasya anṛta kāraṇāni kāraṇa abhāvaḥ yaḥ yat artha karaṇāya yat kṛpayā yam artham sādhayati na sa tat artha niṣpattau aparityakta tad viṣaya dayaḥ tam tatra vañcayati tat yathā suta pathi abhijanāya prasādhita āhārā mātā sattva artha karaṇāya sattva kṛpayā duḥkha kṣaya upāyam sādhitavān aparityakta tad viṣaya dayaḥ ca bhagavān vyāpaka viruddhaḥ tasmāt pramāṇam yaḥ yat arthine tat artha upāyam aviparītam kathayati sa tasya tatra pramāṇam tat yathā ārogya arthinaḥ ārogya upāyam aviparītam kathayan āturasya tatra vaidyaḥ duḥkha kṣaya arthine duḥkhayā upāyam aviparītam kathitavān ca bhagavān svabhāvaḥ 
[I,15,i_I,15,ii]	tat evam pramāṇa bhūtāya iti etat eva stuti padam anena hi bhagavataḥ jñāna lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam asādhāraṇaḥ guṇaḥ udbhāvitaḥ yatas tad yogāt sa pramāṇam bhavati sa tu guṇaḥ na vinā hetunā niṣpadyate iti darśayatā hetu sampad uktā sugata śabdena tu tasya jñānasya vipakṣa prahāṇa viśeṣaḥ phala sampad saṅgṛhītaḥ uktaḥ tasmin asati utplutya ādi gamana vat vākya prāpaṇīyasya arthasya ayuktasya api sūcakam kāya ceṣṭitam kuryāt vṛṣalī vāda ādi vat anyat api asatyam kadācid abhidadhyāt nitya asamāhita tvena vā avyākya akṛta avasthāyām na sakala sattva artha karaṇa samarthaḥ syāt na vā pāṭav avipakṣasya sa vāsanasya aprahāṇāt asya adhigata mārga prakāśana pāṭavam syāt tasmin tu sati ete doṣāḥ na bhavati iti darśayitum prahāṇa viśeṣaḥ uktaḥ 
[I,16,i_I,16,ii]	tāyin iti anena tu tasya eva jñānasya kārya viśeṣaḥ yathā dṛṣṭa mārga upadeśaḥ darśitaḥ sa yadi na syāt tat prāmāṇyam eva na syāt tathāvidham hi yadi tasya kāryam bhavati evam tad yogāt bhagavān anadhigatasya arthasya prakāśakaḥ bhavati tatra vā avisaṃvādakaḥ na anyathā iti atas kārya viśeṣaḥ darśitaḥ karuṇā tu bodhisattva avasthāyām eva yā svarasa vāhinī abhūt sā sugata avasthāyām anukta siddhā eva iti na uktā tayā hi vinā na eva hitam upadeṣṭum utsaheta iti sā api tasya parātham prati sahāya bhūtā veditavyā tat evam bhagavataḥ jñāna lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam tāvat ānulomyena vyākhyā yatra kṛpā ādibhiḥ śāstṛ tva ādīnām sambhavaḥ anumīyate 
[I,16,iii]	idānīm prātilomyena vyākhyā kriyate atha vā tāyaḥ aviparīta satya upadeśaḥ tam duḥkha upaśama hetum sattvebhyaḥ deśitavān bhagavān iti sa teṣām tad arthinām tatra pramāṇam yaḥ yat duḥkha praśama arthine yasmai tat duḥkha svabhāvam ca tat duḥkha hetum ca tat duḥkha praśamam ca tat duḥkha praśama upāyam ca yathābhūtam kathayati sa tasya tatra pramāṇam tat yathā vyādhi duḥkha praśama arthinaḥ āturāya vyādhi duḥkha svabhāva bhāva ādikam yathābhūtam kathayan tasya tatra vaidyaḥ saṃsāra duḥkha praśama arthine puruṣāya saṃsāra duḥkha svabhāva ādikam yathābhūtam kathitavān ca bhagavān svabhāvaḥ 
[I,17,i]	tāni ca satyāni leśataḥ darśitāni yathā duḥkham pañca upādāna skandha lakṣaṇam tasya ca samudayaḥ tṛṣṇā tatas ca duḥkhasya utpattiḥ yathā prayujyate nirodhaḥ mārga sātmye avasthitasya pūrva duḥkha hetu nirodhe sati uttara duḥkha hetu anutpatti lakṣaṇaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ mārgaḥ nairātmya darśana abhyāsaḥ yathā ca tatas nirodha prāptiḥ bhavati tat sarvam prāk eva saṅkṣepataḥ darśitam tasmāt bhavati sati acatuṣṭaya darśanāt muktiḥ tatas ca tad upadeśaḥ saṃsāra arṇava uttaraṇa sādhana tvāt tāyaḥ etāvat eva ca para hita eṣiṇā kāryam yat uta heya upādeya tattvasya sa abhyupāyasya upadeśaḥ sa ca bhagavatā kṛtaḥ tat etasmāt kāryāt praśasta tva ādi viśeṣaṇa traya viśiṣṭam jñānam anumīyate gameḥ bodha arthaḥ teha āśrayaṇāt pūrvam prāpti artham gamim āśritya prahāṇa sampad phalam uktam 
[I,17,ii^1]	samprati jñāna sampad praśastam avabuddhavān yāvat aśeṣam avabuddhavān iti evam sugata tvam veditavyam tatra praśasta tvam tasya jñānasya tattva viṣaya tvāt tat punar pramāṇa saṃvādāt tad deśitasya mārgasya anumīyate apunarāvṛtti tvam sthira tvāt tat punar mārgasya tat niścitasya pramāṇa antareṇa ābādhanāt avasīyate avicalasya vā pūrva apara vacanā vyāhatyā sarvatra pravacane catur ārya satya deśanāyāḥ eka vākya tvāt śeṣam punar atra catuṣu ārya satyeṣu adhigateṣu api jñānasya pratipādanā kauśalam tad abhāva śeṣa jñānam anumīyate citraiḥ upāyaiḥ satya prakāśanāt śrāvakāṇām tu kiñcit mātram kauśalam tat api tad anuśikṣaṇataḥ atas tattva sthira tva aśeṣa tva viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭena jñānena bāhya vīta rāgebhyaḥ adhikaḥ tathā hi na teṣām pramāṇa saṃvādi heya upādeya viṣayam jñānam sthira tva viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭena śaikṣebhyaḥ 
[I,17,ii^2]	teṣām anabhisaṃskārikāyāḥ satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ aprahāṇāt tad samudācāra kaleṣu parāvṛtti sambhavāt aśeṣa tva viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭena aśaikṣebhyaḥ teṣām yathā ukta śeṣa sambhavāt evaṃvidha jñānāt para arthaḥ mārga abhyāsaḥ avasīyate yatas tad adhigamya api na uparata vyāpāraḥ abhūt pratyeka jina vat kim tarhi yathā adhigata mārga ākhyāna tatparaḥ eva āsīt yaḥ yasmin adhigate api avirata vyāpāraḥ na sa tanmātra phala abhikāṅkṣī tat yathā annadhigame api avirata vyāpāraḥ bhojanāya pravṛttaḥ adhigate api ca yathā ukte jñāna viśeṣe na tāvatā uparata vyāpāraḥ abhūt bhagavān vyāpaka viruddhaḥ saḥ eva ca mārga abhyāsaḥ śastṛ tvam upacārāt iti uktam etat 
[I,19,i_I,19,ii]	tatas api dayā anumīyate dayāvān iha para arthe prayujyate na anyaḥ tat evaṃvidhayā hetu phala sampadā bhagavān pramāṇam tathā hi kṛpayā artham eva upadeṣṭum icchati niṣkaruṇaḥ tu jānan api anyathā kathayet iti kṛpāyāḥ prāmāṇye aṅga bhāvaḥ dayāvān api ajñānāt tattvam eva upadeṣṭum akṣamaḥ jñānāt tu bhūtam eva upadiśati iti jñāna asya api prāmāṇyam prati sādhana bhāvaḥ tat ca prāmāṇyam sa hetukam tatas asya yuktaḥ sadbhāvaḥ iti hetu sampad uktā na tu tathāvidhāyām phala sampadi satyām tasyāḥ kaścana upayogaḥ yadi hi vinā api hetu sampadā sā phala sampad syāt syāt eva prāmāṇyam sā tu tayā vinā na sambhavati iti tad anupādānam 
[I,19,iii]	tāyi tvena avaśyam abhiyogavān para avabodhanam prati iti etat darśitam tat evam yatas śreyaḥ bhūtam ācaṣṭe tad ākhyāne ca yatnavān tasmāt pramāṇam yaḥ yasmai śreyaḥ bhūtam ācaṣṭe tad ākhyāne ca yatnavān sa tena viduṣā pramāṇayitavyaḥ tat yathā yathā uktaiḥ guṇaiḥ śiṣyāya upadiśan upādhyāyaḥ viduṣā śiṣyeṇa sattvebhyaḥ śreyaḥ bhūtam ācaṣṭe ca tad ākhyāne ca yatnavān bhagavān svabhāvaḥ 
[I,20,i]	atra vyākhyā prakāre codyate yadi jñānam api prāmāṇyasya sādhana tvena vyavasthāpyate tat kim punar tat prāmāṇyam yasya karuṇā ādayaḥ sādhanam iti vaktavyam ucyate sāmarthya viśeṣaḥ yasmin sati bhagavān anadhigatam artham gamayati tatra ca avisaṃvādakaḥ bhavati sa tu sāmarthya viśeṣaḥ karuṇā ādibhiḥ yuktasya bhavati na itarasya iti tasya sādhana tvena vyavasthāpyate 
[I,20,ii_I,20,iii]	sva prakaraṇebhyaḥ iti etat sva matāt iti asya vyākhyānam mukha śabdena eva ca pūrva uktaḥ prasṛta śabdasya arthaḥ sphuṭam eva gamyate iti na vibhaktaḥ mukham hi dvāram diś mātra darśanam saṅkṣiptam na ca tena vistara pratipādyānām vyutpattiḥ bhavati iti prasiddham eva etat bahuṣu api mata sāmānyāt śloke sva matāt iti eka vacanam vṛttau tu bheda vivakṣāyām sva prakaraṇebhyaḥ iti bahuvacanam samāhṛtya ityādi pūrva kṛtam ca kiñcid anyat ca apūrvam buddhi stham samyak ānīya pramāṇānām samuccayaḥ samuccitiḥ kariṣyate atra ca sarve eva pramāṇa prameya tad ābhāsa ādi nimittāḥ sandarbhāḥ pramāṇa prasaṅgena āyāta tvāt pramāṇa śabdena uktāḥ 
[I,20,iv]	para pramāṇa pratiṣedha dhāya ityādinā pramāṇa siddhi śabdasya artham ācaṣṭe sva pramāṇam ca atra mukhyam para pramāṇam tu pareṣām tatra pramāṇa abhiniveśaḥ iti pramāṇam iti uktam tayoḥ yathāsvam svarūpa parijñānam pramāṇa siddhiḥ tatra para pramāṇasya apramāṇasya sataḥ api āropita pramāṇa svabhāvasya na etat pramāṇa svabhāvam iti yat utpādanam sa pratiṣedhaḥ sā eva ca tasya siddhiḥ sva pramāṇam eva guṇaḥ artha kāmaiḥ guṇyate iti kṛtvā arthau āhakatāt ca tasya udbhāvanam aviparīta lakṣaṇa abhidhānena vyutpādanam sā eva ca tasya siddhiḥ 
[I,21,i_I,21,ii]	yasmāt ityādinā puruṣa artha upayogi tvam pramāṇasya darśayati anyathā tad anupayoginaḥ vyutpādanam vyartha upayogi tvam pramāṇasya darśayati anyathā tad anupayoginaḥ vyutpādanam vyartham iti akartavyam eva syāt prameye punar atra heyam upādeyam ca tad pratipattiḥ yatas pramāṇa āyattā tasmāt pramāṇa siddhaye yatnaḥ saphalaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ atra kecid āhuḥ svatas eva siddhāni pramāṇāni iti tad mata anusāriṇaḥ ca apare ślokam paṭhanti prasiddhāni pramāṇāni vyavahāraḥ ca tad kṛtaḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇasya uktau jñāyate na prayojanam iti 
[I,21,iii]	atas tat nirākaraṇāya āha bahavaḥ ca atra vipratipannāḥ iti bahavaḥ ca atra vipratipannāḥ iti caśabdena yasmāt iti etat anukṛṣyate viruddham pratipannāḥ vipratipannāḥ paraspara viruddha lakṣaṇa praṇayanāt yadi hi pramāṇam idam iti niścaya lakṣaṇā siddhiḥ svatas pramāṇasya syāt na paraspara virodha lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇa kāraiḥ praṇīyet pramāṇa utpattau eva pramāṇa svarūpa siddheḥ eka ākāram eva lakṣaṇa praṇayanam syāt vyavahartāraḥ api vipratipannāḥ viparītam pratipannāḥ apramāṇam pramāṇa tvena adhyavasitāḥ iti arthaḥ tathā hi pramāṇa ābhāsena pravṛttāḥ kecid vipralabhyamānāḥ dṛśyante yadi tu siddhāni eva sarveṣām pramāṇāni syuḥ na kaścid vipralabhyet 
[I,22,i]	tasmāt svatas pramāṇasya sava saṃvedanāt svarūpa siddhi mātram bhavati īpsita artha kriyā samartha vastu prāpaṇa sāmarthya lakṣaṇam tu yat prāmāṇya tasya sataḥ eva pramāṇa paridṛṣṭa vastu sādhya artha kriyā viṣaya pramāṇa antara vṛttyā viścayaḥ bhavati prathamam utttara kālam tu punar punar uttara pramāṇa vṛttyā kāsāñcid jñāna vyaktīnām prāmāṇyam niścinvan abhyāsāt anyāsām uttara pramāṇa vṛttim antareṇa api prājñaḥ tathāvidhānām svarūpa saṃvedana mātrāt eva prāmāṇyam vyavasyati abhyāsena maṇyādīnām iva akṛtrima ādi bhedam tat evam yatas bahavaḥ pramāṇam prati vipratipannāḥ tasmāt teṣām vipratipatti nirāsāya śāstram iti 
[I,22,ii_I,22,iv]	tatra phala tva rūpa viṣaya saṅkhyā vipratipatti pattayaḥ catastraḥ tāsām saṅkhyā vipratipattim nirākartum āha pratyakṣam anumānam ca ityādi pramāṇa vyutpādane kartavye saṅkhī ā ādi vyutpattiḥ apārthikā iti ced na pramāṇa apramāṇa vipratipatti nivartana paratvāt prakaraṇasya tatra yadi saṅkhī ā ādi pratipattiḥ na nirākriyeta kevalam pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ svarūpam vyutpādyeta tadā pareṣām evam syāt nūnam etat viṣaya eva asmākam vipratipattiḥ yāni tu pramāṇa antarāṇi asmābhiḥ abhyupetāni na tat viṣaya iti nanu ca teṣām api doṣa udbhāvanāt kutas iyam āśaṅkhā evam tarhi yathā pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ asmat abhimatāt svarūpāt anyat eva svarūpam tathā teṣām api astitve tat anena na vyutpāditam iti āśaṅkā syāt atas saṅkhyā vyutpattiḥ 
[I,23,i_I,23,iii]	gocara avyutpādane tu aviṣaye gṛhītam pramāṇam yadā bhavati tadā tatra tasya visaṃvāde tadvat sva viṣaye api aprāmāṇyam avagacchet pratipattā iti viṣaya vyutpattiḥ pramāṇāt phalam avyatiriktam iti yadā na vyutpādyate tadā pramāṇasya pramāṇa svarūpa tā eva hīyate tathā hi phalasya tāvat artha adhigama rūpa tvam niyamataḥ abhyupeyam anyathā phala tva ayogāt tasmāt adhigama rūpa tvam phalam tatas jñāna rūpāt vyatiriktam yadā pramāṇam tadā tena ajñāna rūpeṇa bhāvyam ajñāna rūpasya ca pramāṇa svarūpa tā na syāt rūpa ādi vat iti phala vyupattiḥ tat na apārthikā saṅkhī ā ādi vyutpattiḥ dvayoḥ api sva viṣaye tulya bala tā khyāpanāya samuccaya vacanaḥ caśabdaḥ 
[I,23,iv]	kaḥ punar asya vākyasya arthaḥ kim pratyakṣa anumānam ca pramāṇe iti anena pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ dvi tvam pratipādyate pratyakṣam anumānam ca ete pramāṇe eva na pramāṇam pramāṇāni ca iti atha prāmāṇyam pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ pratipādyate pratyakṣam anumānam ca pramāṇe eva na apramāṇe iti kim ca atas yadi pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ niṣphalam vacanam tayoḥ dvi tvasya siddha tvāt na hi pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ dvi tvam prati kasyacid vipratipattiḥ atha dvitīyaḥ saṅkhyā avadhāraṇam na kṛtam syāt tatas ca dvividham eva pramāṇam iti yat pratipipādayiṣitam tat eva na pratipāditam syāt siddha sādhya tā ca tayoḥ prāmāṇyasya siddha tvāt atha vā cārvākam prati etat ucyate tathā api pratyakṣa apekṣayā siddha sādhanam eva 
[I,24,i]	na eṣa doṣaḥ atra hi dve vākye pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti eka vākyam pramāṇe iti dvitīyam evam ca vyākhyeyam pramāṇe eva na pramāṇāni pramāṇam ca iti arthaḥ atas eva vṛttau avadhārayati dve eva iti vyavaccheda phala tvāt vākyasya vinā api eva śabdam tad arthaḥ upalabhyate evam anena vākyena dve eva pramāṇe iti pratipāditam ke punar te dve iti saṃśayitasya paśna avasaraḥ idam ucyate pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti pratyakṣa anumāne eva te dve pramāṇe na tu anye eva kecid dve iti atra vyākhyāne na bhavati yathā ukta doṣa avakāśaḥ 
[I,24,ii]	atha katham gamyate na ekatvam pramāṇasya baha autvam vā iti eka tvam tāvat na bhavati anumānasya api prāmāṇyāt anyathā idam pramāṇam idam apramāṇam iti eṣā vyavasthā na syāt tathā hi kāsāñcid jñāna vyaktīnām pravṛttau saṃvādam visaṃvādam ca upalabhya tad jātīyatayāni asya api jñānasya saṃvāt etarau niścinvan pramāṇa itara vyavasthām kuryāt na anyathā tat ca yathā dṛṣṭa sādharmyāt tathā paricchidyamānam na anumeya tām atipatati kim ca anumānasya aprāmāṇye śāstra praṇayanam na syāt para avabodha artham hi śāstram kriyate sa ca para avabodhaḥ na anumānāt anyatas avasīyate pratyakṣasya śarīra mātra viṣaya tvāt 
[I,25,i_I,25,ii]	na ca śarīram eva buddhiḥ tad siddhau api buddhi vikalpe saṃśayāt na enam anya sambandhinam puruṣa mātra pratyakṣam anveti pratiṣedham ca ayam anumāna apavādīkurvan para loka ardena pratyakṣeṇa kartum arhati tasya bhāva viṣaya tvāt tat punar artha sāmarthya apekṣaṇāt anapekṣāyām vyavadhāna ādi bhāve api bhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti atas anumānasya api prāmāṇyam abhyupeyam tasmāt na ekatvam pramāṇasya 
[I,25,iii_I,26,i]	bahu tvam tu syāt tat ca viṣaya bahu tvāt vā ekasmin api viṣaye aneka pramāṇa avatārāt vā na tāvat viṣaya bahu tvāt atra kāraṇam āha yasmāt lakṣaṇa dvayam prameyam iti etat vivṛṇoti na hi ityādinā tatra sva lakṣaṇam yat artha kriyā sama stham tat eva vastu sāmānya lakṣaṇam punar tad viparītam yadi evam taimirika ādi upalabdhāḥ keśa ādayaḥ na sva lakṣaṇam keśa ādi sādhya artha kriyāyām artha tvāt na api sāmānya lakṣaṇam spaṣṭa pratibhāsi tvāt iti teṣām prameya antara tvam syāt 
[I,26,ii]	na eṣa doṣaḥ yatra hi vyavahartṛṇām viṣaya tva adhyavasāyaḥ tatra iyam cintā na ca taimirika ādibhiḥ upalabdhāḥ keśa ādayaḥ taiḥ sva jñāna pratibhāsinaḥ viṣaya tvena adhimucyante abhāvaḥ tarhi sāmānyam mā bhūt na hi tad viṣaya tvena adhyavasīyate iti ced na jñeya tvena adhyavasāyāt asti tatra api viṣaya adhimokṣaḥ yadā punar abhāvav ataimirika ādi dṛṣṭānām keśa ādīnām jñāna antareṇa jñeya tvena grahaṇam tat eṣṭam eva sāmānya rūpa tvam kevalam yasmin jñāne te pratibhāsante tasya jñeya tvena te na gṛhyante iti teṣām asāmānya rūpa tvam ucyate 
[I,26,iii_I,27,i]	yadi te na vastu katham sphuṭam pratibhāsante jñāna rūpa tayā sva lakṣaṇa tvāt yadā tu prati avamarśa jñānena viṣayīkriyante keśa ādi vat keśa ādi idam iti tadā sāmānya ākāreṇa asphuṭena prati avabhāsamānānām sāmānya rūpa tvam vyavasthāpyate yadi teṣām jñāna rūpa tvāt vastu tvam sāmānye api prasaṅgaḥ tathā tat api sva lakṣaṇam iṣṭam iti adoṣaḥ sāmānya rūpa tvam tu tasya viṣaya apekṣayā vyavasthāpyate artha antara vyāvṛtta padārtha samāśrayeṇa utpadyamānā prati avamarśa buddhiḥ abhinna ākārā teṣu abhinnam eva ākārām darśayati iti sa buddhi gataḥ ākāraḥ arthānām vyavasthāpyate avastu tvam api asyāt eva bāhya rūpeṇa adhyavasitasya atad rūpa tvāt 
[I,27,ii]	yadi tarhi sāmānyam sarva sāmarthya rahitam tad māna arham eva na bhavati iti aprameyam eva tat katham ācāryeṇa viṣaya dvaividhyam uktam tat tasya eva svarūpa para rūpābhyām adhigateḥ tasya eva hi vastunaḥ pratyakṣeṇa svarūpa adhigamāt ekam prameyam sva lakṣaṇam tasya eva anumānena sāmānya ākāra anurakta grāhya aṃśa ātmakena para rūpeṇa adhyavasita tad bhāva tayā adhigamāt dvitīyam sāmānya lakṣaṇam 
[I,27,iii^1]	katham punar etat gamyate para rūpeṇa sva lakṣaṇam eva adhigamyate iti yasmāt anumāna vikalpasya bāhya tayā prati avabhāsamānam aṃśamasva lakṣaṇam api sva lakṣaṇa tvena adhyavasāya puruṣaḥ artha kriyā arthī sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva pravartate anyathā yadi sāmānyam anumānena paricchinnam syāt artha kriyā arthī tatra eva pravartate na hi ghaṭam paricchidya ghaṭam paricchidya ghaṭau asāye avasthitaḥ tad artha kriyā arthī ghaṭe pravartate na eva vā pravartate 
[I,27,iii^2]	sāmānyasya kvacid anupayogāt pravartate ca sva lakṣaṇe tad sādhya artha kriyā prāptaye anumānāt tena adhyavasita tad bhāvaḥ iti gamyate pratyakṣeṇa api para rūpeṇa eva adhigatiḥ ayam tu viśeṣaḥ anumānena sādhāraṇa bhūtena para rūpeṇa arthasya grahaṇam pratyakṣeṇa tu asādhāraṇa bhūtena iti tasmāt sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa bhūtābhyām para rūpābhyām adhigateḥ prameya dvayam uktam na hi vijñāna vat arthasya svatas saṃvittiḥ yat eva tu artha ākārasya jñānasya sva saṃvedanam sā eva artha saṃvittiḥ artha pratibhāse hi jñāne anubhūte adhigataḥ iti manyate atas eva bāhye api arthe prameye sva saṃvittim phalatvena vyavasthāpayiṣyati iti apare 
[I,28,i_I,28,ii]	gatam etat idam tu vaktavyam katham prameya dvi tvāt pramāṇa dvi tvam iti āha sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam ca ityādi caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam pratyakṣam eva sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam eva na pramāṇa antaram ayam ca arthaḥ vistareṇa sva lakṣaṇam anirdeśyam grāhya bhedāt ityādinā pratipādayiṣyamāṇaḥ iti darśayan āha pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ iti atha vā anena prameya dvaya darśanena ekatri ādi pramāṇa nirāsaḥ kṛṭaḥ sva lakṣaṇāt anyat api prameyam darśayatā pratyakṣam api pramāṇam asti iti eka pramāṇa nirāsaḥ kṛtaḥ tṛtīyasya prameyasya abhāvam darśayatā tri ādi pramāṇa nirāsaḥ 
[I,29,i]	yat tarhi ityādi yadi prameya niyamaḥ sva sāmānya laṣaṇābhyām anyat prameyam na asti eva iti abhyupeyate evam tarhi nīla ādīnām kṛtaka tva ādi liṅga darśanāt anityam rūpam iti evamādi grahaṇam na syāt tathā hi nīla ādi sva lakṣaṇam anitya tā sāmānyam anayoḥ saṅkareṅa grahaṅāt na tad sāmānyam eva sva lakṣaṇam eva vā atas viśeṣa sāmānya rūpam prameya antaram eva etat na pramīyate pramīyate ca tasmāt anityam rūpam ityādi viśeṣa sāmānya viṣayam grahaṇam pramāṇa antaram tathā hi na tat pratyakṣam sāmānyasya api grahaṇāt na api anunmānam viśeṣasya api grahaṇāt vinā api liṅgena tathā apratīteḥ sambhavāt ca tat katham iti tad grahaṇam katham na pramāṇa antaram iti arthaḥ 
[I,29,ii]	asakṛt vā iti anena api viśeṣa dṛṣṭa ākhyam yat anumānam tat pramāṇa antaram iti darśayati tat yathā pratyakṣeṇa ekadā paricchinne vahnau dhūme ca punar paryāyeṇa tena eva dhūmena yadā saḥ eva ayam vahniḥ iti paricchinatti tadā tad viśeṣa dṛṣṭa ākhyam agri grahaṇam pramāṇa antaram sāmānyatas dṛṣṭāt anumānāt tat eva ca atra anumānam iṣṭam tad lakṣaṇam ca viśeṣa dṛṣṭe na sambhavati viśeṣeṇa liṅgasya sambandha ayogāt tat evam dvābhyām ākārābhyām pramāṇa bahu tvam sambhavet prameya bahu tvāt vā ekasmin eva vā viṣaye aneka pramāṇa avatārāt tat ubhayathā api pareṇa darśitam yat tarhi ityādinā granthena 
[I,30,i_I,30,ii]	eka aneka pramāṇa nirāsaḥ vā prameya dvaya darśana āt yaḥ prāk uktaḥ sa na asti iti pratipāditam na tāvat eka saṅkhyā nirāsaḥ viṣaya aniyamāt yadā na sāmānya viṣayam eva anumānam kim tarhi pramāṇa antara viṣaye api pravartate tadā pratyakṣasya api sāmānye pravṛtti avirodhāt na apratyakṣa viṣaye pratyāyanāya anumānam kalpayitavyam iti ekam eva pramāṇam syāt na api tri ādi saṅkhyā nirāsaḥ prameya antara sambhavāt prameya dvi tvena hi pramāṇa dvi tvam uktam yadā tu prameya antaram sambhavati tadā tasya pratyāyakam pramāṇa antaram syāt iti na dve eva pramāṇe asti etat grahaṇam iti na idam apahnūyate kim tu tasya saṃdhāne na pramāṇa antaram 
[I,31,i]	ayam tāvat pūrvasya parihāraḥ tasya iti anitya ādeḥ varṇa ādeḥ ca sandhānam yojanam yat tat sandhāne pravartate tat nimittam jñānam na tad pramāṇa antaram katham punar tad sandhānam iti āha sva sāmānya lakṣaṇābhyām ityādi prāk tau adrūpa ādikam avyapadeḥ yena sva lakṣaṇena gṛhṇāti pratyakṣeṇa paścāt tat eva varṇa tva ādinā sāmānya lakṣaṇena sa vikalpena manaḥ vijñānena tatas sāmānya lakṣaṇam ca anitya tva ādi yat kiñcid kṛtakam tat sarvam anityam iti evam gṛhītvā tatas kṛtakam ca idam varṇa ādi tasmāt anityam iti evam manasā sandhatte yojayati varṇa tva ādi sāmānyam sāmānyena eva anitya tvena tasmāt na pramāṇa antaram api tu anumānam eva kim kāraṇam viśeṣeṇa na yojayati tasya tena agrahaṇāt 
[I,31,ii]	syāt etat yadi varṇa sāmānyena anitya tva ādīn yojayati evam sati sāmānyasya eva avastunaḥ anitya tva ādayaḥ dharmoḥ prāpnuvanti na sva lakṣaṇasya tatra āvṛttteḥ ye hi vastuni na vartate na te vastu dharmāḥ tat yathā anutpāda ādaya tatra āvṛtteḥ ye hi vastuni na vartate na te vastu dharmāḥ tat yathā anutpāda ādayaḥ iti na ayam doṣaḥ vastunaḥ eva anitya ādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ tathā asādhanāt yadi api vikalpa pratibhāsinaḥ sāmānyasya eva tathā vastu adhyavasāyena grahaḥ tathā api tasya vastunaḥ kṣaṇika tva ādayaḥ vidyamānāḥ eva ākārāḥ anumāna vikalpe pratibhāsante sa hi yathā sthita vastu pratyāya kaliṅga āśrayeṇa utpannaḥ vastunaḥ sataḥ eva ākārān adhyavasyati atas varṇa sāmānye anitya tā ādi sādhane api tatra tad ākāra siddhyā vastunaḥ eva saḥ ākāraḥ sidhyati iti avagantavyam sāmagrī viśeṣa janmanaḥ mukha pratibimba jñānasya viṣaye lakṣmī ādi siddhyā mukha lakṣmyādi siddhi vat arthaḥ 
[I,32,i_I,32,ii]	sa tu ayam anumāna vikalpaḥ yadi api sambhavinaḥ eva ākārān arthasya adhyavasyati tathā api sva lakṣaṇasya rūpam agṛhītam eva tena anyathā darśana vat spaṣṭam pratibhāseta tatra vastunaḥ rūpam na ca paraspara vilakṣaṇau ākārau ekasya vastunaḥ staḥ yena aspaṣṭam gṛhyeta na itareṇa tasmāt viśeṣasya agrahaṇāt na sa tam anitya tayā yojayati api tu varṇa sāmānyam eva sva viṣayam atas na pramāṇa antaram evam idam anumānena varṇa ādeḥ anitya tā grahaṇam adhikṛtya uktam yadā tu antyakṣaṇa darśinaḥ naṣṭaḥ ayam iti tadā pratyakṣeṇa anitya tā svabhāva pratipatteḥ gṛhītam eva niścinoti iti etat pramāṇam eva na bhavati tadā ca asakṛt vāti anena asya sādhāraṇaḥ parihāraḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ aniṣṭhā sakteḥ iti ayam veditavyaḥ 
[I,33,i]	katham punar pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītam eva pūrvam paścāt niścaya jñānam gṛhṇāti yasmāt na anitya tā nāma anyā kācid calāt vastunaḥ tena antyam kṣaṇam sadṛśa apara apratisandhāyinam pratyakṣeṇa paricchin dan naśvara tām api tasya svabhāvam pratyeti iti sā eva ca anitya tā iti pratyakṣa siddhā sā atha punar anitya tā bhāvāt arthān taram tadā na svabhāvaḥ naśvaraḥ syāt na hi anyasya bhāve anyaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma tatas nāśita asvabhāva āpattiḥ bhāvasya iti ced ayuktam etat na hi svayam acala svabhāvasya anyena svabhāva antaram ādhātum śakyate prakṛtyā ca cala ātmake viphalā anyā anitya tā tattva anya tvābhyām avācya tve api avastu tvāt na sa svabhāvaḥ bhāvikaḥ iti saṃvṛtya anityaḥ syāt na paramārthataḥ tasmāt bhāvaḥ eva anitya tā tatas ca dharmiṇi rūpa ādau gṛhīte anityatā api gṛhītā eva iti gṛhīta grahaṇāt na idam pramāṇam 
[I,33,ii]	yadi na anyaḥ anitya tā ādikaḥ dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ nanu evam anumānam api na pramāṇam syāt tathā hi na asiddhe dharmiṇi dharmaḥ śakyaḥ sādhayitum tad siddhau ca tad ātmatayā dharmasya api siddha tvāt iti ced na aniścayāt sadṛśa apara utpattyā hi saḥ eva ayam iti bhrāntasya na tatra pratyakṣam niścayam janayati aniścayāt ca avyavahāra yogyaḥ agṛhīta kalpaḥ eva saḥ iti na tatra tasya prāmāṇyam api tu yatra ākāre niścayam ādadhat smṛti dvāreṇa pravartayati tatra eva kutas pravṛtti phala tvāt pramāṇasya tasmāt aniścit eṣu ākāreṣu niścayam utpādayat tatra pravartanāya anumānam pramāṇam iti asamānam 
[I,34,i_I,34,ii]	atha dvitīye kalpe na pramāṇa antaram iti katham granthe nīyate yāvatā pramāṇam eva idam na bhavati tatas na idam pramāṇam iti yuktam vaktum syāt satyam etat kim tu pareṇa pramāṇa antaram iti kṛtvā apanyastam atas tathā eva pratiṣiddham iti adoṣaḥ na ca punar punar abhijñānaḥ iti abhijñāne phale kartavye yat jñānam viśeṣa dṛṣṭam tat na pramāṇam iti arthaḥ yadi api jñāna abhijñānayoḥ vastutas na bhedaḥ tathā api pramāṇa phala vat bhedaḥ utprekṣyate abhijñeya artha ākāra utpattyā jñānam pūrva gṛhīta artha grahaṇāt abhijñānam iti caśabdena pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītasya eva punar anityam varṇa ādi iti yat grahaṇam tat api na pramāṇam iti darśayati punar punar iti anena asakṛt iti asya artham ācaṣṭe 
[I,34,iii]	nanu ca pūrva gṛhītasya arthasya sakṛt api grahaṇe na pramāṇam tat kim ucyate asakṛt iti parama topa pradarśana artha tvāt adoṣaḥ sāṅkhyena hi viśeṣa dṛṣṭa anumānasya lakṣaṇam uktam yadā tena eva dhūmena tasya eva agreḥ punar punar astitvam pratipadyate iti atas tat matam darśayitum evam uktam na punar sakṛt grahaṇāt pramāṇāt pramāṇam iti kṛtvā 
[I,35,i]	vivādāḥ padībhūtam vastu kāraṇam antareṇa na pratīyate iti atas pṛcchati kim kāraṇam iti ācāryaḥ tu adhigata viṣaya tvam apramāṇye kāraṇam upadarśayiṣyan āha aniṣṭhā sakteḥ iti sāṅkhyātaḥ lakṣaṇataḥ ca pramāṇām iyat tā paricchedaḥ niṣṭhā tad abhāvaḥ prasajyate iti arthaḥ anadhigata artha adhigantṛ pramāṇam iti sāmānyena pramāṇa lakṣaṇam saṅkhyā dve trīṇi vā iti evamādi tat na prāpnoti yadi sarvam jñānam pramāṇa tvena iṣyate iti anena prāk pakṣa virodham āha anavasthayā vyavasthāyāḥ nirākaraṇāt smṛta ādi vat iti dṛṣṭāntam āha dṛṣṭāntam āha viṣaye api evat nirdeśaḥ asti iti āha smṛtiḥ eva smṛtim iti bhāve kta vidhānāt tat yathā iti evamādinā hetoḥ sādhyena anugamam dṛṣṭānte darśayati tadvat iti pramāṇa phalam yat pūrva adhigata artha viṣayam na tat pramāṇam smṛti ādi vat tathā ca viśeṣa dṛṣṭam vyāpaka viruddhaḥ 
[I,35,ii]	syāt etat na sa yathādṛṣṭaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ tena gṛhyate kim tu tad sāmānyam iti na tarhi viśeṣa dṛṣṭam tad anumānam api tu pūrva dṛṣṭa sāmānyena uttarasya grahaṇāt sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam eva syāt etat na tatra agni sāmānya mātra grahaṇam kevalam pratiniyata deśa vartinaḥ grahaṇāt iti neyatā viśeṣa samāśrayeṇa samāna tā hīyate tathā hi aguru dhūma ādinā tat jananam vahnim pratipannam api agni sāmānyam eva pratyeti na tu pratiniyatam bhedam iti yat kiñcid etat 
[I,36,i]	syāt etat yatra bhinnau dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikau tatra tayoḥ sāmānyena anumānam sambhavati iha punar yaḥ eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ saḥ eva dārṣṭa antikaḥ saḥ eva ayam iti pradarśanāt atas na sāmānyena anumānam iti yadi yat eva sādhyam saḥ eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ evam tarhi tena gṛhīta avismṛtena bhavitavyam na hi anyathā dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavitum arhati tatas ca adhigata viṣaya tvāt saḥ eva doṣaḥ atha manyase na eva idam adhigata viṣayam yatas adhigatasya dharmiṇaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭa artha bhāvaḥ dharmaḥ anadhigataḥ anena adhigamyate iti ayuktam etat yadi tāvat pūrva apara kāla dṛṣṭau arthau bhinnau evam sati atasmin tad bhāva adhyāropaḥ viparyāsaḥ eva na pramāṇam atha abhinnau adhigata viṣayam yatas adhigatasya dharmiṇaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭa artha bhāvaḥ tasya anadhigataḥ adhigamyate iti uktam tat ayuktam uktam yatas na ayam kacit arthasya dharmaḥ yaḥ prāk na āsīt paścāt bhavati yadi syāt saḥ eva tayoḥ svabhāva bheda asrayaḥ iti nānā bhavaḥ syāt tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ 
[I,37,i_I,37,ii]	tasmāt tat eva idam iti niścayaḥ viśeṣa dṛṣṭa tvena abhimataḥ na smṛteḥ bhidyate idam hi smṛteḥ svarūpam yat uta abhra aṣṭa darśana saṃskārasya tat eva idam iti pūrva dṛṣṭa ākāra adhyavasāyaḥ taḥ asya api asti iti smṛtiḥ eva svabhāva vipratipatti nirākaraṇa ātāha pratyakṣam ityādi pratigatam akṣam pratyakṣam prādi samāsaḥ etat lakṣyam kalpanā apoḍham iti lakṣaṇam kalpanāyāḥ apoḍham apagatam kalpanayā vā apoḍham rahitam kalpanā apoḍham kalpanā apoḍha nirdeśāt ca jñāna ātmakam tat iti gamyate yatas jñānasya eva kalpanā saṃsargaḥ asti atas tad pratiṣedhena tat eva pratīyate tat yathā dhenuḥ ānīya tām avatsa iti vatsa pratiṣedhena godhenuḥ eva na anyā 
[I,37,iii]	atha kā iyam kalpanā nāma iti kalpanānām bahu tvāt kā atra kalpanā vivakṣitā iti saṃśayān asya paśnaḥ nāma jāti ādi yojana iti namnaḥ jāti ādibhiḥ atulya kakṣa tvāt ādi śabdena parigrahe api parikalpitāḥ hi jāti ādayaḥ na tattvataḥ santi nāma jāti ādīnām yojanā nāma jāti ādi yojanā kṛt yogā ca ṣaṣṭhī samasyate iti samāsaḥ sādhanam kṛtā iti vā kā punar asau nāma ādīni tadvata arthena yayā yojyante saṃsṛjyante sā pratītiḥ kalpanā na ca atra yojanam prati vyāpṛtā eva pratītiḥ kalpanā vivakṣitā kim tarhi yā api yojanam prati na vyāpṛtā tatra ca yogya pratibhāsā sā api yaḥ hi yatra yogyaḥ sa tat akurvāṇaḥ api tena vyapadeśam arhati pācaka vat pākena tena stana pāna ādiṣu bāla dāraka ādeḥ yat kalpanā jñānam tat nāma ādi saṃsarga abhāve api sa vikalpakam siddham bhavati 
[I,38,i]	yadṛcchā śabdeṣu ityādi anapekṣita jāti ādi pravṛtti nimittāḥ yadṛcchā śabdāḥ jñāna dharmaḥ hi kalpanā na śabda dharmaḥ tatas nāmnā viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ gṛhyate iti vaktavyaḥ abhilāpena kalpanāyāḥ tulya viṣaya tām darśayitum ucyate iti āha tat punar abhilāpa vat kalpanā jñānam api na sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam atas na tat pratyakṣa tvena abhimatam iti jñāpana artham ḍitthaḥ iti ḍittha śabda svarūpa ātmanā kila saḥ arthaḥ tat abhinna rūpa tayā pratīyate evam jāti ādibhiḥ tad abheda upacāra āpannāḥ te arthaḥ ucyante daṇḍī viṣaṇi iti saṃyogi samavāyi dravya bhedena udāharaṇa dvayam 
[I,38,ii]	atra iti kriyā dravya śabdeṣu kriyā dravyābhyām tadvatām yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa śabda pravṛtti nimittam tathā hi kāraka tvam daṇḍi tvam iti bhāva pratyayaḥ kriyā kāraka ādi sambandhe bhavati yathā uktam sama asakṛt tad hiteṣu sambandha abhidhānam iti śabda pravṛtti nimitte ca bhāva pratyayaḥ bhavati tathā ca āhuḥ yasya guṇasya hi bhāva adravye śabda niveśaḥ tad abhidhāne tu atalau iti pācakaḥ daṇḍī iti ca kṛttat dhitau tasmāt atra sambandhe bhāva pratyayaḥ 
[I,39,i]	anye tu artha śūnyaiḥ iti sva matam darśayati arthena jāti ādinā viśeṣaṇena rahitaiḥ iti arthaḥ yathā yadṛcchā śabdā jāti ādi viśeṣaṇa vṛtti nirapekṣāḥ eva saṅketa vaśāt sva artham abhidadhati tathā gavā ādi śabdāḥ api icchā mātra āyatta vṛttayaḥ hi śabdāḥ te puruṣaiḥ icchayā yatra yatra yathābhūte niyujyante tam tam artham tathābhūtam pratyāyayantaḥ kena cāryante jāti ādayaḥ tu asiddhāḥ iti kutas teṣām śabda pravṛtti nimitta bhāvaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[I,39,ii^1]	atha kasmāt ityādi anyatara abhāve abhāvāt dvaya adhīnā vṛttiḥ tat kasmāt dvaya adhīn ajanma jñānam aindriyam indriyeṇa eva ucyate na viṣayeṇa ālokaḥ tu na sarva indriya jñā nimittam cakṣuḥ vijñānasya api keṣāñcid na bhavati iti na upanyastaḥ manaskārasya tu loke viṣaya vat cakṣuḥ vat ca kāraṇa tvam na prasiddham iti anupanyāsaḥ kāraṇa antara upalakṣaṇa mātram vā viṣaya grahaṇam atra yathā kathañcid pratyakṣa śabdam vyutpādya saḥ avikalpe sarvatra samyak jñāne sañjñātvena paribhāṣyate iti ācāryam atam paraḥ tu atat jānānaḥ akṣa nimittaḥ ayam asañjñā śabdaḥ iti matvā pṛṣṭavān ācāryaḥ tu abhyupagamya parihāram āha asādhāraṇa hetu tvāt iti akṣāṇi hi sva santati patitasya api manaḥ vijñāsya indriya antara vijñānasya ca na āśrayībhavanti atas rūpi indriya vijñāna nirdeśaḥ taiḥ iva nyāyyaḥ 
[I,39,ii^2]	tat asādharaṇa hetu tvāt evam hi cakṣuḥ ādi vijñānam eva pratipādayitum śakyate na tu viṣayaiḥ nirdeśena tasya tatra āgamaka tvāt tat punar sādhāraṇa kāraṇa tvāt tathā hi viṣayāḥ manaḥ vijñānāni asantāna vijñāna sādhāraṇāḥ nava candra ādi prekṣā svan eka santāna cakṣuḥ ādi vijñāna kāraṇa tvāt tad pṛṣṭha labdha manaḥ vijñā kāraṇa tvāt ca aya atra abhiprāyaḥ lokena hi asya śabdasya asmin abhidheye pratyāyana sāmarthyam asti iti gamaka tvam abhisamīkṣya śabdaḥ prayujyate tat ca gamaka tvam indriya vijñāne akṣa vyapadeśasya asti na viṣaya vyapadeśasya gamaka tvena ca śabda niyoga arha tā vyāptā atas tad gamaka tvam viṣaya vyapadeśāt nivartamānam tat niyoga arha tām api nivartayati atas na viṣayaiḥ vyapadiśyate iti 
[I,40,i]	nanu ca icchādhīn avṛttayaḥ śabdāḥ sarva artha pratyāyana yogyāḥ iti uktam satyam sā eva tu icchā lokaḥ yāsa ādhāraṇena vyapadeśe asti na sādhāraṇena tathā hi lokaḥ asādhāraṇena eva vyapadiśati yat darśayati asādhāraṇena ca vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ityādi vyavahāra tā ca loke tad vyavasthā atra vidheyā tasya pratyāyana tvāt iti manyate 
[I,40,ii]	upapannam etat iti yuktam yasmāt pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati kim atra anyayā yuktyā iti abhiprāyaḥ pratyātma vedyaḥ hi sva saṃvedanena jñāna antareṇa vā sarveṣām abhilāpa saṃsarga yogyaḥ vikalpaḥ asaṃsṛṣṭa vikalpam ca pratyakṣam vikalpa rahitam eva ātmānam paricchindat utpadyate tathā hi sarva viṣayebhyaḥ vikalpān apanīya pratyastam ita aśeṣa vikalpena manasā sthitaḥ api cakṣuḥ vijñānena rūpam īkṣate prāṇī tat ca kalpanā rahitam pratyakṣam eva santi eva indriya dhiyaḥ kalapanāḥ kim tu tāḥ na upalakṣyante iti ced vārttam etat tathā hi avikalpa avasthāyāḥ ūrdhvam kiñcid vikalpayan sa citta dhārām saṅkalati evam ca evam ca kalpanā mama āsīt iti tat iyam kalpanā upalakṣya svarūpā eva tat yadi indriya vijñāne syāt prāk api upalakṣyeta na ca saṃhṛta vikalpau asthāyām upalakṣyate tena sā tatra na asti iti gamyate 
[I,41,i]	syāt etat yat etat vyāpṛta indriyasya jñānam manaḥ vijñāna tvena vaḥ abhimatam āviṣṭa abhilāpam ahiḥ ahiḥ iti dhārāvāhi yojakam ca abhidhāna abhidheyayoḥ darśakam ca arthasya tad vikalpakam api avikalpa jñā vat yakṣam eva iṣṭavyam anyathā vicchinnam darśanam syāt vikalpaḥ ca vikalpena ādarśānāt darśanena vā avikalpanāt tayoḥ asaha vṛtteḥ ca asti ca avicchinnam darśanam tasmāt indriya jam eva idam sa vikalpam iti vikalpaka pratyakṣa vādinaḥ api tarhi gavā ādau san nihite viṣaye tatra ca pratyakṣa pravṛtte artha antara nāma anusmṛta vikalpa antara sammukhībhāve ca sati pratyupasthita viṣaya grāhi vikalpakam jñānam pratyakṣa tvena abhimatam katham na vyavahitam vyavadhāne vā katham avicchinnam darśanam bhavati iti tulyam codyam 
[I,42,i]	syāt etat vijātīya vikalpa kāle na asti darśanam tathā api tat na eva vicchinnam avasīyate laghutara vṛttinā darśana antara udayena tat śūnye kāle pratisandhīyamāna tvāt alāta vat alātam hi pūrva pūrva deśam hitvā antara antara deśa varti na sakala cakra ābhāsām deśam vyāpnoti iti tatra viniyata deśa pratibhāsi eva vijñānam syāt na sarva diś anu gata pratibhāsam atha ca cakra ābhāsam darśanam bhavati atas pratisandhānāt cakram paśyāmi iti matiḥ yathā tathā iha api iti tat etat nirvikalpa pratyakṣa vādinaḥ api tulyam yat uktam laghutara vṛttinā ityādi tat krama bhāvinoḥ api darśana vikalpayoḥ avicchinna darśana adhyavasāya sādhanāya paryāptam eva nirvikalpa pratyakṣa vādinaḥ api atha vā sa vikalpam avikalpam ca yuga pad ve vijñāne vartete tayoḥ svabhāva bhedam anavadhārayan pratipattā mohāt aikyam adhyavasyati tasmāt manaḥ vijñānam eva etat sa vikalpakam indriya jñānam tu tena sahabhāvi krama bhāvi vā nirvikalpakam eva iti sthitam etat 
[I,43,i]	pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati iti atra kaścid āha yadi pratyakṣa śabdena pratyakṣam abhidhīyate katham tad kalpanā apoḍham anuktam gamyate katham iti tat etat kalpanā svarūpa saṃvarṇanena eva nirastam na hi abhidheya tā kalpanā yatas abhidhīyamānasya kalpanā apoḍha tā nivarteta kim tarhi pratīti viśeṣaḥ iti uktam 
[I,43,ii]	na kevalam pratyakṣeṇa eva kalpanā apoḍha tvam siddham api tu āgamena api iti darśayan āha abhidharme api ityādi samaṅganam samaṅgaḥ saṅgatiḥ iti arthaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānena samaṅgaḥ saḥ asya asti iti cakṣuḥ vijñāna samaṅgī cakṣuḥ vijñānena saṅgataḥ iti yāvat nīlam vijānāti iti nīlam artha svarūpeṇa jānāti no tu nīlam iti na tat nāmataḥ nīlam etat iti jānāti etat eva uttareṇa pada dvayena spaṣṭayati na tu arthe dharma sañjñī iti na arthe nāma sañjñi iti arthaḥ 
[I,43,iii]	katham tarhi ityādi sañcita ālambanāḥ pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ iti yaḥ ayam siddhāntaḥ sa katham yujyate yadi tat ekatas eka tvena ālambanam na vikalpayanti evam manyate sañcita śabdena samudāyaḥ ucyate bhāve niṣṭha vidhānāt sañcitam sañcayaḥ samudāyaḥ iti hi paryāyāḥ sa ca sañcayaḥ na ekasya eva paramāṇoḥ api tu bahūnām sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ tatra sāmānye yadi akṣadhīḥ pravarteta tadā asau vikalpikā syāt sāmānya buddhiḥ hi niyatam vikalpena anubadhyate na hi sāmānyam vastu satsiddhāntaḥ iṣyate tasmāt sā eva tat vikalpayati iti kṛtvā yat ca ityādi āyatana sva lakṣaṇam cakṣuḥ vijñāna grāhya tva ādi tat pratyete sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ na dravya sva lakṣaṇam iti dravyam nīla ādi bhedāḥ nīla ādi dravya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tva pratiṣedhena sāmarthyāt teṣām yat sāmānyam abhinnam sa viṣayaḥ iti uktam bhavati atas ca kalpanā apoḍha tvam nirudhyate tat katham tat śāstram anyathā netum śakyate iti bhāvaḥ 
[I,44,i]	tasya ubhayasya api eka parihāram āha tatra aneka artha janya tvāt ityādi tatra iti śāstre aneka artha janya tvāt iti aneka paramāṇu janya tvāt iti arthaḥ sva hetu pratyayebhyaḥ ye paramāṇavaḥ jāyante te anyonya sannidhāna avasthā prāptāḥ eva santaḥ pratyekam vijñāna upajanana samarthāḥ sañcita śabdena uktāḥ san jātam citam caya paryāyam eṣā iti sañcitāḥ prādibhyaḥ dhātu jasya vā iti bahuvrīhiḥ uttara pada lopaḥ ca praparṇaḥ iti yathā na eva vā atra kta pratyayaḥ bhāve vihitaḥ kim tarhi karmaṇi eva paraspara upasarpaṇa pratyayaiḥ hi te sañcitāḥ saṃhīkṛtāḥ taiḥ tathāvidhaiḥ anekaiḥ sva pratibhāsāḥ janyante iti sañcita ālambanāḥ iti uktāḥ sarvān tān sañcita ākhyāna viśeṣeṇa ālambante na ekam eva dravyam iti kṛtvā 
[I,45,i^1]	yat ca uktam āyatana sva lakṣaṇam pratyetaḥ ityādi atra api taiḥ eva yathā uktaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ sahitena eva cakṣuḥ ādi vijñānam janyate na svakena eva tasmāt aneka artha janya tvāt sva arthe sāmānya gocaram iti uktam sāmānyam gocaraḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ nanu ca sāmānyam abhinna kalpitam indriya jñānasya ca viṣayaḥ paramāṇu ākhyam anekam vastu tat katham sāmānya gocara tvam upapadyate na eṣa doṣaḥ yat tat sañcita śabdena āyatana sva lakṣaṇa śabdena ca uktam anekam paramāṇuvaḥ tu tat eva pratiniyata vijñāna janana sāmarthyena sādharmyeṇa paraspara apekṣayā samānam samānam eva sāmānyam 
[I,45,i^2]	sva arthe tad hita vidhānāt cātuḥ varṇya vat tat etat uktam bhavati sañcita gocaram āyatana sva lakṣaṇa gocaram ca uktam iti na tu bhinneṣu abheda kalpanāt iti sāmānya viṣayam uktam iti anena sambandhaḥ na tu bhinneṣu abheda kalpanayā sañcita viṣayam āyatana sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam ca uktam iti arthaḥ na dravya sva lakṣaṇam iti anena api eka paramāṇu dravya niyama nirākaraṇam śāstram kṛtam draṣṭavyam na sāmarthya ākṣiptam sāmānya viṣaya tvam iti aviruddham 
[I,46,i]	ye tu eka indriya vijñāna kārya tvena eka rūpa āyatana ādi saṅgrahe api na anekam dravyam yugapad gṛhyate api tu krameṇa eva iti āhuḥ te idam vaktavyāḥ yadi yugapad bahūnām dravyāṇām grahaṇam na asti katham tarhi tilam āṣādīnām vicchinna deśa avasthitānām sakṛt grahaṇam iti na hi taiḥ asaṃyukta tvāt vijātīya tvāt ca dravya antam ekam ārabdham yasya grahaṇam syāt darśanasya laghu vṛtti tvāt bhrāntyā kramavatī api tatra akrama adhyavasāyaḥ iti ced krama pātiṣu api tarhi teṣu lāghau asya tulya tvāt sakṛt eva gṛhṇāmi iti adhyavasāyaḥ syāt kim ca repha sakāra ādiṣu varṇeṣu laghu vṛtti tvāt darśanasya ākrama grahaṇa adhyavasāyaḥ syāt tatas ca krama bhedāt śruti bhedaḥ na syāt rasaḥ saraḥ iti evamādiṣu śabdeṣu āśu bhramaṇa udaka bindu pāta ādiṣu ca darśanasya lāghavāt krameṇa gṛhṇāmi iti bhāve grahaṇa adhyavasāyaḥ na syāt tasmāt yāvat gocarībhūtam tat sarvam yugapad eva pratīyate iti 
[I,46,ii]	āhuḥ ca iti viṣaya vipratipattim nirākurvan tat eva nirvikalpa tvam samarthayate dharmiṇaḥ aneka rūpasya iti artha antara vyāvṛtti samāśrayeṇa kalpitāḥ ye dharma bhedāḥ sāmānya rūpāḥ jñeya tva ādayaḥ tad apekṣayān eka rūpasya iti uktam na punar aṃśavān asau viṣayā na itarasya iti darśayan āha na indriyāt sarvathā gatiḥ iti indriyāt iti hetau pañcamī lya blope vā indriyāt dhetoḥ indriyam vā prāpya sarveṇa prakāreṇa sva sāmānya lakṣaṇābhyām grahaṇam na bhavati iti arthaḥ 
[I,47,i]	tasya tarhi kīdṛśam ālambanam iti āha sva saṃvedyam ityādi sva saṃvedyam anāgamikam anirdeśyam anākhyeyam atha vā sva saṃvedyam iti ukte kim svabhāvam tat iti vaktavyam iti āha anirdeśyam iti anirdeśya tvam tu tasya jñānayaḥ rūpa bhedāt iti manyate tathā hi yat ca śābdam jñānam yat ca aindriyam anayoḥ bhinnaḥ pratibhāsaḥ spaṣṭāspaṣṭtvāt na hi yathā vyāpṛta indriyasya artha rūpam indriya jñāne sphuṭena ākāreṇa pratibhāsate tathā śābde yadi punar indriya gocaraḥ eva nirdeśyaḥ syāt śābde api tathā eva pratibhāseta na ca evam 
[I,48,i]	na ca yaḥ śābde na pratibhāsate sa śabda arthaḥ tasmāt bhinna rūpa jñāna grāhya tvāt na indriya viṣayaḥ sita tvāt nirdeśyaḥ iti yadi etaḥ bhinna rūpa jñāna grāhyam na tat tat eva tat yathā aśvāt bhinna jñāna grāhyaḥ mahiṣaḥ indriya viṣayāt bhinna rūpa jñāna grāhyaḥ ca śabda viṣayaḥ sita tva ādiḥ vyāpaka viruddhaḥ 
[I,48,ii]	syāt etat aindriyasya jñānasya cakṣuḥ ādiḥ āśrayaḥ śābdasya tu manaḥ tasmāt āśraya bhedāt eka viṣaya tve api tayoḥ pratibhāsa bhedaḥ iti yadi evam katham idānīm cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādīni bhinna arthāni iti vaḥ niścayaḥ tatra api hi śakyate vaktum ekaḥ eva teṣām viṣayaḥ pratibhāsa bhedaḥ tu āśraya bhedāt iti kasyacid artha ākārasya anukārāt śābdasya eva eka viṣaya tvam na cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādīnām na hi tāni parasparam arthasya kañcana ākāram anukurvanti iti ced na tatra api jñeya tva ādi anukāri tvam asti eva 
[I,48,iii]	yāpīyam kalpanā yadi śābda indriya jñānayoḥ na ekaḥ viṣayaḥ yaḥ sa astra ādimān sa gauḥ iti upadeśāt gām pratipadya paścāt vyakti viśeṣam paśyan katham evam avasyati yaḥ asau mayā śrutaḥ ayam asau iti katham ca gāmānaya iti uktaḥ indriya viṣayaḥ eva pravartate na hi anyam upalabdhavataḥ anyatra saḥ eva ayam iti pratyayaḥ bhavati na api anyatra codite anyatra pravṛttiḥ yuktā bhavati ca tathā pratyayaḥ pravartate ca śabdāt indriya viṣaye tasmāt ekaḥ tayoḥ viṣayaḥ iti sā api akalpanā eva tattva vicāra vyāpṛtāḥ hi vyākhyātāraḥ khalu evam viṣaya vivekam kurvanti na vyavahartāraḥ te tu tattva adhyavasāyena dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya vyavakaranti iti alam atiprasaṅgena evam sva saṃvedyam anirdeśyam rūpam pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ na ca evaṃvidhe kalpanā pravartate tasyāḥ śābdena eka viṣaya tvāt iti viṣaya nirdeśena api pratyakṣasya avikalpa tā samarthitā bhavati 
[I,49,i_I,49,ii]	katham tarhi idānīm aniścaya ātmanaḥ pratyakṣāt vyavahāraḥ niścinvan hi idan tayā sukha duḥkha sādhanayoḥ prāpti parihārāya pravartate na eṣa doṣaḥ artha ālocana mātre api hi pratyakṣe anubhava ahita sāmarthya bhāvi smaraṇa pūrvakābhyām abhilāṣa itarābhyām vyavahāraḥ bhavati vastu dharmaḥ hi eṣa yat anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smṛti bījam ādhatte yādṛśam ca sukha sādhanam duḥkha sādhanam vā anubhūtam tādṛśa darśanāt asya prabodhe sati tat eva idam iti smṛtiḥ bhavati tatas abhilāṣa itarayoḥ anyataraḥ tatas api puruṣasya yathārham pravṛttiḥ iti evam tāvat ityādi nigamanam iha evam tāvat pañca indriya jam iti vacanāt tāvat śabdena anyat api apañca indriya jam asti tasya ca lakṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ pṛthak vakṣyamāṇaḥ iti etat sūcitam tat ca sarvam nirvikalpam eva iti nyāya mukhaḥ eva parigatam 
[I,50,i]	atas kasyacid nipuṇa mateḥ codyam āśaṅkate tatra idam codyam nanu sarve eva amī pratyakṣa bhedāḥ nirvikalpāḥ eva tatas ca pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti anena eva saṅgṛhītāḥ tathā hi nyāna mukhena eṣām pṛthak lakṣaṇam praṇītam tatra kim arthaḥ ayam iha pṛthak lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ ucyate iti atas asya parihārāya āha parama tāpekṣam ca atra viśeṣaṇam iti viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaḥ bhedaḥ iti paryāyāḥ tat ca prakṛta tvāt pratyakṣa lakṣaṇasya iti gamyate atra iti prakaraṇe yaḥ ayam pṛthak lakṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ sa pareṣām vipratipatti lakṣaṇam yat matam tad apekṣaḥ 
[I,50,ii]	tatra manaḥ vijñāne pratyakṣaḥ indriya jñāna anubhūtatam eva tam artham gṛhṇāti iti keṣāñcid vipratipattiḥ rāga ādi saṃvedane na asti eva tat iti yogi jñāne api eṣā eva yatas evam pareṣām vipratipattiḥ atas tad apekṣaḥ pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti anena saṅgṛhītasya api apañca indriya jasya pratyakṣasya pṛthak lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ ucyate para vipratipatti nirāsāya iti bhāvaḥ 
[I,50,iii_I,51,i]	apare tu kim punar pañca indriya jam sa vikalpam api asti yatas etat viśeṣaṇam iti āha parama tāpekṣam ca ityādi pareṣām indriya jam jñānam kiñcid sa vikalpakam yat vyutpanna vyavahārasya kiñcid avikalpakam yat itarasya iti matam atas tad apekṣam indriya jñānasya kalapana apoḍham iti etat viśeṣaṇam para parikalpita sa vikalpa indriya jñāna vyavaccheda artham iti vyācakṣate teṣām yadi parama tāpekṣam etat viśeṣaṇam uktam evam sati akriyamāṇe asmin parama tāpekṣe sva matena lakṣaṇam anuktam eva syāt tatas ca lakṣaṇam pratyakṣasya kim syāt etat ca udyama samāhitam syāt iti uktam etat sarve tu avikalpakāḥ eva iti tuśabdena na svamata apekṣaḥ ayam pṛthak lakṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ ucyate vipratipatteḥ abhāvāt iti artham dyotayati viśeṣaṇena pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti anena eva sarva lakṣya saṅgrahaḥ 
[I,51,ii]	mānasam ca ityādi caśabdaḥ samuccaya arthaḥ artha śabdaḥ ayam jñeya paryāyaḥ rāga ādīnām svam rāga ādi svam sva śabdaḥ ayam ātma vacanaḥ arthaḥ ca rāga ādi svam ca tasya saṃvittiḥ artha rāga ādi sva saṃvittiḥ saṃvedyate jñāyate anayā iti saṃvittiḥ saṃvitteḥ pratyekam abhisambandhaḥ sāvikalpikā mānasam pratyakṣam 
[I,51,iii]	tatra manaḥ vijñānam indriya gṛhītam eva artham gṛhṇāti tatas vā anyam iti dvayī kalpanā yadi pūrvā tatas tasya prāmāṇyam eva na syāt gṛhīta grahaṇāt smṛti ādi vat atha dvitīyā tadā andha ādeḥ api artha grahaṇam syāt indriya jñāna nirapekṣam hi manaḥ vijñānam yadi bāhye arthe pravartate tadā cakṣuḥ ādi vikalasya api darśanam prāpnoti tat vaktavyam kīdṛśam tat iti āha mānasam api ityādi rūpa ādayaḥ ca te viṣayāḥ ca iti karmadhārayaḥ 
[I,52,i]	nanu ca rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ eva tat kim artham viṣaya grahaṇam anālambyamāna rūpa ādi vyavaccheda artham na hi avijñāyamāna viṣayāḥ bhavanti kasya punar te viṣayāḥ anantaram indriya jñānasya prakṛta tvāt tasya eva rūpa ādi viṣayāṇām vikāraḥ rūpa ādi viṣaya vikāraḥ saḥ ālambanam yasya tat tathā uktam samudāya vikāra ṣaṣṭhyāḥ ca bahuvrīhiḥ uttara pada lopaḥ ca iti vacanāt samāse uttara pada lopaḥ ca suvarṇa alaṅkāraḥ iti yathā kaḥ punar viṣayasya vikāraḥ yaḥ tena janitaḥ uttarakṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ sa tasya vikāraḥ iti vyavahriyate na tu avasthite dharmiṇi dharma antara nivṛttau dharma antarau abhāvaḥ sāṅkhya parikalpitasya pariṇāmasya niṣiddha tvāt tat etat uktam bhavati indriya jñāna viṣaya janita samantara rūpa ādi kṣaṇa ālambanam iti anena aprāmāṇya doṣaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ kutas punar tasya niyata viṣaya tā iti ced yatas tasya yaḥ samanantara pratyaya viśeṣaḥ sa sva viṣaya upajanita anantara rūpa ādi kṣaṇa sahakāryā iva tat janayati atas tat yathā ukta viṣayam eva iti avagaccha 
[I,53,i]	anubhava ākāra pravṛttam iti anubhūyate anena iti anubhavaḥ ākāraḥ ābhāsaḥ sa punar ananubhava rūpaḥ api asti yaḥ smṛti ādīnām iti atas tad vyavacchedāya anubhava grahaṇam anubhavaḥ ākāraḥ yasya tat tathā uktam kim punar tat pūrva ukta nyāyena indriya jñānam eva tena anubhava ākāreṇa pravṛttam utpannam anubhava ākāra pravṛttam etat uktam bhavati indriya jñānāt samanantara pratyayāt utpannam iti anena yat uktam andha ādeḥ api artha grahaṇam syāt iti tat nirastam yasmāt na tad bāhyeṣu artheṣu svatantram pravartate kim tarhi indriya pratyaya apekṣam andha ādeḥ ca indriya jñānam na asti iti na asti tat 
[I,53,ii^1]	rāga ādiṣu ca sva saṃvedanam iti svasya saṃvedanam sva saṃvedanam saṃvedyate anena iti saṃvedanam grāhaka ākāra saṅkhyātam anubhava svabhāva tvam anubhava svabhāva tvāt eva hi rāga ādayaḥ anubhava ātma tayā prakāśamānāḥ ātmānam saṃvedayante ātma saṃvedanāḥ iti ca vyapadiśyante atas tad anubhava ātma tvam eṣām pramāṇam yat punarbhāva rūpam saṃvedanam sva adhigama ātmakam tat tasya phalam veditavyam ātmā tu teṣām prameyaḥ rāga ādi grahaṇam spaṣṭa saṃvedana darśana artham sarva jñānānām ātma saṃvedanasya pratyakṣa tvāt avikalpaka tvam tu tasya aśakya samaya tvāt viṣayīkṛte hi samayaḥ śakyate kartum na ca anutpannam rāga ādi ātmānam saṃvittiḥ viṣayīkaroti 
[I,53,ii^2]	rāga ādi ātma rūpa tayā tasyāḥ api anutpanna tvāt utpanne api rāga ādi ātmani saṃvittiḥ abhilāpam na yojayati tathā hi sa abhilāpam ādāya tatra yojayet abhilāpa grahaṇe ca kṣaṇika tvāt na sā na api rāga ādayaḥ iti kim kena yojyeta iti aśakya samaya tvāt rāga ādīnām saṃvittiḥ na āviṣṭa abhilāpāḥ yena yatra śabdasya samayaḥ na gṛhītaḥ na tad śabdena tam saṃyojya gṛhṇāti tat yathā cakṣuḥ vijñānam gandham na gṛhītaḥ ca rāga ādi ātmani tad saṃvedanena śabda samayaḥ kāraṇa abhāvaḥ 
[I,54,i]	atra kecid āhuḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ tathā hi sva saṃvitteḥ nirvikalpaka tvam sādhyam sā ca jñānasya api tāvat na samasti kutas punar sukha ādīnām ajñāna rūpāṇām te hi ekasmin ātamani jñānena saha samavāyāt tena eka artha samavāyinā gṛhyante iti svayam prameya rūpāḥ eva atas te parasya api na saṃvedakāḥ kutas punar ātmanaḥ iti taiḥ tat jñānam avaśyam sukha ādi ākāram abhyupeyam anyathā tasya te vedyāḥ eva na syuḥ na hi jñāna sattā eva arthānām saṃvedanā yuktā tasyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt sarva artha grahaṇa prasaṅgāt yat jñānam yat ākāra rahitam na tat tasya saṃvedakam go jñānam iva āśvasya sukha ādi ākāra rahitam ca sukha ādi jñānam vyāpaka virudddhaḥ 
[I,55,i]	bhavatu jñānam tat ākāram tatas kim iti ced idam tatas yat tat eva hlāda paritāpa ādi ākāra anugatam sukha ādi iti siddham sukha ādi jñāna rūpam bodha rūpam hi vastu sātā ādi rūpam teṣām api siddham tatra jñānam sukham duḥkham iti ādikāḥ yatheṣṭam sañjñāḥ kriyantām na atra kaścid nivārayitā yathā jñāta hlāda ādikaḥ ākāraḥ ajñāna rūpa sukha ādi kṛtaḥ na bhavati tathā anyatra pratipāditam iha tu bahu grantha bhayāt na pratanyate 
[I,55,ii]	yaḥ api āha na antārāḥ sukha ādayaḥ na api cetanāḥ kim tarhi tad viparīta svabhāvāḥ prameyāḥ eva iti tasya api yathā ukta nītyā hlāda ādi ākāra bodha ātmalkam vastu siddham tasya eva ca sva saṃvedanam pratyakṣam uktam na tad vyatiriktasya sukha ādeḥ para parikalpitasya tat ca sva saṃvedanam sādhayiṣyamāṇam iti na asti āśraya asiddhiḥ 
[I,56,i]	nanu sarvasya eva jñānasya indriya jasya api manaḥ āśrayaḥ iti api ete pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ indriya dvaya āśrayāḥ iti vacanāt tat kasmāt idam eva mānasam ucyate iti āha indriya anapekṣa tvāt iti rūpi indriya nirapekṣa tvāt iti bhāvaḥ yasya manaḥ eva āśrayaḥ na rūpi indriyam tad mānasam abhisaṃhitam ye tarhi pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ tad samprayoginaḥ ca rāga ādayaḥ teṣām sva saṃvedanam katham mānasam pratyakṣam sva saṃvitti sāmānyena tad jātīya tvāt katham punar indriya anapekṣa tve pratyakṣa śabdaḥ yujyate yāvatā akṣa nimittaḥ pratyakṣa vyapadeśaḥ uktam etat jñāna viśeṣasya pāribhāṣikī iyam sañjñā iti atha vā manasaḥ api akṣa tvāt pakṣa antare api adoṣaḥ 
[I,56,ii]	tathā yoginām iti yathā mānasam avikalpakam pratyakṣam tathā yoginām api yogaḥ samādhiḥ sa yeṣām asti te yoginaḥ guru nirdeśa avyavakīrṇam iti tena avyavakīrṇam rahitam iti arthaḥ etena spaṣṭa avabhāsi tvam api tasya labdham nirvikalpasya spaṣṭa tva avyabhicāri tvāt mātra śabdaḥ adhyāropita artha vyavaccheda arthaḥ tena yat bhūta artha viṣayam ārya satya darśana vat tat eva pramāṇam na abhūta artha viṣayam viplutam pṛthivīkṛtsnā ādi nanu ca ayam arthaḥ vakṣyamāṇāt eva apavādāt labhyate tat kim mātra grahaṇena satyam etat tathā api prādhānya jñāpana artham asya lakṣaṇa vākyaḥ eva ayam arthaḥ paridīpitaḥ prādhānnyam punar mokṣa hetu tvāt nirvikalpaka tvam punar tasya spaṣṭa avabhāsi tvam ca bhāvanā niṣpatti phala tvāt yat bhāvanā niṣpatti phalam jñānam tat nirvikalpam spaṣṭa avabhāsi ca bhavati tat yathā kāma śoka ādi upaplutānām priyā viṣayam jñānam tathā ca yogi jñānam svabhāvaḥ 
[I,57,i]	kalpanā jñānam api nāma iti asya ayam arthaḥ yat sva saṃvedyam tat svādhigamam prati pratyakṣam rāga ādi jñāna vat tathā ca kalpanā jñānam iti svabhāvaḥ satyam etat ityādinā iṣṭa siddhim darśayati evam manyate yatra viṣaye yat jñānam śabda saṅketa grāhi tat tatra śabda dvāreṇa tasya viṣaya grahaṇāt sa vikalpakam bhavati svarūpam ca aśakya samayam yathoktam prāk atas tatra adhigantavye sarvam jñānam pratyakṣam eva iti 
[I,57,ii_I,58,i]	evam tāvat pratyakṣam iti tāvat śabdaḥ krame pratyakṣam uktvā tad ābhāsa abhidhānam iti kramaḥ nanu ca pratyakṣam kalapana apoḍham iti bruvatā sa vikalpam pratyakṣa ābhāsam iti uktam bhavati tat ca prāk eva uktam nāma jāti ādi yojanena tat kim artham punar tasya vacanam yat artham tat utttaratra āviṣkariṣyāmaḥ 
[I,58,ii]	bhrānti saṃvṛti sat jñānam ityādi anena caturvidham pratyakṣa ābhāsam uktam tatra bhrānti jñānam iti anena anya artha kalpanā jñānam ekam tāvat uktam tathā hi asat eva udaka ādikam artha antaram saṅketa samāśrayāt mṛgatṛṣṇā ādiṣu adhyāropayanti upadyate kalpanā saṃvṛti satsu ityādinā saṅketa samāśraya samāropa kalpanā pravṛttam dvitīyam kim punar kāraṇam saṃvṛti satsu yat jñānam tat pratyakṣa ābhāsam iti āha artha antara adhyāropāt iti tat dhi prajñapti vastuṣu rūpa ādiṣu artha antara bhūtān ghaṭa ādīn adhyāropayati na prajñapti vastu mātram pratipadyate katham punar etat jñāyate iti āha tad rūpa kalpanā pravṛttta tvāt iti tat dhi tān saṃvṛti satas artha antara tvena kalpayat upadyate adhyāropita artha ākāra kalpanayā pravṛtta tvāt saṃvṛti jñānam ghaṭa ādīn adhyāropayati na tu tad prajñapti vastu mātram pratyeti 
[I,58,iii]	tatra tāvat rūpa ādīnām udaka āharaṇa ādi eka kārya tayā tad anyebhyaḥ bhinnānām sakṛt samuditānām sva kārye niyojana artham tatra lokasya yaḥ śabda saṅketaḥ tam āśrayam kṛtvā artha antareṇa ghaṭa ādinā rahiteṣu api rūpa ādiṣu bhāvataḥ artha antaram adhyāropayantī pravartate kalpanā ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ iti ādikā tathā samuccaya ādi vyavaccheda phala śabda niveśa samāśrayeṇa eka tva ādi veśinī tathā deśa antara utpādiṣu evam satsu tathā bahuṣu eka kāryeṣu samudāyeṣu evam nairantaryādi avastheṣu atathā bhūta tavyavat chedāya śabda samayam āśritya artha antara bhūtam karma sattām ghaṭa tva ādi saṃyoga ādi ca yathākramam adhyāropayanti upajāyate kalpanā tat evam prabhedataḥ śabda kalpā eva saṅketa mātra samāśrayam dvitīyam etat kalpanā jñānam 
[I,59,i]	mṛgatṛṣṇā ādiṣu yā toya ādi kalpanā sā na anuda kavyavacchedāya udake kṛtam saṅketa mātra āśritya pravartate yena saṅketa samāśraya ayam eva antarbhāvāt na pṛthak vacanam tasyāḥ syāt kim tarhi asat eva udaka ādikam tatra bhūta saṅghāte saṅketa samāśrayāt pūrva dṛṣṭam anyat eva artham adhyāropayanti utpadyate atas eva āha toya ādi kalpanā pravṛtta tvāt iti ghaṭa ādayaḥ tu sva upādānāt anye na santi eva saṅketa mātra nimittā eva tad adhyāropiṇī kalpanā iti pūrvasyāḥ pṛthak uktā 
[I,59,ii_I,60,i]	anumāna tad phala ādi jñānam iti anumīyate anena iti anumānam liṅgam tatra saḥ eva ayam dhūmaḥ iti sambandha kāla anubhūta artha kalpanā pravṛttam jñānam tad phale api liṅgi jñāne pūrva anubhūta kalpanā asti saḥ eva atra agniḥ iti sāmānyena anumānāt smārte api pūrva anubhūta ākāraḥ vikalpaḥ ittham tad mayā anubhūtam iti ābhilāṣikam api pūrva anubhūta kalpanām na ativartate vinā tyābhilāṣa abhāvāt ādi śabdena saṃśaya jñāna grahaṇam tatra api kim tat eva idam āhosvit anyat iti evam ākārā pūrva anubhūta kalpanā jāyate iti idam pūrva anubhūta artha kalpanā jñānam tṛtīyam sa taimiram iti anena indriya upaghāta jam ca taimira ādi jñānam caturtham pratyakṣa ābhāsam uktam iti 
[I,60,ii]	tatra dve pūrvake kalpanā jñāne na pratyakṣe iti khyāpana artham ukte kutas punar tayoḥ pratyakṣa āśaṅkā yena tad nivṛttaye yatnaḥ kriyate te hi pratyakṣasya saṃvṛttinī tasmāt sūkṣmam utpāda kāla vibhāgam duravadhāra tvāt anupalakṣayataḥ pratyakṣe eva ete iti kasyacid matiḥ syāt dṛśyate ca keṣāñcid vipratipattiḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiṣu jñānam saṃvṛti satsu mṛgatṛṣṇā ādiṣu ca udaka ādi jñānam pratyakṣam eva iti tathā hi tasya eva mṛgatṛṣṇā ādau toya ādi jñānasya vyavacchedāya avi abhicāri iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇe viśeṣaṇam upāttam akṣa upaghāta ja jñāna nivṛtti artham tat iti ced na artha san nikarṣa grahaṇāt evān artha sambhūtasya dvi candra ādi jñānasya nivṛtteḥ anyathā indriya jam iti eva vācyam syāt 
[I,61,i]	anumāna ādi jñānam tu siddham eva yathāpūrva anubhūta samaya smṛti bala pravṛttam apratyakṣam ca iti tasya apratyakṣa tve siddhe api yat iha upādānām tat pūrvayoḥ eva kalpanā jñānayoḥ apratyakṣa tva sādhanāya yat pūrva anubhūta samaya smṛti bala bhāvi na tat pratyakṣam yathā idam anumāna ādi jñānam tathā ca pūrvake jñāne vyāpaka viruddhaḥ tat evam trividham eva kalpanā jñānam lakṣaṇa vacanena arthāpattitaḥ nirastam 
[I,61,ii]	caturthaḥ tu yaḥ pratyakṣa ābhāsaḥ saḥ apavādaḥ atra draṣṭavyaḥ na tu lakṣaṇa vacanena artha āpattyā nirākṛtasya udāharaṇam anyathā lakṣaṇa vyabhicāraḥ syāt tasmāt tena apavāda vacanena bāhya abhyantara upaghāta pratyaya upahata indriya jñānam kalpanā apoḍha tve api pratyakṣa ābham ucyate sa taimiram iti atra tu timiram sarva indriya upaghāta pratyaya upalakṣaṇa mātram kila draṣṭavyam 
[I,61,iii]	yaḥ tu āha dvi candra ādi jñānam na eva indriya jam api tu mānasam eva iti tena vaktavyam kim indriya jasya lakṣaṇam iti indriya bhāva abhāva anuvidhānam iti ced tat iha api tulyam tad vikāra vikāri tvam iti ced atra api etat eva uttaram api ca icchayā sarpa ādi bhrānti vat eva tat nivartyeta śakyante hi kalpanāḥ pratisaṅkhyāna balena nivartayitum kim ca vikṛta akṣasya vikāra nivṛttau kalpayataḥ api na nivarteta na ca edam tasmāt idam api aindriyam eva uktam ca ācāryeṇa te api hi paramārthataḥ anyathā vidyamānāḥ dvi candra ādi ābhāsasya nīla ādi ābhāsasya ca jñāsya kāraṇam bhavanti iti na atra abhiniveṣṭavyam yatas evam indriya jam api viplutam asti atas eva bhrānti ityādinā uktāt vikalpa vargāt iti karaṇa vyavacchinnāt pṛthak avikalpakam pratyakṣa ābham ācāryeṇa uktam sa taimiram iti 
[I,62,i^1]	atra codyate iha avisaṃvādi pravartakam jñānam pramāṇam abhimatam na hi ābhyām artham paricchidya pravartamānaḥ artha kriyāyām visaṃvādyate iti abhidhānāt indriya upaghāta jasya api ca kasyacid jñānasya kvacid samīhite avisaṃvādanam pravartaka tvam ca asti eva tatas yat etat keśa ādi pratibhāsi taimira ādi jñānam yasya samīhite keśa ādi vastuni saṃvādaḥ na asti tasya mā bhūt prāmāṇyam yat punar etat kāmalā upapluta locanasya śukre śaṅkha ādau pīta śaṅkha ādi nirbhāsam yat ca cira kāla timira āvṛta nayana tvāt viprakṛṣṭa tvāt vā spaṣṭeṣu nīla ādiṣu aspaṣṭa nīla ādi ākāram yat api naiyāna saṅkṣobha āhita vibhramam sthireṣu api vṛkṣa ādiṣu gami kriyā āviṣṭa pādapādi pratibhā asi tasya evam prakārasya ani asya api ca ātasmin tad grahāt bhrāntasya api vastuni pratibandhāt īpsita artha avisaṃvādinaḥ kvacid prāmāṇyam eva nyāyyam tathā hi tatas pravartamānaḥ asati pratibandhe niyamena śaṅkha ādi vastu mātra āyāta artha kriyā samartham artham abhisamīhitam āsādayati atha saṃvādinām api eṣām vitatha pratibhāsi tvāt prāmāṇyam na iṣyate 
[I,62,i^2]	anumānasya api tarhi na iṣṭavyam atas eva na ca na iṣyate tasmāt teṣām api samīhita artha kriyā samarthe śaṅkha ādi vastu mātre yatra saṃvādaḥ tatra aviruddham prāmāṇyam paśyāmaḥ śakyate ca vaktum yatas jñānāt pravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ asati pratibandhe niyamena abhīṣṭam artham āsādayati tat tatra tasya pramāṇam tat yathā abhimatam pratyakṣam anumānam ca yathā uktāt ca jñānāt pravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ asati pratibandhe niyamena abhīṣṭam śaṅkha ādi vastu mātram āsādayati iti svabhāvaḥ na ca idam anumānam aliṅga ja tvāt nirvikalpa tvāt ca na ca tṛtīyam pramāṇam iṣṭam itas pratyakṣam eva iti abhyupeyam yat kalpanā apoḍham samīhita artha avisaṃvādi tat pratyakṣam tat yathā abhimatam pratyakṣam tathā ca prakṛtam jñānam svabhāvaḥ 
[I,64,i]	syāt etat śaṅkha ādi mātre vastuni samīhite saṃvāda ādiṣṭam eva tasya pratyakṣa tvam viśiṣṭe tu pīta ādi ākāravati visaṃvādān na iṣyate iti na tarhi sa taimiram iti anena apavāda padena bāhya abhyantara upaghāta pratyaya upahata indriya jñānam kalpanā apoḍha tve api pratyakṣa ābham uktam kevalam tatra sa taimira vacane timiram sarva indriya upaghāta pratyaya upalakṣaṇa mātram iti evam vyākhyeyam upahata indriya jñānasya api kasyacid pratyakṣa tvāt na api abhrāntam iti viśeṣaṇam kartavyam bhrāntasya api kasyacid kvacid pratyakṣa tvena iṣṭa tvāt 
[I,64,ii^1]	tasmāt sa taimiram iti etat apavāda padam anyathā vyākhyāyate timira śabdaḥ ayam iha ajñāna vacanaḥ yathā nimira ghnam ca mandānām ityādau vākye timire bhavaḥ taimiraḥ vyavaccheda phala tvāt ca vākyasya sarva vākyam sa avadhāraṇam iti timiraḥ eva bhavaḥ iti sa avadhāraṇe vākya arthe tat dhitaḥ bhavati kaḥ punar asau visaṃvādaḥ sa hi yadi bhavati ajñānaḥ eva bhavati na jñāne tasya ekāntena saṃvādi tvāt prasiddhataram ca etat loke saha tena taimireṇa vartate iti sa taimiram 
[I,64,ii^2]	visaṃvādī iti yāvat sa vikalpasya ca visaṃvādinaḥ bhrānti ādi śabdena upādānāt idam nirvikalpam avasīyate smārta abhilāṣikam ca iti ca ayam vaśabdaḥ samuccaya arthaḥ bhinnakramaḥ ca sa taimiram ca iti evam draṣṭavyaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ bhavati visaṃvādi ca jñānam pratyakṣa ābhāsam iti evam bhrāntasya api nirvikalpasya yata saṃvādaḥ tatra pratyakṣa tvam yatra tu visaṃvādaḥ tatra tad ābhāsa tvam iti etat siddham bhavati na ca evam sati kaścid virodhaḥ kalpanā jñāna vat yathā hi kalpanā jñānasya sva adhigama apekṣayā pratyakṣa tvam bāhya viṣaya apekṣayā tat ābhāsa tvam na viruddhyate tathā yathā uktasya api jñānasya viṣaya bheda apekṣayā tat ubhayam iti 
[I,65,i_I,65,ii]	atra ca iti asmad mate sa vyāpāra pratīta tvāt iti saha vyāpāreṇa pratītya tvāt iti arthaḥ etat pramāṇa tva upacāra nibandhanam pramāṇam phalam eva sat iti pramāṇasya adhigamaḥ phalam tat ca svayam eva tad ātmakam iti tatas na vyatiriktam na hi atra bāhyakānām iva pramāṇāt artha antaram phalam iti mā bhūt iha api tadvat eva doṣaḥ tasya eva tu ityādinā ayam arthaḥ sūcitaḥ na eva vyavasthira svabhāvam kiñcid asti sādhyam sādhanam vā pratīti rūpa anupāti tvāt sarvatra sādhya sādhana vyavahārasya iha api ca asti jñānasya adhigama rūpa tvāt sādhya tva pratītiḥ iti phala tvam upacaryate tasya eva ca viṣaya ākāra parigrahāt sa vyāpāra pratītiḥ iti pramāṇa tvam upacaryate vyavahriyate iti arthaḥ tathā hi tat jñānam viṣaya ākāra tām dadhānam nirvyāpāram api satsu a viṣaye adhigama ātmanā vyāpāreṇa khyāti na anyathā tasmāt sā eva tasya ātma bhūtā viṣaya ākāra tā pramāṇam iti 
[I,66,i]	yuktam ca etat tathā hi na kriyā sādhanam iti eva sarvasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sarvam sādhanam sarvā vā kriyā sarvasya sādhyā anavasthā prasaṅgāt kim tarhi tasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ tad sādhanam yā yatas sādhanāt avyavadhānena prasiddhim upayāti sā eva ca tasya kriyā sādhyā tatra rūpa ādau karmaṇi anubhava ātmanā sādṛśya ātmanaḥ jñānasya tena svabhāvena karaṇa bhūtena bhāvyam yena idam nīlasya jñānam idam pītasya iti vibhāgena vyavasthā kriyate anyathā sarvam jñānam sarvasya arthasya syāt na vā kasyacid kiñcid aviśeṣāt 
[I,66,ii_I,67,i]	indriya ādeḥ āvilatā ādi bhedaḥ niyāmakaḥ iti ced na tasya ajñāna svabhāva tvāt sarva jñāna hetu tvāt ca na api san nikarṣaḥ atas eva na api artha ālocanam asati viṣaya sārūpye artha ālocanasya eva asiddheḥ viśeṣaṇa jñānam api atas eva tasmāt yaḥ ayam niyamaḥ nīlasya eva iyam adhigatiḥ pītasya eva ca iti ādikaḥ saḥ artha sārūpyāt anyatas na sidhyati tatas tat eva sādhanam artha adhigateḥ sarva kārakopa yoge api asya arthasya iyam adhigatiḥ iti sambandhasya tatas eva avyavadhānena siddheḥ tat ca tasya sādhana tvam vyavasthā samāśraya tvena na tu nirvartaka tvena abhedāt 
[I,67,ii]	syāt etat vastunaḥ abhedāt jñāna aṃśayoḥ aikye yā eva kriyā tat eva kārakam atas hatam etat iti tat asat yatas vastunaḥ abhede api yaḥ ayam dharma bhedaḥ prameya rūpa tā artha adhigatiḥ ca iti saḥ abhyupagamyate eva vyāvṛtti bheda upakalpitaḥ abhinne api vastuni vijñāna pratibhāsa bhedena sādhya sādhana vyavasthā darśanāt ca yathā nipīyamānam madhum adayati ātmanā ātmānam dhārayati buddhyā gṛhṇāti iti na ayam vastu san niveśī sādhya sādhana vyavahāraḥ iti acodyam etat 
[I,68,i]	katham yathāvyāpāram antareṇa api tadvat tayā pratibhāsate iti āha tat yathā ityādi iha nīla ādi ākāraḥ ekaḥ eva anubhūyate sa vijñānasya ātma bhūtaḥ avaśyam abhyupeyaḥ anyathā tasya arthena sambandhaḥ na syāt na ca tasmāt tad ākāram atat ākāram vā bahis vyatiriktam vastu upalabhyate na ca ālambanam gaṭate katham ca na ghaṭate yathā ca na ghaṭate tathā vāda vidhi parīkṣāyām vakṣyati 
[I,68,ii]	yat api idam kalpyate satsu api anyeṣu hetuṣu jñāna kārya aniṣpattiḥ kāraṇa antaram sūcayati sa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ syāt tasmāt vyatirekataḥ bāhya artha sidhiḥ iti tat api ayuktam yatas vijñāna kārya aniṣpattiḥ vijñāna vāsanā paripāka vaikalyāt api sambhavati tasmāt na vijñāna vyatiriktasya kasyacid saṃvittiḥ sambhavati vijñānam eva tu sva saṃvid itam utpadyate iti sva saṃvittiḥ eva phalam bhavatu nāma bāhya arthaḥ tathā api yathā saṃvedanam eva viṣayaḥ niścīyate iti tat eva phalam yuktam na hi yathā svabhāvam anubhavaḥ arthasya yatas yathā asau vyavasthita svarūpaḥ tathā śakyeta niścetum sarva jñānānām eka ākāra tva prasaṅgāt aneka ākārāḥ tu vijñaptayaḥ tathā hi ekasmin eva vastuni pratipattṛ bhedena paṭum anda tā ādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ anugatāni vijñānāni upalabhyante na ca ekam vastu aneka ākāram aneka tva prasaṅgāt
