[I,69,i_I,69,ii]	atas na arthasya yathā svabhāvam niścayaḥ śakyate kartum iti sandhānaḥ bāhya itar apakṣayoḥ ekena eva sūtreṇa phala viśeṣa vyavasthām cikīrṣuḥ āha sva saṃvittiḥ phalam vātra iti pūrvam viṣaya saṃvittiḥ phalam uktā atas vikalpa arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ atra iti pūrva ukte pratyakṣe su ābhāsam viṣaya ābhāsam ca iti svam ābhāsaḥ asya iti su ābhāsam sva rūpa ābhāsam grāhaka ākāram iti arthaḥ sva rūpam eva asya jñānasya ābhāsaḥ yat eva hi jñānasya jñāna rūpa tvam tena eva svena rūpeṇa ābhāsate iti kṛtvā viṣaya ābhāsam ca iti atra yadā bāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ āśrīyate tadā viṣayasya iva ābhāsaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ yadā tu na āśrīyate tadā viṣayaḥ ābhāsaḥ asya iti viṣayaḥ punar atra grāhya aṃśaḥ tatra viṣaya vyavahārāt tasya ityādi sati asati vā bāhye arthaḥ ubhaya ābhāsam jñānam saṃvedyate tasya yat sva saṃvedanam sva anubhavaḥ tad phalam bhaviṣyati 
[I,69,iii]	kim kāraṇam iti kayā yuktyā na hi sva saṃvittiḥ sambhavati iti eva phala tvena kalpayitum yujyate bāhya artha pakṣe tu asambhāvanīyam eva etat viṣayasya hi adhigamāya cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ vyāpāryante na tu vijñānasya na ca vijñāna upalabdhiḥ eva viṣaya upalabdhiḥ vijñānāt viṣaya bhedāt atas sva saṃvitteḥ phala tvam anupapannam iti manyamānasya praśnaḥ 
[I,70,i]	tad rūpaḥ hi artha niścayaḥ iti kāraṇam yadā hi ityādyasya eva vivaraṇam hi śabdaḥ yasmāt arthe yasmāt yadā sa viṣayam jñānam arthaḥ tadā sva saṃvedana anurūpam artham pratipadyate pratipatta iṣṭam aniṣṭam vā tasmāt sva saṃvittiḥ phalam yujyate sa viṣayam iti saha viṣayeṇa sa viṣayam tatra antar jñeya pakṣe grāhyān alakṣaṇena viṣayeṇa sa viṣayam tatra eva viṣaya vyavasthānāt bāhya artha pakṣe tu bāhyena tatra vijñaptimātra tāyām vijñāna vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ abhāvāt buddhiḥ eva yat eṣṭam svam ākāram anubhavati tat eṣṭam artham niścinoti viparyayāt viparītam 
[I,70,ii]	katham punar ātmanā eva ātmānam anubhavati jñānam na hi tasya eva karma kartṛ karaṇa bhāvaḥ yujyate iti ced evam etat na eva tasya paramārthataḥ karma ādi bhāvaḥ tathā api tādātmyāt prakāśa vat tatra tathā avyavahāraḥ na virudhyate prakāśaḥ hi ātma prakāśanam bhavati na pradīpa antaram apekṣate na api ātmānam bhāvataḥ prakāśayati kevalam prakāśa ātmatayā utpadyamānaḥ ātmanaḥ prakāśakaḥ iti ucyate tadvat anubhavāt manopajāyamānā buddhiḥ ātmanaḥ prakāśikā iti vyavahriyate bāhya pakṣe api yathā saṃvedanam eva arthaḥ avasīyate na hi yathārtham anubbhavaḥ iti prāk eva uktam 
[I,71,i]	atha saṃvedana anurūpam artham pratipadyate iṣṭam aniṣṭam vā iti etāvat eva kim na uktam kim yadā hi sa viṣayam jñānam arthaḥ tadā iti anena asti prayojanam yasmāt prāk sva saṃvedanam pramāṇam uktam tena ca jñāna svarūpam eva saṃvedyate iti sva saṃvedanam tasya eva phalam iti sphuṭam avasīyate tatas ca sva saṃvedana anurūpam hi artham pratipadyate iṣṭam aniṣṭam vetīyati ucyamāne sva saṃvedanam eva pratyakṣam adhikṛtya idam phala vyavasthānam iti kasyacid āśaṅkā syāt sarvasya ca pramāṇasya idam phalam iti atas āśaṅkā nivāraṇa artham yadā hi sa viṣayam jñāna arthaḥ iti uktam artha śabdaḥ ca ayam prameya vacanaḥ sa viṣayam iti ca sākalye avyayībhāvaḥ atas etat uktam bhavati na kevalam yadā jñānam pramāṇasya prameyam apekṣate tadā sva saṃvedana anurūpam artham pratipadyate iti sva saṃvittiḥ phalam api tu yadā api viṣayam tadā api iti 
[I,71,ii]	iha asati bāhye arthe sva saṃvedana phala vyavasthāyām grāhaka ākārasya prāmāṇyam vakṣyati tatas ca asati bāhye arthe prameye yathā sva saṃvedana phala vyavasthāne grāhaka ākāraḥ pramāṇam iṣṭam tathā sati bāhye arthe prameye grāhaka ākāraḥ eva pramāṇam iti āśaṅkā syāt atas tat nirāsāya āha yadā tu ityādi bāhye prameye sva saṃvedana phala vyavasthāyām api viṣaya ābhāsa tā eva jñānasya pramāṇam iṣyate na tu vijñaptimātra tāvat grāhaka ākāraḥ 
[I,72,i]	nanu yadā api bāhyaḥ arthaḥ prameyaḥ iti pakṣaḥ tadā api grāhaka ākāraḥ abhimataḥ eva tasya sva saṃvedya tvāt tat kim iti tadā pramāṇa tvena na vyavasthāpyate iti āha tadā hi jñāna sva saṃvedyam api ityādi jñānasya sva saṃvedyam iti vigrahaḥ yadi api sarvakālam sva saṃvedyam asti svarūpam tathā api tat anapekṣya jñānasya bāhye prameye viṣaya ābhāsa tā eva pramāṇam na su ābhāsa tā bāhye arthe tasyāḥ sādhana tva ayogāt ayogaḥ tu apara artha tvāt grāhaka ākāraḥ hi ātma viṣayaḥ katham bāhye arthe pramāṇam syāt na hi anya viṣayasya anyatra prāmāṇyam yuktam 
[I,72,ii]	yasmāt ityādinā tasya prāmāṇye kāraṇam āha mīyate iti niścīyate yathā yathā ityādi jñānasya jeyā ākāra vaśena bāhyaḥ arthaḥ niścīyate iti arthaḥ atra ca yathā dhūmena agniḥ anumīyate iti ucyate na ca asau sākṣāt tena anumīyate kim tarhi tad hetukena dhūma jñānena tathā yat api saḥ arthaḥ tena mīyate iti ucyate tathā api tad sādhanayā sva saṃvidā iti veditavyam tathā hi yathā yathā artha ākāraḥ jñāne san niviśate śubha aśubha ādi rūpeṇa tathā tathā sva saṃvittiḥ prathate yathā yathā ca sā khyāti tathā tathā arthaḥ niścīyate śubha aśubha ādi rūpa ādiḥ yadi hi tad ākāram utpannam syāt tadā tādṛśasya ātmahaḥ saṃvittiḥ syāt tatas ca tad vaśa ādi viṣaya niścayaḥ bhavet na anyathā tasmāt viṣaya ābāsa tā pramāṇam 
[I,73,i_I,73,ii]	nanu ca iha viṣaya sārūpyasya saṃvidam prati sādhana tvam pratipādayitum iṣṭam atas yasmāt sā khyāti tad vaśāt iti vaktavye kim artham yasmāt saḥ arthaḥ tena mīyate iti uktam asti prayojanam sā hi sva saṃvid artha saṃvidaḥ yat kāryam artha niścayaḥ tat karoti atas upacāreṇa artha saṃvid eva kāryataḥ draṣṭavyā iti amum artham sūcayitum evam uktam evam hi pramāṇa phalayoḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ na bhavati yatra eva sādhanam bāhye tatra eva saṃvid iti kṛtvā katham tarhi sva saṃvittiḥ phalam uktam paramārthataḥ tādātmyāt sva saṃvittiḥ phalam uktam upacāreṇa tu kāryataḥ artha saṃvittiḥ eva sā dṛṣṭavyā iti aviruddham iha vijñaptimātra tāyām grāhaka ākāraḥ pramāṇam grāhya ākāraḥ prameyam iti vakṣyati atas tatra ca udyam āśaṅkate 
[I,73,iii]	tatra idam codyam katham punar abhinna ātmanaḥ jñānasya grāhaka ākāra ādi vibhāgaḥ yena asati api bāhye arthe pramāṇa ādi syāt iti atas tat parihārāya āha evam ityādi asyāyām samudāya arthaḥ na eva tattvataḥ tasya vibhāgaḥ asti kevalam avidyā upaplutaiḥ tad grāhaka ākāra ādi vibhāga vat iva lakṣyate atas yathādarśanam iyam pramāṇa prameya vyavasthā kriyate na yathātvam iti katham punar avibhaktam sat tathā pratibhāsate yathā mantra ādi upapluta akṣāṇām mṛd śakala ādayaḥ hasti ādi rūpa rahitāḥ api hasti ādi rūpāḥ pratibhāsante yathā ca dūre maruṣu mahān alpaḥ api ābhāti tathā idam api avidyān dhānām jñānam atathābhūtam api tathā ābhāti na ca śakyate kalpayitum mantra ādi sāmarthyāt te tathā eva utpannāḥ iti yatas anupapluta darśanaiḥ tad deśa san nihitaiḥ tathā na dṛśyante 
[I,74,i]	evam iti yathoktam dvi ābhāsam jñānam iti jñāna saṃvedanam iti jñānasya karmaṇaḥ saṃvedanam darśanam kimbhūtam aneka ākāram anekā ākārāḥ yasya tat tathā uktam te punar ākārāḥ yaḥ anena bhrāntena nirīkṣyante grāhaka pratibhāsa ādayaḥ te vivakṣitāḥ upādāya iti tad pramāṇa nibandhanam gṛhītvā tathā tathā ityādi nirvikalpe tāvat grāhaka ākāraḥ kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣam pramāṇam spaṣṭa pratibhāsaḥ grāhya ākāraḥ sva lakṣaṇam prameyam liṅga je api grāhaka ākāraḥ anumānam pramāṇam vyakti bheda anuyāyī vāspaṣṭa pratibhāsaḥ grāhya ākāraḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇam prameyam iti upacaryate iti vyavahniyate etena etat sūcayati vyāvahārikasya pramāṇasya prameṇasya ca idam svarūpam uktam atra api vipratipannānām sammmonirāsāya loka uttaram eva tu vibhrama viveka nirmalam anapāyi pāramārthikam pramāṇam tasya eva ca gocaraḥ bhūtam prameyam iti 
[I,75,i]	nirvyāpārāḥ tu sarva dharmāḥ iti etena tasya jñāna saṃvedanasya bhrānta tvam udbhāvitam na hi tattvataḥ kasyacid dharmasya aneka ākāra darśana ātmakaḥ vyavahāraḥ sambhavati ākārāṇām apariniṣpanna tvāt bhrāntiḥ eva tu sā yat avidyān dhāstad avedya vedaka ākāram api jñānam tathā paśyanti yadi tarhi atattva vidām sarvam eva jñānam upaplutam katham pramāṇa itara vyavasthā upaplava vāsanā viśeṣa sadbhāvāt yatas jala ādi pratibhāsinaḥ jñānāt sparśana āhlāt atṛpti ādi pratyayānām sambhavaḥ tad vyavahāra avisaṃvāda apekṣayā pramāṇam itarat tathāvidha vāsanā virahāt apramāṇam iti adoṣaḥ 
[I,75,ii]	atha yat idam kāryāt kāraṇa anumānam tat katham katham ca na syāt yatas dhūma pratibhāsi jñānam pūrvam eva āvirbhavati paścāt anala pratibhāsi na hi tad prāk dhūma pratibhāsinaḥ jñānāt saṃvedyate tatas anagni janyaḥ eva dhūmaḥ syāt iti katham tena agneḥ anumānam na eṣa doṣaḥ dahana ākāra jñāna janana vāsanā viśeṣa anugataḥ eva hi citta santānaḥ dhūma ābhāsām dhiyam utpādayati na tu yaḥ kaścid atas tam gamayat dhūmatuḥ jñānam prabodha paṭu vāsanām dahana ākārām buddhim bhaviṣyantīm pratipattuḥ gamayati atra hi hetu dharma anumānena rasāde rūpa ādi vat anumānam bhavati iti acodyam 
[I,76,i]	āha ca ityādinā tām prameya ādi vyavasthām darśayati yaḥ ābhāsaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ sva aṃśasya ca māna tvena vidhānāt iha viṣaya ābhāsaḥ gṛhyate prameyam tat iti sa viṣaya ābhāsaḥ prameyam pramāṇa phalate punar grāhaka ākāra saṃvittyoḥ iti grāhaka ākārasya pramāṇa tā saṃvitteḥ phala tā atra ca yadi api saṃvitti śruteḥ aplāctara tvam tathā api grāhaka ākārasya pramāṇa tvāt tasya ca vyutpādya tvena adhikṛta tvāt abhyarhita tvam atas grāhaka ākāra śabdasya eva pūrva nipātaḥ trayam na atas pṛthak kṛtam iti trayasya api tattvataḥ apariniṣpanna tvāt na jñānāt pṛthak karaṇam 
[I,77,i]	iha dvi rūpa tām aṅgīkṛtya sva saṃvitteḥ phala tvam uktam na ca tat dvairūpyam jñānasya upapadyate tad anupapatti abhāvāt iti matvā pṛcchati atha dvi rūpam ityādi kasmāt punar trairūpye praṣṭavye dvi rūpa tā praśnaḥ dvairūpye siddhe sva saṃvittiḥ api sidhyati iti abhiprāyāt dvairūpye hi siddhe viṣaya sārūpyam ātma bhūtam jñānasya saṃvedyate iti arthāt ātma saṃvedanam sidhyati 
[I,77,ii]	viṣaya jñāna viśeṣāt tu ityādi viṣaya jñānam rūpa ādi grāhi cakurādi vijñānam viṣaya jñānam viṣa ya jña ānata jñānam atra yadi tad śabdena viṣaya jñānam sambadhyeta tasya upādānam anarthakam syāt vinā api tena viṣaya jñāna ālambanasya jñānasya pratīteḥ tasmāt tad chanda upādāna sāmarthyāt guṇa bhūtaḥ api viṣayaḥ sambadhyate anyasya iha aprakṛta tvāt tat etat uktam bhavati viṣaya jñāne viṣaya ākāram jñānam iti tat eva viśeṣaḥ tathā hi tad viṣaya jñānāt adhikena viṣaya ākāreṇa viśiṣyate para abhiprāyeṇa evam uktam paraḥ hi viṣaya jñānasya anubhava ākāram kevalam icchati tat jñānasya tu anubhava ākāraḥ api asti atra ca buddheḥ anubhava ākārasya siddha tvāt sa sādhyate na hi kaścid vādī yaḥ jñānasya jñāna rūpam na icchati viṣaya ākārāḥ tu na siddhiḥ parasya iti tena dvairūpyam sādhyate 
[I,78,i]	viṣaye hi iti hi śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe bhinna kramaḥ ca tad artha sva ābhāsam eva iti etat pramāṇa phalam tatra artha ābhāsam viṣaya ākāra tvāt su a ābhāsam anubhava ākāra tvāt viṣaya anurūpa jñāna ābhāsam iti rūpa ādeḥ viṣayasya anurūpam jñānam viṣaya ākāram viṣaya jñānam sva jñānena ālambyate iti eṣa hetuḥ uktaḥ yatra hi jñāne yat vastu yena ākāreṇa pratibhāsate tat tat ākāram eva tena ālambyate iti etat uktam tathā hi sāsna ādi ākāreṇa gauḥ sva jñāne pratibhāsamānaḥ tad ākāraḥ eva tena ālambyate viṣaya jñāna jñāne ca viṣaya ākāra anurakta viṣaya jñāna ākāraḥ eva upalabhyate na tu tad vyatirekeṇa kiñcid ākāra antaram na ca apratibhāsamānaḥ tasya viṣayaḥ yujyate atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt viṣaya ākāram viṣaya jñānam sva jñānena ālambyate iti eṣa hetu arthaḥ labhyate su ābhāsam ca iti viṣaya ākāra viṣaya jñāna ābhāsam sat svarūpeṇa api pratibhāsate iti arthaḥ 
[I,78,ii^1]	anyathā iti dvi rūpa tā bhāve yadi viṣaya anurūpam eva viṣaya jñānam syāt iti na anubhava rūpam api nanu ca na eva kaścid viṣaya eka rūpam jñānam icchati tat kim artham idam uktam viṣaya ākāre jñāne sādhyamāne kvacid iyam āśaṅkā syāt viṣaya ākāram ced jñānam pratipadyate sva rūpa parityāgena eva pratipadyate iti atas tām nirākartum sva rūpam ajahat eva tad viṣaya ākāram anukaroti iti darśana artham etat uktam svarūpam vā iti anubhava ākāram eva vā na viṣaya ākāram api jñāna jñānam api viṣaya jñānena aviśiṣṭam syāt iti jñāna jñānam viṣaya jñāna ālambana jñānam tad viṣaya jñānena aviśiṣṭam aviśeṣitam bhavet viṣaya anukāra anurakta viṣaya jñāna ākāra tvena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭam na utpāditam syāt iti arthaḥ yadi hi ālambanena ātmīya ākāra anugatam sva jñānam utpādyate iti etat asti tadā viṣaya jñānāt utpadyamānam jñānam yathā ukta ākāra viśiṣṭam syāt asati tu asmin yathā viṣayaḥ sva jñānam na viśeṣayati 
[I,78,ii^2]	svasā ārūpyeṇa viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭam na utpādayati tathā viṣaya jñānam api sva jñānam na viśeṣayeta viśeṣayati ca tasmāt viṣaya jñānasya api asti viṣaya ākāraḥ yat yat ākāram sva jñānena ālambyate tad ākāram tat bhavati tat yathā sa astra ādim adākāraḥ sva jñānena ālambyamānaḥ gauḥ sa astra ādim adākāraḥ viṣaya ākāram ca viṣaya jñānam sva jñānena ālambyate tad ākāraḥ ayam ālambyate iti asyāḥ vyavasthāyāḥ tad ākāra nibandhana tvāt tasyām sādhyāyam idam kāryam tad ākāra tve tu svabhāvaḥ viṣaya anubhava jñānam ca atra upalakṣaṇa mātram cintā jñānam api yathā cintita artha ākāram jñāna ākāram ca sva jñānena upalabhyate tathā hi yathā viṣaya jñāna jñānam viṣaya anubhava jñānasya ne kevalām artha rūpa tām vā pratyeti api tu īdṛś artham tat jñānam āsīt iti ubhaya ākāram gṛhṇāti tathā īdṛś artha ākārā cintā āsīt iti sva jñānena gṛhyate 
[I,80,i^1]	syāt etat nirākāram eva viṣaya jñānam utpadyate tasmin tu artha kārya tayā artha kāryam etat jñānam iti eṣā smṛtibhiḥ bhavati tasyām satyām anubhava jñāna hetuḥ api arthaḥ smaryate tatas paścāt bhrāntyā anubhava jñānam arthena saṃyojya artha ākāra tayā adhyavasyati na ca yāvatā bhrāntena pratipattrā tat tathā avasīyate tāvatā tad ākāram eva tat bhavati iti yuktam iti āha na ca uttarottarāṇi ityādi cakāraḥ avadhāraṇe uttarottarāṇi viṣaya jñāna jñāna ādīni tāni pūrvasya anubhava jñānasya yaḥ viṣayaḥ uttara uttara jñāna apekṣayā jñāna antarita tvāt viprakṛṣṭaḥ tad ābhāsāni na eva bhavanti na eva prāpnuvanti iti arthaḥ kutas tasya aviṣaya tvāt tasya yathā uktasya arthasya uttarottara jñānānām aviṣaya tvāt yadi sa teṣām api viṣayaḥ syāt tadā tad utpanneṣu teṣu artha kārya tayā artha kāryāṇi etāni jñānāni iti eṣā smṛtiḥ syāt tatas teṣām api hetuḥ saḥ arthaḥ smaryeta tatas ca tena arthena saṅkalayya tad pratibhāsi tvena bhrāntena pratipattrā gṛhyeran na ca asau teṣām viṣayaḥ 
[I,80,i^2]	kim tarhi ādyasya eva jñānasya tatas tat eva artha sāmarthya bhāvi saṃyojya arthena tad ākāratayā gṛhyeta na uttarottarāṇi teṣām tad aviṣaya tvāt gṛhyante ca tāni api artha ākāra anukāritayā tathā hi uttarottarasya jñāsya ekaikaḥ ākāraḥ adhikaḥ upalabhyate ghaṭa jñāna jñānena hi ghaṭa ākāram jñānam ālambamānaḥ saha ghaṭa ākāreṇa ghaṭa ākāram jñānam āsīt iti pratyeti tad jñānena tu ghaṭa jñāna jñānam ālambamānaḥ ghaṭa jñāna jñānam āsīt iti saha ghaṭa jñāna ākāreṇa ghaṭa jñāna jñānam evam uttareṣu api veditavyam tat evam uttara uttara jñānāni pūrva viprakṛṣṭa artha ākārāṇi gṛhyante na ca teṣām sva viṣayaḥ yatas tu aduktayā nītyā tathā gṛhyeran tasmāt tāni svabhāvataḥ eva tad ākārāṇi bhavanti iti abhyupeyam na ca ādyasya jñānasya viṣaya ākāra śūnya tve pūrva viprakṛṣṭa artha ābhāsāni bhavanti yathoktam prāk tasmāt tat api artha ābhāsam eṣṭavyam atas ca siddham dvairūpyam 
[I,81,i]	viṣaya jñāne tu yat jñānam tad viṣaya anurūpa jñāna ābhāsam su ābhāsam ca iti etat eva kutas yatas tad veśena viṣaya jñānasya viṣaya sārūpyam syāt iti ced yatas tat eva kutas yatas tad vaśena viṣaya jñāna sambandhinau tad dvāra āyātau viṣaya ākāra anubhava ākārau tṛtīyaḥ ca su a ābhāsa lakṣaṇaḥ ākāraḥ iti ete trayaḥ ākārāḥ sva jñānena ālambyante etat ca uttarottarasya jñānasya ekaikaḥ ākāraḥ adhikaḥ upalabhyate iti anena samprati eva ākhyātam tat kim iti vismaryate tasmāt tatra api viṣaya anurūpa jñāna ākāra tayā sādhye yat yat ākāram sva jñānena ālambyate ityādi sādhanam vijñeyam nanu evam tad jñāna ādiṣu api sādhanam vācyam iti anavasthā syāt na etat asti yasya hi jñānasya san nikṛṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ tatra sandehaḥ jāyate kim ayam nīla ākāraḥ viṣayasya jñānam tu nirākāram uta jñānasya iti yasya tu jñānasya viprakṛṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ tadānīm na asti iti niścitaḥ tasya viṣaya ākāra tām prati saṃśayaḥ na bhavati eva iti na anavasthā 
[I,82,i]	smṛteḥ uttara kālam ca ityādi pūrvam ekasya viṣaya sārūpyeṇa viśeṣeṇa dvairūpyam sādhitam idānīm jñānānām paraspara vivekena smṛteḥ sādhyate yathā hi paraspara vilakṣaṇeṣu rūpa ādiṣu anubhūteṣu anyonya vivekena smṛtiḥ bhavati tathā jñāneṣu api tasmāt asti dvi rūpa tā jñānasya anyathā anubhava mātreṇa pratyartham aviśiṣṭeṣu sarva jñāneṣu bhedenān anubhūteṣu rūpa jñānam āsīt mama na śabda jñānam iti śabda jñānam vā na rūpa jñānam iti yā iyam vivekena smṛtiḥ sā na syāt 
[I,83,i]	syāt etat yathā anubhava ātma tve tulye sāmagrī bhedāt subha ādi bhedaḥ bhavati tathā prativiṣayam apara apara sāmagrīkṛtaḥ bhedaḥ sūkṣmaḥ asti atas vivekena smṛtiḥ bhaviṣyati iti asat etat spaṣṭaḥ hi bhedaḥ smṛti nibandhanam tathā hi kasmiṃścid upekṣā sthānīye viṣaye yat jñānam dhārāvāhi tasya api apara apara indriya ādi sāmagrī tathā api na bhedena smaraṇam yatheyantaḥ buddhi kṣaṇāḥ vyatītāḥ iti yathā ca yama lakayoḥ ākāra sāmye api asti bhāvataḥ bhedaḥ tathā api aspaṣṭa tvāt tasya na bhedena pratyabhijñānam bhavati kim tarhi tayoḥ parasparam samāropaḥ tasmāt aspaṣṭa bhede arthe na vivekinī smṛtiḥ bhavati atas artha kṛtaḥ kaścid anubhava vasyā asti viśeṣaḥ yatas vivekena smṛtiḥ bhavati iti icchata artha sārūpyam eṣṭavyam tatas ca siddham dvi rūpam jñānam iti 
[I,83,ii]	sva saṃvedya tā ca iti anenān antara uktāyāḥ eva upapatteḥ sādhya antaram āha na kevalam smṛteḥ uttara kālam dvairūpyam siddham jñānasya api tu sva saṃvedanam api yat pramāṇa phala tvena iṣṭam asti tāvat jñānasya kṛtaścit anubhavaḥ atas smṛtiḥ api syāt tāvatā tu kutas sva saṃvedya tā iti matvā pṛcchati kim kāraṇam iti ātmanā eva jñānasya anubhavaḥ yuktaḥ na anyena iti niścitya āha na hi asau ityādi asya ayam arthaḥ yatra smṛtiḥ tatra anubhavaḥ rūpa ādi vat asti ca smṛtiḥ iti kāryam 
[I,84,i]	syāt etat ityādinā jñāna antareṇa anubhavaḥ abhīṣṭaḥ eva atas siddha sādhyatā iti para abhiprāyam āviṣkaroti jñāna antareṇa ityādinā siddha sādhyatām pariharati yena hi jñānena jñānam anubhūyate tatra api uttara kālam smṛtiḥ dṛṣṭā na ca anubhūte smṛtiḥ yuktā tatas anyena tad ālambanena jñānena bhāvyam tatra api ca smṛtiḥ tatas tatra api anyena iti atas jñāna antareṇa anubhave anavasthā jñānānām eka jñāna abhinirhṛtāyām eva jñāna paramparāyām uttarottarāṇi jñānāni pūrva pūrva jñāna ālambanāni anantāni prasajyante iti arthaḥ tathā sati kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ ityādi viṣaya antare jñānasya pravṛttiḥ na syāt iṣyate ca tatra yatas jñānāt sañcāraḥ tasya sva saṃvedanam syāt 
[I,85,i]	syāt etat mā bhūt antyasya jñānasya jñānasya jñāna antara saṃvedya tvam smṛtiḥ ca tat ekam ananubhūtam asmṛtam eva ca āstām atas viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ syāt iti ayuktam etat tathā hi yat antyam jñānam na anubhūyeta tatas sarvāṇi pūrva kāla bhāvīni jñānāni ananubhūtāni syuḥ tad upalambhasya parokṣa tvāt yasya yat upalambhaḥ parokṣaḥ na tat tena anubhūtam tat yathā devadattasya jñānam devadatta anubhūtam yajñadattena parokṣaḥ ca ātma sambandhi pūrva kāla bhāvi jñāna upalambhaḥ prāṇinaḥ viruddha vyāptaḥ atha vā yat apratyakṣa upalambham na tat pratyakṣam parokṣa vat tathā ca ananubhūta upalambham jñānam viruddha vyāptaḥ 
[I,85,ii]	syāt etat yat ātmanā anubhūtam jñānam tat eva pratyakṣam bhavati tena paraiḥ yat anubhūtam na tat pratyakṣam iti sa tarhi ātma anubhavaḥ kutas siddhaḥ yadi hi anubhavaḥ sidhyet tad ātmani paratra vā iti syāt vibhāgaḥ saḥ eva tu asiddhaḥ tasya asiddhau ubhayatra api parokṣa tvena aviśeṣāt ātmani ayam anubhavaḥ na anyatra iti etat parokṣa upalambhena durjñānam tat kutas ātma anubhavaḥ yadi hi grāhya upalambha asiddhau api vastu pratyakṣam iṣyate sarvam idam jagat pratyakṣam syāt apratyakṣa upalambha tvena aviśeṣāt na ca bhavati tasmāt sva saṃvedyātā jñānasya abhupeya iti 
[I,86,i_I,86,ii]	iha ācārya vasubandhoḥ vāda vidhiḥ iti loke pravādaḥ ayam tu sa astra kṛt tat kṛtānām śāstra antarāṇām nirdoṣa tām dṛṣṭvā sa doṣasya vāda vidheḥ tat praṇīta tām asambhāvayan āha na vāda vidhiḥ ācāryasya iti nanu ca adṛṣṭa kartṛkāṇām śāstrāṇām kartā pravādāt eva avasīyate sa ca iha api asti iti katham na vāda vidhiḥ ācāryasya iti āha asāraḥ vā iti niścayaḥ iti prakṛta tvāt ācāryasya tatra iti gamyate anena etam artham sūcayati na tāvat prasiddhi mātreṇa artha niścayaḥ bhavati artham antareṇa api tasya sambhavāt yadi api ca tena sa viracitaḥ tathā api prathamam anupajāta prajñā atiśayena satā paścāt vyavadāt abuddheḥ asya tatra āsāra niścayaḥ jātaḥ iti 
[I,86,iii]	katham punar etat avagamyate yathā tasya tatra āsāra niścayaḥ iti āha anyathā avayava prokteḥ iti nirdoṣa avayava abhidhānāt iti arthaḥ yat doṣa darśanāt ca ācāryeṇa vāda vidhau asāra niścayāt vāda vidhāne anyathā avayavāḥ proktāḥ te eva asmābhiḥ doṣāḥ prakāśyante iti darśayan āha tena ityādi tena iti doṣavat tvena 
[I,87,i_I,87,ii]	tathā hi anyathā avayava prokteḥ iti anena doṣavat tvam vāda vidheḥ sūcitam pramāṇa ādiṣu iti pramāṇa avayava tad ābhāsa jāti tad uttareṣu tatas arthāt vijñānam pratyakṣam iti yasya viṣayasya vijñānam vyapadiśyate yadi tatas eva tat utpadyate na anyatas na api tatas anyatas ca tat jñānam pratyakṣam tat yathā rūpa ādi jñānam sukha ādi jñānam iti etena bhrānti jñānam nirastam yathā śuktikāyām rajata jñānam tat dhi rajatena vyapadiśyate rajata jñānam iti na ca tat rajatāt utpadyate śuktikayā eva tu tat upajanyate saṃvṛti jñānam api anena apāstam tathā hi tad haṭa ādibhiḥ vyapadiśyate ghaṭa jñānam ghaṭa jñānam iti evam na tu tat tebhyaḥ bhavati teṣām saṃvṛti sattvena akāraṇa tvāt rūpa ādibhyaḥ eva hi tathā āsat niveṣṭebhyaḥ tat bhavati anumāna jñānam api anena eva nirastam dhūma jñāna sambandha smṛtibhyām api hi tat bhavati na agnitaḥ eva 
[I,87,iii_I,87,iv]	tatas bhavati eva na tu na bhavati iti ayam api atra arthaḥ abhimataḥ tat evam vyavasthitaḥ idam paryanuyujyate kim ayam pratyaya apekṣaḥ niyamaḥ āhoḥ vidālambana apekṣaḥ iti kim ca atas ubhayathā api doṣaḥ pūrvam niyamam tāvat adhikṛti āha tatas arthāt iti sarvaḥ ced iti yadi tatas iti ādyasya eva vivaraṇam nanu vijñāna vyapadeśa hetoḥ viṣayasya prakṛta tvāt tatas iti anena prakṛta pratyavam arśinā saḥ eva pratyavamṛśyate iti asaṃśayam etat tat kutas iyam āśaṅkā yadi tatas iti anena sarvaḥ caturvidhaḥ api pratyayaḥ ucyate iti nāya mātra arthaḥ yaḥ tvayā parikalpitaḥ yasmāt iha sarva dharma ātmaka tvāt ālambana pratyayaḥ eva sarva śabdena uktaḥ 
[I,88,i]	katham punar tasya sarva dharma ātmaka tvam ālambanam sarva dharmāḥ iti lakṣaṇāt na ca anyaḥ sarva dharma svabhāvaḥ vijñānasya pratyayaḥ vyapadeśa hetuḥ asti yaḥ tatas iti anena ucyate tasmāt ālambana pratyayaḥ eva sarva śabdena uktaḥ iti veditavyam tatas ca ayam arthaḥ bhavati yadi sarva dharma svabhāvaḥ pratyayaḥ ucyate yadi ālambana pratyayaḥ ucyate iti yāvat tena tat acodyam yasya ālambana pratyayasya sambandhi tayā jñānam vyapadiśyate na tat tat eva bhavati kim tarhi pratyaya antarāt api caturbhiḥ citta caittā hi iti vacanāt tat evam pratyaya niyama pakṣe siddhānta virodhaḥ udbhāvitaḥ 
[I,88,ii]	ālambana niyamam adhikṛtya āha ālambanam ced ityādi atra ati vyāpitā lakṣaṇasya uktā viṣaya mātram iti atra yā tadānīm san nihitaḥ rūpa ādi vyaktiḥ vijñānasya ālambana tvena sā viṣaya śabdena ucyate mātra śabdaḥ ālambana antaram vyavacchinatti smārta ādi jñānam api rūpa ādibhiḥ vyapadiśyate rūpa smṛtiḥ āmla abhilāṣaḥ agni anumānam iti ālambana antara nirapekṣam ca tatas tasya api pratyakṣatā syāt 
[I,89,i]	syāt etat anumeya viṣayam jñānam na agni mātrāt utpadyate api tu pakṣa dharma tva sambandha jñānāt api tat kutas ayam prasaṅgaḥ iti āha na hi agni ādi jñānam ityādi yadi api tad artha antarāt api jāyate tathā api na tad artha antaram tena ālambyate tatas ca ālambana antara anapekṣā utpatti tvāt kena tasya pratyakṣa tvam na syāt 
[I,89,ii]	nanu ca yena viṣayeṇa yat jñānam vyapadiśyate yadi tat tatas bhavati na tu na bhavati iti eṣaḥ api atra niyamaḥ abhimataḥ na ca smṛti ādīni yena ālambanena vyapadiśyante tasmāt utpadyante tasya asattvāt na etat asti pāramparyeṇa api tatas utpatteḥ abhimata tvāt anyathā katham idam yujyate yat uktam vāda vidhau anumāna jñānam api anena eva nirastam dhūma jñāna sambandha smṛtibhyām api śabdāt agnitaḥ api tat bhavati iti uktam bhavati tat etat katham yujyate yadi vyapadeśa hetoḥ pāramparyeṇa api atra janaka tvam abhimatam anyathā yadi smṛti ādīnām viṣayasya vyapadeśa hetoḥ tadānīm asattvāt ajanaka tvam tat idam anumānaḥ api ajanaka tvam samānam iti idam vacanam ayujyamānam syāt 
[I,90,i]	atha smṛti ādīnām kalpitam sāmānyam viṣayaḥ vyapadeśa hetuḥ tat ca saṃvṛti sattvāt ajanakam tatas na teṣām pratyakṣata iti matam atra api etat eva uttaram tathā hi anumānasya api saṃvṛti sat eva ālambanam tatas ca tat ayuktam syāt yat uktam dhūma jñāna sambandha smṛtibhyām api hi tat bhavati na agnitaḥ eva iti tasmāt sthitaḥ eva ati vyāpitā doṣaḥ 
[I,90,ii^1]	iha dvaye vādinaḥ antar jñeya vādinaḥ bāhya artha vādinaḥ ca tatra antar jñeya vādinām adṛṣṭa tatva avasthāyām pramāṇam prameyam ca apariniṣpannam eva tattvataḥ kevalam bhrāntānām yathādarśanam idam māna meya vyavasthiti darśanam etat ca prāk eva pratipāditam bāhya artha vādinaḥ tu paramārthataḥ eva bāhyam prameyam tat viṣayam ca pramāṇam icchati tat ca yathā na yujyate tathā pratipādayitum idānīm ālambana adhikāreṇa vicāram ārabdhum āha rūpa ādiṣu tu ālambana arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam ye hi manyante 
[I,90,ii^2]	vāda vidhi dūṣaṇa paraḥ eva ayam ārabhyaḥ iti teṣām yat uktam sva saṃvedyam tu anirdeśyam rūpam indriya gocaraḥ iti atra gocara arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ kim yadābhāsam tatra jñānam utpadyate tathā tad gocaraḥ ityādi tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ iti pratividheyam tasmāt sāmānyena eva bāhya artha āśrayiṇī pramāṇāt vyavasthā na ghaṭataḥ iti pratipādana paraḥ ayam ārabhyaḥ iti veditavyam tatra api bāhya artha vādiṣu balinaḥ sva yūthyāḥ teṣu nihateṣu atare nihatāḥ eva bhavanti jyeṣṭha mallaḥ iva hinate tad anye mallāḥ iti taiḥ eva saha vicāram karoti 
[I,91,i]	ālambana arthaḥ iti ālambana śabdasya arthaḥ kim yadābhāsam iti anena pratyekam rūpa ādi paramāṇūnām sva rūpeṇa apratibhāsanāt samūha ākāreṇa ca teṣu vijñānasya pratibhāsanāt ābhāsā artham ālambana artham darśayati atha yathā ityādinā kāraṇa artham yathā vidyamānāḥ iti nīla ādi svalakṣaṇena anya ābhāsasya api iti samūha ābhāsasya api yadi api su ābhāsam vijñānam na janayati tathā api iti api śabdasya arthaḥ 
[I,91,ii]	sañcita ālambana tvāt iti samūha ālambana tvāt sañcitam sañcayaḥ iti kṛtvā sañcayaḥ ca samūhaḥ sañcita ālambana tvam tu teṣām samūha pratibhāsa tvāt atha vā sañcita tva ālambana tvāt iti samūha ābhāsa tvāt iti arthaḥ ālambyate anena iti karaṇam kārakam kṛtvā ābhāsaḥ ālambana śabdena uktaḥ saṃvṛti sat eva ālambanam iti apratyakṣata iti śeṣaḥ saṃvṛti sat ālambana tvam tu samūhasya adravya sattvāt anena yat saṃvṛti sat ālambanam na tat pratyakṣam smṛti ādi vat tathā ca indriya jñānam iti vyāpaka viruddham prasaṅgam āha 
[I,92,i]	nanu dravya satām eva sa paramāṇūnām ākāraḥ te eva hi paraspara anugṛhītāḥ tathā pratibhāsantaḥ iti aneka ākāra artha vādinaḥ kadācid asiddha tām udbhāvayeyuḥ iti āśāṅkya āha kāmam ityādi kāmam iti abhyupagame nīla ādi ābhāseṣu vijñāneṣu tatas arthāt iti atas lakṣaṇāt pratyakṣatā syāt tvad matena kutas iti āha tathā hi ityādi teṣu iti nīla ādi ābhāseṣu vijñāneṣu tad samudāye prajñaptisatyā api iti nīla ādi paramāṇu samudāye sa hi yadi api prajñaptisan tathā api nīla pīta ādi jñāneṣu dravya sadākāraḥ labhyate tvat abhimatayā yuktyā atha vā teṣu iti nīla ādi paramāṇuṣu dravya sadākāraḥ labhyate 
[I,92,ii_I,92,iii]	dravya saṅkhyā ādi ākāreṣu api tu prāpnoti iti yadi paramāṇu ākāra tvāt samūha ākārasya parama artha sattvam dravya saṅkhyā ādīnām api paramāṇu ākāra tvāt parama artha sattvam syāt tatas ca tad ākāra vijñānam pratyakṣam syāt tatra api śakyataḥ iyam yuktiḥ vaktum yat āha te eva hi ityādi atha yathā ityādi pakṣa antara upanyāsaḥ evam sati ityādi dravya ādiṣu yat jñānam tasya pratyakṣatāyāḥ aprasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ kutas iti āha tathā teṣām ityādi tathā iti ghaṭa ādi rūpeṇa teṣām iti dravya ādīnām na hi nīla ādi paramāṇu vat tattvataḥ santi taiḥ ca jñānam vyapadiśyate ghaṭa jñānam dvi tva jñānam iti na ca tatas tat utpadyate teṣām tattvataḥ asattvāt atas na tat jñānasya pratyakṣatā prasaṅgaḥ saṃvṛti sat ālambana tvam api asiddham na hi svarūpeṇa paramāṇūnām ālambanatvaḥ indriya jñānasya saṃvṛti sat ālambanam bhavati 
[I,93,i]	kaḥ tarhi doṣaḥ iti āha evam tu ityādi na hi ityādinā atra eva upapattim āha yadi pratyekam paramāṇuṣu jñānam syāt evam sati ekaikena paramāṇunā tat vyapadiśyeta tatas ca pratyekam ca te jñānasya kāraṇam pratyekam ca taiḥ tat vyapadiśyate iti tad ālambanasya jñānasya pratyakṣa tvam labhyeta na ca evam tasmāt yasya tat vyapadiśyate iti etat na prāpnoti 
[I,93,ii]	atha matam samudāya ābhāsa tvāt tasya vyapadiśyate paramāṇavaḥ ca samudāya avasthāḥ eva paraspara anugṛhītāḥ hetavaḥ jñānasya tatas yasya tat vyapadiśyate tatas eva utpadyate iti siddhā pratyakṣatā nīla ādi jñānānām iti āha pratyekam ca ityādi samudāya avasthāyām api ekaikasya eva kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na samudāyasya iti arthaḥ tatas saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ yasya tat vyapadiśyate iti etat na prāpnoti iti 
[I,94,i]	yadābhāsam na tat tasmāt iti samūha ābhāsam kasmāt na syāt iti āha citā laṃbanam hi pañcakam iti samūha ābhāsam iti arthaḥ karaṇam kārakam kṛtvā ābhāsaḥ ālamba śabdena uktaḥ yatas tat parama arthena iti paramāṇoḥ na tasya vyapadiśyate iti atat ābhāsa tvena tasya anavadhāri tvāt 
[I,94,ii_I,94,iii]	artha rūpa viviktam ityādi sarvasya hi jñānasya viṣayeṇa vyapadeśaḥ dṛśyate rūpa jñānam śabda jñānam iti viṣaya rūpa vyatirekeṇa tu aśakyam tat vyapadeṣṭum nanu ca jñānam buddhiḥ iti vinā api viṣayeṇa vyapadeśaḥ dṛśyate na abhiprāya aparijñānāt kaḥ punar atra abhiprāyaḥ viṣayasya sambandhi tayā artha rūpa viviktam na śakyam ākhyātum iti ayam abhiprāyaḥ tathā hi yasya arthasya yat jñānam vyapadiśyate yadi tatas eva tat bhavati iti etat viṣaya cintā prakṛtam eva anyathā jñānam iti vyapadiśan eva katham evam brūyāt evam tarhi viṣaya rūpeṇa vyapadeśaḥ asya bhaviṣyati āha viṣayaḥ asya ca iti sāmānya rūpeṇa rūpa tva ādinā vyapadiśyeta sāmānyam ca kalpitam buddhi ārūḍham eva na indriya viṣaya abhimate asti tat katham tatra vyapadiṣṭe tat vyapadiṣṭam bhavati atas yena vyapadiśyate iti etat na sambhavati iti darśayan na āha tasmāt na vyapadiśyate iti 
[I,95,i^1]	nanu ca avyapadeśyam api vastu dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya adhya vasita tat bhāvatayā vyavahartṛbhiḥ vyapadiśyate tvayā api avaśyam etat abhyupeyam anyathā vyavahāra ayogāt syāt etat evam yadi bāhyam kiñcid dṛśyam syāt tat ca na asti ālambana lakṣaṇa yogāt iti aparihāraḥ eva ayam nanu ca ayam uktaḥ eva arthaḥ tat kim artham punar ucyate asti prayojanam pūrvam hi paramāṇūnām paramāṇu rūpam eva sarva sūkṣmam adhikṛtya ucyate prāk teṣām eva dravya satām tad rūpam iti aneka ākāra artha vādinaḥ matam āśaṅkya tasya dṛśyatām abhidheya tām ca abhyupetya doṣa antara abhidhitsayā pratyakṣatā anujñātā samprati sati api tasmin tasya api adṛśya tvena anabhidheya tvāt kutas pratyakṣata iti pratipādanāya idam ucyate katham punar tasya api adṛśya tvam evam manyate 
[I,95,i^2]	sarvathā vā su a ākāra vijñāna janaka tvam grāhya tvam syāt kenacid vā ākāreṇa yadi prathama vikalpaḥ jñānasya sarvathā artha svabhāvatā āpatteḥ ajñāna tva prasaṅgaḥ atha dvitīyaḥ samanantara atītam jñānam anya viṣayasya api jñānasya grāhyam syāt yatas tasya api jñāna tva ādinā kenacid ākāreṇa sva ābhāsa jñāna jananam asti eva iti tasmāt ayuktam grāhya lakṣaṇam atas ca sthitam etat na bāhya artha āśrayā pramāṇa ādi vyavasthā yujyate iti 
[I,96,i_I,96,iii^1]	naiyāyikānām tu iti rūḍheḥ anantaram ca tad matasya upakṣepāt ākṣapādānām iti gamyate indriya artha san nikarṣa utpannam ityādi indriyāṇi ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi arthāḥ pañca gandha ādayaḥ tad āśrayāḥ karma sattādāyaḥ ca teṣām sannikarṣaḥ sanmandhaḥ sa tu pañca vidhiḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samaveta samavāyāḥ ca tatra indriyasya dravyeṇa saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ san bandhaḥ na rūpa ādibhiḥ anyathā ubhaya āśraya tvāt saṃyogasya te api guṇavantaḥ syuḥ nirguṇaḥ ca guṇāḥ tasmāt indriya saṃyogāt dravye jñānam utpadyate yadātmā manasā saṃyujyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam arthena dravya mātra arhe abhipretaḥ dravya samaveteṣu tu rūpa ādiṣu guṇeṣu tathā dravya tva ādiṣu sāmānya viśeṣeṣu karmaṇi ca saṃyukta samavāyāt rūpa tva ādiṣu saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt tathā guṇa tva karma tvayoḥ śabde tu samavāyāt sa hi śravaṇa śaṣkulī paricchina dharma abhisaṃskṛta ākāśa deśa lakṣaṇe śretra indriye samavetaḥ gṛhyate yaḥ tu śrotra ādi vicchin deśaḥ utpadyate 
[I,96,iii^2]	sa tatra asamaveta tvāt na gṛhyante eva tena tu śabda antarāṇi sarva dikkāni ārabhyante taiḥ api anyāni evam śabda antara ārabdha śabda paramparayā śrotra indriye yaḥ samavaiti śabdaḥ tasya indriya samavāyāt grahaṇam bhavati yadātmā manasā saṃyujyate manaḥ api śrotreṇa śabda jātau tu samaveta samavāyāt sattāyām tu dravya samavetāyām saṃyukta samavāyāt guṇa karma samavetāyām saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt śabda samavetāyām tu samaveta samavāyāt iti tat evam pañca prakāraḥ sambandhaḥ jñāna hetuḥ 
[I,97,i_I,98,i]	tasmāt utpannam na abhi vyaktam jñānam pratyakṣam jñāna grahaṇam sukha ādi vyavaccheda artham vyapadiśyate jñāpyate saṃyogi ādinā liṅgena iti vyapadeśyaḥ viṣayaḥ na asya vyapadeśyaḥ viṣayaḥ asti iti avyapadeśyam atha vā tat eva jñānam sva rūpeṇa na vyapadiśyate na nirdiśyate iti avyapadeśyam mṛgatṛṣṇā ādiḥ viṣayaḥ vyabhicārī yathā jala ādi rūpa tvena gṛhyate tathā asattvāt na asya vyabhicārī asti iti avyabhicāri atha vā tat eva jñānamat asmin tad grahāt vyabhicāri 
[I,98,ii_I,98,iv]	vyavasāya ātmā asya iti vyavasāya ātmakam ātma śabdaḥ svabhāva vacanaḥ kārya vacanaḥ vā indriya artha udbhavaḥ iti udbhavati asmāt iti udbhavaḥ indriya arthau udbhavaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ indriya artha grahaṇam tat sannikarṣa upalakṣana artham na asti vyapadeśya ādi sambhavaḥ iti ādi grahaṇāt vyabhicāri tvasya vyavasāya ātmaka tvasya ca yadi na asti kim iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam iti āha viśeṣaṇa artham na asti vyapadeśya ādi sambhavaḥ iti ādi grahaṇāt vyabhicāri tvasya vyavasāya ātmaka tvasya ca 
[I,98,v]	yadi na asti kim iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam iti āha viśeṣaṇam hi ityādi yadi avyapadeśya ādi svabhāvam itara svabhāvam ca indriya sannikarṣa jam jñānam syāt tatas idam viśeṣaṇa trayam yujyate iha ca avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri iti ca viśeṣaṇa dvayam sambhavati eva na vyabhiccarati vyavasāya ātmaka tvam tu na sambhavati eva tat eva ca viśeṣaṇam bhavati yat tasmin āśraye bhavati tam ca vyabhicarati tatra asattvāt yathā nīlatvam itpalasya 
[I,98,vi]	na ca asti indriya budddheḥ iti yadā bahu vrīhi pakṣaḥ tat evam uktam anena vyapadeśya tvasya asambhavena avyapadeśya tvasya avyabhicāram darśayati kasmāt na asti iti āha anumāna viṣaya tvāt ityādi vyapadeśyam hi sāmānyam na sva lakṣaṇam tasya pūrvam adṛṣṭa tvāt tat ca sāmānyam anumānasya eva viṣayaḥ dhūma ādibhiḥ pūrva dṛṣṭa sāmānyena agni ādi anumānāt na pratyakṣasya tasya asādhāraṇa viṣaya tvāt 
[I,99,i]	atha api syāt yadi viṣayaḥ na vyapadiśyate na nāma jñānam tu vyapadiśyate tat asti vyapadeśyam tatas ca vyabhicārāt yuktam avyapadeśya tvam viśeṣaṇam iha ca tat eva jñānam svarūpeṇa yat na nirdiśyate tat avyapadeśyam uktam iti āha anirdeśya tve ca avyabhicāraḥ iti kasmāt iti āha na hi indriya buddhiḥ ityādi anirdeśya svarūpam eva hi sarvam jñānam na eva anirdeśya tve vyabhicāraḥ asti atha sāmānya rūpeṇa api yat na nirdiśyate tat avyapadeśyam evam api asambhavaḥ syāt sarvam eva hi jñānam sāmānya rūpeṇa vyapadiśyate tat anena tat puruṣa pakṣe api doṣaḥ uktaḥ 
[I,99,ii]	pakṣilaḥ tu āha jñānasya samākhyā śabdaḥ na asti yena pratīyamānam vyavahārāya kalpate anyatra iti karaṇa yuktāt viṣaya saṃśabdanāt rūpam iti jñānam rasaḥ iti jñānam iti tadā ca vyapadiśyamānam śābdam bhavati tatas vyavaccheda artham avyapadeśyam iti āha artha grahaṇa kāle tu samākhyā śabdaḥ na vyāpriyate tadā tasya avyapadeśya tvam iti tasya api etat eva uttaram anirdeśya tve ca avyabhicāraḥ iti vyavahāra kāle api jñāna svarūpasya vyapadeṣṭum aśakya tvāt saḥ api hi tāvat viṣayaḥ sva rūpeṇa vyapadeṣṭum aśakyaḥ kutas punar tena anyaḥ vyapadekṣyate na ca vyapadeśa acchābda tvam prasajyate kim tarhi vācya tvam iti asamīkṣita abhidhānam etat 
[I,100,i]	na ca vyabhicāri viṣaya tve sambhavaḥ asti iti anuvartate manaḥ bhrānti viṣaya tvāt ityādi vyabhicāraḥ atathā bhāvaḥ yathā asau upalabhyate tathā tasya asattvam yathā marīcika ādeḥ viṣayasya sa ca yatra jñāne sva rūpeṇa pratibhāsate tat apekṣayā vyabhicāri tvam bhrānte ca manaḥ vijñāne sa tathā pratibhāsate tathā hi anudaka ādi svabhāvam api bhūta saṅghātam udaka ādi rūpeṇa adhyavasyanti upajāyate manaḥ bhrāntiḥ tatas tat kalpita tvāt tasyāḥ eva sa viṣayaḥ na indriya jñānasya tatas na tad vyavaccheda artham avyabhicāri grahaṇam kartavyam 
[I,100,ii_I,101,i]	nanu asati tasmin akṣa upaghāta jam yat vyabhicāri viṣayam dvi candra ādi jñānam tasya api pratyakṣatā syāt tatas tat nirāsāya tat avaśyam kartavyam na etat asti artha sannikarṣa grahaṇena eva tasya pratipakṣepāt anyathā indriya jam iti evam vācyam syāt na tu indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti tasya vyavacchedya abhāvāt idam bahuvrīhim ahikṛtya uktam yadā tu tat eva jñānam svayam avyabhicāri iti tat puruṣaḥ paraiḥ ākṣīyate tadā evam vaktavyam avyabhicāri tvāt dvi candra ādi jñānam tu sannikarṣaḥ diś mātra darśanena eva pūrva anusāreṇa gamyate iti kṛtvā 
[I,101,ii]	vyavasāyaḥ api hi ityādinā viśeṣaṇasya asambhavam āha no vikalpya iti niścayaḥ hi evaṃrūpaḥ gauḥ eva ayam na aśvaḥ iti sa ca yāvat go tva ādi sāmānyam na vikalpayati tena ca tadvantam na yojayati tāvat na upajāyate eva na ca ghrāṇa ādi jñāna vat iti asambhavaḥ viśeṣaṇasya nirvikalpayan api cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate na ca vikalpa dvayam yugapad abhyupeyate saṃvedyate vā iti kutas asiddhiḥ 
[I,101,iii]	atha ityādi ayathārtham jñānam mithyājñānam ādi śabdena saṃśaya jñānam gṛhyate tasya ayatha artha ādi jñānasya nivṛttasya vyavasāya ātmakam iti ucyate etat darśayati na atra vyavasāya śabdaḥ niścaya paryāyaḥ kim tarhi bhūta artha grahaṇa paryāyaḥ vyavasāya ātmakam iti bhūta artha grahaṇa svabhāvam iti arthaḥ kasmāt ayuktam viśeṣaṇam iti āha avyabhicārāt ca iti caśabdāt asambhavāt ca indriya buddhau ayathārtha tvasya kutas punar asambhavaḥ iti āha sarvā hi ityādi mātra śabdaḥ ayathārtha grahaṇa nirāsa arthaḥ sva artha grahaṇa mātreṇa asambhavam darśayati ayathārtha tvam hi yat nivartayitum iṣyate tat indriya jñāne na sambhavati eva indriya buddhiḥ iti ca yadi api sāmānya śabdaḥ tathā api prakaraṇāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannāyām eva vartate 
[I,102,i]	avyabhicārāt iti anena etat darśayati yadi api mūḍhaḥ sambhavaḥ manyate tathā api tat pūrvam eva nirākṛtam avyabhicāri iti anena viśeṣaṇena tat kim etena vyavasāya ātmaka vacanena iti atha vā na kevalam asambhavān na yuktam kim tu avyabhicārāt ca tam avyabhicāram darśayati sarvāḥ hi ityādinā kvacid caśabdaḥ na paṭhyate tatra arthaḥ katham tathā api ayuktam viśeṣaṇam iti āha avyabhicārāt iti indriya buddheḥ yathārtha tvasya avyabhicārāt iti arthaḥ katham avyabhicāraḥ iti āha sarvāḥ hīyādi 
[I,102,ii]	nanu ca vyavasāya ātmakam iti atra kārya paryāyaḥ ātma śabdaḥ tatas ca yathā ukta doṣa abhāvaḥ iti āha etena ityādi prayuktaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ vyavasāya kāryam iti vyavasāyaḥ kāryam asya iti vigrahaḥ katham prayuktam iti āha na hi asti ityādi indriya buddhi antaram hi sāmānya ākāreṇa arthaḥ buddhau sanniviśate tathā tatra asat niviṣṭasya nāma jāti ādi yojanā na sambhavati tat antaram kim etat iti abhyūha vikalpaḥ tatas pūrva anubhūta anusāreṇa anusmaraṇa vikalpaḥ tad anantaram nirūpaṇa vikalpaḥ niścaya ātmakaḥ bhavati tat yadi vyavasāyaḥ kāryam yasya tat jñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iṣyate evam sati pūrva anubhūta smaraṇa antaram niścaya jñānam bhavati iti anusmaraṇa jñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa jam prāpnoti sākṣāt grahaṇam viprakṛṣṭa ayatha artha jñāna kāryasya vyavacchedya tve pratyakṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt 
[I,103,i]	tat anena prapañcana yasya yatra vyabhicāraḥ sambhavaḥ ca na asti na tat tasya viśeṣaṇam tat yathā balākāyāḥ śukla tvam kṛṣṇa tvam ca na asti ca avyapadeśya tva ādeḥ indriya jñāne yathāyogyam vyabhicāraḥ sambhavaḥ ca iti vyāpaka abhāvam darśayati kaḥ punar ayam vyabhicāraḥ nāma yadi tatas anyatra bhāvaḥ evam sati nīla tvam bhramarasya niśeṣam syāt avyapadeśya tvam ca jñānasya dāha duḥkha ādau api bhāvāt atha tatra abhāvaḥ evam api prayatna ānantarīyake tat na asti yatas vyabhicāraḥ sādhyasya syāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvam eva tu kvacid anitye na asti iti tasya eva syāt vyabhicāraḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ anekadhā hi vyabhicāra śabdasya arthaḥ kvacid anyathā bhāvaḥ vyabhicārī viṣayaḥ iti kvacid anyatra bhāvaḥ vyabhicārī hetuḥ iti kvacid tatra abhāvaḥ vyabhicāri viśeṣaṇam iti ādikaḥ iha tu tatra abhāvaḥ abhimataḥ 
[I,104,i]	atha api ityādi anena etat darśayati na aniṣṭa nivṛttaye avyapadeśya ādi grahaṇam kim tu pramāṇa ādīnām svabhāva parijñānāt niḥśreyasa prāptiḥ atas tat svabhāva pradarśanāya tasmāt siddha sādhanam iti tat na ityādinā etat āha pratyakṣa lakṣaṇe vivakṣite kaḥ avasaraḥ jñāna svabhāva pradarśanasya iti tatra etat syāt tat eva pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam na śakyate vaktum vinā tad svabhāva pradarśanena iti āha tasya ca ityādi lakṣaṇam hi nāma yat artha antara vyāvṛttena rūpeṇa lakṣyam gamayati tat ca lakṣyam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti anena eva siddham iti vṛkṣā svabhāva kathanam anena hetuḥ āviṣkṛtaḥ atha niṣprayojanasya api nirdeśaḥ kriyate evam sati atiprasaṅgaḥ iti darśayan āha jñāna svabhāva nirdeśya tve ca ityādi anena dṛṣṭāntaḥ yasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam pratyupayogaḥ na asti na tat tat adhikāre nirdeśyam guṇa tva ādi vat na asti ca pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam pratyupayogaḥ avyapadeśya tva ādeḥ vyāpaka abhāvaḥ 
[I,104,ii_I,105,i]	yaḥ tu manyate na eva indriya artha sannikarṣa jasya pratyakṣasya avyapadeśya tva ādi viśeṣaṇam kim tarhi pratyakṣa dvayam eva etat paraspara asaṅkīrṇa rūpam ekena sūtreṇa lakṣyate avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam iti anena hi sūtra eka deśena mānasam lakṣyate indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti anena tu indriya artha sannikarṣa jam tatas ca indriya artha udbhave na asti ityādi yat uktam tat sūtra artha aparijñāna vijṛmbhitam atas eva saḥ api adoṣaḥ na sukha ādi prameyam vā iti yaḥ uktaḥ anantaraḥ api hetuḥ asiddhaḥ iti tena manasaḥ indriya tvam vaktavyam pratyakṣa vyapadeśa prasiddhi artham kim ca avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam iti etāvat lakṣaṇam astu anena eva pūrvasya api pratyakṣaṇa vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,105,ii]	sarvatra ca ityādinā lakṣaṇasya avyāpitām āha yatas cakṣuḥ śrotra vijñānayoḥ api pratyakṣateṣṭā tayoḥ ca sannikarṣa utpattyi asambhavaḥ tam asambhavam darśayan āha sa antara grahaṇam ityādi sa antara grahaṇam vicchinnaḥ iti grahaṇam adhika grahaṇam indriya atirikta grahaṇam tat na syāt kutas iti āha na hi ityādi etena yat indriyeṇa nirantaram na tat indriyāt sa antaram iti gṛhyate na api adhikam iti gandha ādi vat tathā ca rūpa śadau iti viruddha vyāptam prasaṅgam āha asti ca tat tathāvidham grahaṇam tathā hi indriya parimāṇa atirikta svarūpāḥ vicchinnāḥ iti ca śaila ādayaḥ śabdāḥ ca gṛhyante iti prasiddham etat prāpti grahaṇe tu sati yāvatā bhāgena prāptiḥ tāvatā iva grahaṇam syāt avicchinnāḥ iti gṛhyeran rūpa grahaṇam ca atra cakṣuḥ viṣaya upalakṣaṇa artham yaḥ yatas sāntaraḥ iti gṛhyate na tasya tena saha nairantaryam tat yathā pārasya apareṇa sva grāhakāt indriyāt sa antarau iti ca gṛhyete rūpa śabdau iti prasaṅga viparyayeṇa vyāpaka viruddha dvayam etat iti śabda upānānam asiddha tā parihārāya 
[I,106,i]	nanu ca indriyam atīndriyam tat katham tat apekṣayā kiñcid sāntaram iti gṛhyeta adhikam iti vā na ca rūpa ādīnām parimāṇam asti nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām tat kutas teṣām ādhikya grahaṇam na ca paraḥ gandha ādibhiḥ saha indriyasya nairantaryam icchati taiḥ tasya saṃyoga abhāvāt tat katham idam yuktam na hi indriya nirantare gandha ādau ityādi yatra dravye gandha ādayaḥ samavetāḥ tat dravyam atra indriya nirantaram jñeyam tena saha indriyasya saṃyogāt tat dvāreṇa ca gandha dīnām api nairantaryam asti ca saṃyukta samavāya lakṣaṇam iti adoṣaḥ 
[I,107,i]	yat tu uktam nanu ca indriyam atīndriyam ityādi tatra yadi indriya apekṣayā na tathā rūpa śabdau gṛhyete kim apekṣayā tarhi vaktavyam adhiṣṭhāna apekṣayā iti ced evam tarhi yadi rūpa śabdau adhiṣṭhānāt vicchinnau iti adhikau iti ca gṛhyete tad abahis vartinaḥ indriyāt api tau tathā eva gṛhyete yaḥ yatas vicchinnaḥ iti adhikaḥ iti ca gṛhyate sa tad abahis vartinaḥ api vastunaḥ tathā eva gṛhyate tat yathā ghaṭāt vicchinnaḥ iti adhikaḥ iti ca gṛhyamāṇaḥ parvataḥ ghaṭābahis vartinaḥ api udaka ādeḥ tathā eva gṛhyate indriya adhiṣṭhānāt vicchinnau iti adhikau iti ca gṛhyete vivāda āspadībhūtau rūpa śabdau svabhāvaḥ 
[I,107,ii]	yat api uktam na ca rūpa ādīnām ityādi tatra yadi rūpa ādīnām parimāṇam na asti katham tarhi alpam rūpam mahat rūpam iti gṛhyate upacārāt iti ced syāt etat rūpa ādayaḥ yatra samavetāḥ tat dravyam aṇu mahat vā tad dvāreṇa rūpa ādeḥ ādhikya ādi aupacārikam iti astu yathā tathā tena tu bhāktena api gandha ādi vat rūpa ādeḥ api adhikam iti grahaṇam na prāpnoti iti etāvat ucyate api ca tulya pratyaya paricchedya tvāt aupacārika tvam eva ayuktam yādṛśaḥ hi dravye mahat dravyam alpam vā iti pratyayaḥ tad aviśiṣṭaḥ rūpa ādiṣu mahat rūpam alpam vā iti na ca mukhya upacaritayoḥ tulya pratyaya paricchedya tvam na hi yādṛśena pratyayena mukhyaḥ gauḥ paricchidyate tādṛśena eva upacāritaḥ vāhīkaḥ yadi vā āśraya dvāreṇa guṇāḥ guṇavantaḥ pratīyante sarvaḥ śabdaḥ mahān iti eva pratīyate tad āśrayasya nabhasaḥ mahā parimāṇa tvāt tatas ca hasti maśaka ādi śabdānām parimāṇa bheda pratītiḥ na syāt tasmāt ca te api guṇavantaḥ abhyupeyāḥ na vā dravyam api iti 
[I,108,i]	bahis vṛtti tvāt ityādinā hetvoḥ asiddham āha tathā hi adhiṣṭhānābahis vṛtti tvam āśritya sa antara adhika grahaṇayoḥ hetvoḥ siddhiḥ abhisaṃhitā bahis vṛtti tve tu sā na upapadyate yasmāt indriyam bahis nirgatya visargatya visarpat viṣayeṇa saṃyuktam tam adhiṣṭhānāt adhikam avabhāsayati pradīpa āloka vat tasmāt upapadyate tad viṣayasya sa antara adhika grahaṇam adhiṣṭhānāt na indriyāt iti bhāvaḥ 
[I,108,ii]	atra codyate cakṣuṣaḥ taijasa tvāt raśmayaḥ nirgatya artham prakāśayanti iti abhyupagamāt uktam bahis vṛtti tvam āśaṅkitum śrotram tu śravaṇa śaṣkulī paricchinnaḥ ākāśa pradeśa viśeṣaḥ tasya na eva paraḥ bahis vṛtti tvam icchati tat katham tasya tad āśaṅkitam iti evam manyate pradeśa vat tvam ākāśasya bhāktam paramārthataḥ tu tat niravayavam eva yathā uktayā nītyā bhākta pakṣe yat abahis vṛtti tvam tatra doṣaḥ ukte agatyā parama artha pakṣa samāśrayeṇa bahis vṛtti tvam kadācid paraḥ kalapayet iti tasmāt yuktam āśaṅkitum tatra cikitsā ādi prayogāt iti upapattiḥ 
[I,109,i]	nanu pāda abhyaṅga ādiḥ adhiṣṭhānāt anyatra api cakṣuḥ ādeḥ kriyate tatas na ayam ekāntaḥ yatra cikitsā prayogaḥ tatra indriyam iti na etat asti tatra api dhātrī cikitsā dvāreṇa kumārakasya iva cakṣuḥ ādeḥ adhiṣṭhāna sthasya eva naḍī sañcāreṇa cikitsā prayogāt anyathā tatra asat nihitam tena sambandhaman anubhavat katham cikitsyeta atha cikitsā kāle pāda ādau sannihitam evam sati pāda āde rūpa grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt svādhiṣṭhāna stham eva yathā uktena prakāreṇa cikitsyate iti abhyupeyam tat etat uktam bhavati yat indriyam svādhiṣṭhāne cikitsyate tat tatra eva vartate ghrāṇa ādi vat svādhiṣṭhāne ca cikitsi ete cakṣuḥ śrotre iti svabhāvaḥ 
[I,109,ii_I,110,i]	atas indriyāt eva iti nipātaḥ bhinnakramaḥ vicchinnaḥ eva iti evam drṣṭavyam kim kāraṇam yatas adhiṣṭhānāt api vicchinne arthaḥ iti gṛhyate na kevalam indriyāt adhiṣṭhāna dvāreṇa eva hi indriyāt arthasya sa antara grahaṇam pratīyate yathā uktam prāk doṣa antaram vaktu kāmaḥ bahis nirgatim abhyupeti āha sati api ca ityādi anyathā ityādinā bahis nirgatasya viṣaya upalambha asāmarthye hetum āha yasya indriyasya adhiṣṭhāna pidhāne viṣaya grahaṇam na asti tasya bahis nirgatasya apratibaddham viṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyam na asti tvac ādi indriya vat na asti ca sva adhiṣṭhāna pidhāne cakṣuḥ śrotrayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇam kāya abhāvaḥ 
[I,110,ii^1]	nanu cakṣuṣaḥ prabhāva lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ adhiṣṭhāna pidhāne vinaśyati adhiṣṭhāna pidhāna kāle tatra eva āśu praviśati vā tatas ayam adoṣaḥ apihita adhiṣṭhānam eva hi tad viṣaya grahaṇa samartham na anyathā iti śrotra indriyam prati tāvat ayam asamādhiḥ tasya adhiṣṭhāna pidhāne api bahis vṛtti tvāt nitya tvāt ca cakṣuḥ prati yadi nāma ayam parihāraḥ iti pratyāśā syāt sā api tyajyatām yatas cakṣuṣaḥ ātma bhūtaḥ prabhāva yavī nirgatya sarva ātmanā viṣayeṇa samprayukta tvāt tatra eva sannihitaḥ na adhiṣṭhāne tat avyatirikta tvāt cakṣuḥ api na hi tasya avayavāḥ santi 
[I,110,ii^2]	yatas bhāgena adhiṣṭhāne api varteta tatas ca tadānīm tad adhiṣṭhāna abhimataḥ śarīra avayavaḥ tasya adhiṣṭhānam na bhavati eva asambandhāt indriya antara vat iti prasaṅgaḥ vā atha sāvayavaḥ prabhāva yavī kalpyate evam api yaḥ tasya pradeśaḥ viṣayeṇa samprayuktaḥ jñāna upajanana hetuḥ tatra saḥ eva doṣaḥ atha artha antara tvam tasya cakṣuḥ indriya āt iṣyate saḥ eva tarhi cakṣuḥ rūpa darśana sāmarthyāt tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca cakṣuṣaḥ tatra api ca sāvayava tva niravayavatva pakṣayoḥ sa doṣaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti yat kiñcid etat 
[I,111,i_I,112,i]	pañcānām ca indriya tvaḥ iti ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi iti sūtrāt na sukha ādi prameyam vā iti lakṣaṇa nyūna tām āha sukha ādi jñānasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena asaṅgrahāt tatas ca sukha ādīnām prameya tva abhyupagama virodhaḥ tatra etat syāt yadi api sukha ādi pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ na bhavati tathā api anumāna ādi viṣaya tvāt prameyam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha yat dhī ityādi sva grahaṇam parakīyeṣu mukha prasāda ādi liṅgasya sulabha tvāt sveṣu tu yadā liṅga abhāvāt na anumānam sādṛśya abhāvāt na upamānam upadeśa abhāvāt na āgamaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa abhāvāt na pratyakṣam tathā katham teṣām prameya tā atha ayam na iṣyate doṣaḥ evam tarhi sukha ādi jñānam pañcamam pramāṇam upasaṅkhyeyam iti darśayan āha tasya vā iti tathā api pramāṇa catuṣṭvā abhyupagama bādhā manaḥ vā astu indriya antaram iti yadi eṣa doṣaḥ na iṣyate iti abhiprāyaḥ evam api pañca indriya abhyupagama vyāghātaḥ 
[I,112,ii_I,112,iii]	aniṣedhāt iti anena iṣṭam eva śāstre manaḥ indriya tvena iti darśayati asti hi ekeṣām iti sāṅkhya ādīnām anya indriya rutam vṛthā iti ghrāṇa ādīnām api indriya tvasya tatas eva siddha tvāt tad vacana vaiyarutam syāt tasmāt punar vacanāt avasīyate anyeṣām indriya tvam nābhimatam iti kecid āhuḥ ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ iti na eva atra ghrāṇa ādīnām indriya tvam vidhīyate kim tarhi indriya tvena prasiddhānām eva bhaitika tvam abhaitikam ca manaḥ tasmāt na nirdiśyate iti etat ca na anya indriya saṅkhyā svabhāva nirākaraṇāt ghrāṇa ādi iti bhūtebhyaḥ iti ca bhaitika tva siddheḥ indriya grahaṇa ānarthakyam syāt 
[I,112,iv]	jñānasya ca ityādi indriya sannikarṣayoḥ pramāṇa tve na syāt phala abhāvaḥ jñānasya phala tvāt jñānāt anartha antara phala vādinaḥ ca yathā sva mate darśitam iti manyate niścaya ātmakam hi ityādi yasya aniścaya ātamakam pramāṇam iṣṭam tasya niścayaḥ phalam artha antaram syāt na tu vyavāniḥ caya ātmakam pramāṇam icchataḥ anyat phalam bhavati nanu ca niścaya jñānam aneka jñāna antaritāt anusmaraṇa vikalpāt anantaram bhavati yathā uktam prāk na ca vyavahitasya phala tvam yuktam anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt tat kutas tasya phala tā satyam tathā api yasya aniścaya ātmakam pramāṇam iṣṭam tasya sthūla darśi tayā niścayaḥ artha antaram phalam syāt iti kalpanā api tāvat sambhavet yasya tu vyavasāya ātmakam eva pratyakṣam iṣṭam tasya kalpanā api eṣā na sambhavati iti darśana artham evam uktam tat evam artha antara phala abhyupagama vyāghātaḥ 
[I,113,i_I,113,ii]	viśeṣaṇa jñānam ityādinā yadi api niścaya ātmaka tvena abhedaḥ tathā api viṣaya bhedena jñāna bhedāt pramāṇāt phalasya bhedam darśayati bhinna tvāt na viśeṣeṇa iti ādeḥ ayam arthaḥ yadi atas anya viṣayam karaṇam na tasya tatra phalam bhavati tat yathā palāśāt anya viṣayasya cchedanasya palāśe viśeṣyāt anya viṣayam ca viśeṣaṇa jñānam karaṇam iti vyāpaka viruddhaḥ anya viṣayasya pramāṇasya iti hetuḥ pramāṇasya iti ca etat karaṇa tva upalakṣaṇam na ca anyatra phalam yuktam iti pramāṇa phalam na hi anya viṣayasya ityādi vyārptiḥ yathā ityādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ viśeṣya jñā hetu tvāt iti asiddha tām āha evam manyate yathā cchedanam khadirāt icchadā nimitta tvāt khadira ādi viṣayam evam viśeṣaṇa jñānam viśeṣya jñāna nimitta tvāt viśeṣya viṣayam iti viśeṣya jñāna nimitta tvam tasya tad abhāve tad abhāvāt na ati prasaṅgāt iti 
[I,114,i]	yaḥ ca pramātā kartā yat ca gavā ādi karma pramīyate yatra ca deśe adhikaraṇe yasmāt ca apāyāt apādānāt yasmai ca dātum tat ca sampradānam etat api sarvam viśeṣya jñāna hetu tvāt viśeṣaṇa jñāna vat karaṇam prasajyate iti arthaḥ tasmāt ityādi iha dvau tad śabdau tatra dvitīyasya sambandhī yat śabdaḥ yasya iti ṣaṣṭhī antar śrūyamāṇaḥ api anumīyate yathā gati buddhi pratyavasāna artha śabda karmā karmakāṇām aṇikartā sa ṇā vid yatra sa ca karmaṇi iti anena sāmānādhikaraṇye vyākhyeyaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ bhavati yasya eva jñānasya yatra karmaṇi jñeye vyāpāra khyātiḥ kāraka antara avyavahitasya vyāpāra pratītiḥ tasya eva karmaṇaḥ jñeyasya tat jñānam pramāṇam iti iha ca viśeṣaṇa jñānasya eva vyāpāra khyātiḥ tad ākāra utpattyā anyathā viśeṣaṇa jñānam eva tat na syāt tasmāt tasya eva viśeṣaṇasya tat pramāṇam na viśeṣyasya tatra tad vyāpārā prathanāt 
[I,115,i]	nanu ca pramāṇam karaṇam kārakam kriyāyāḥ ca kārakāṇi bhavanti na kāraka antarasya tat katham tasya eva karmaṇaḥ tat pramāṇam iti ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ na eva iyam sambandha lakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī kim tarhi kṛt yoga lakṣaṇāḥ yathā palāśānām śātanaḥ iti ayam arthaḥ tasya eva viśeṣaṇasya tat pramāṇam tat eva tena pramīyate na viśeṣyam iti tasmāt siddham bhinna viṣaya tvam 
[I,115,ii]	tatra ca ityādi nanu ca viśeṣaṇe adhigantavye viśeṣya jñānasya phala tvam uktam tat kim ucyate phala abhāvaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ tatra eva viśeṣaṇaḥ eva adhigantavyaḥ iti arthaḥ yadā mandāloke dośe viśeṣaṇam eva kevalam gavā ādi mātram paricchidyate na vyakti viśeṣaḥ tatra saṃśayāt gavā ādi mātrasya ca sāmānya rūpa tvāt tasya ca viśeṣaṇa antara abhāvāt na sāmānyasya viśeṣaṇam sambhavati tadā viśeṣaṇa jñānasya pramāṇa tvam vā syāt phala tvam vā anyatara abhyupagame anyatarasya hāniḥ iti abhyupeta bādhā 
[I,116,i]	dvayam tat ced iti tat parihāraḥ atra ca ekasya ubhaya rūpa virodha parihārāya tat yathā ityādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ yoginām hi yoga niṣpattau ātmānam paśyatām sa grāhyaḥ ca bhavati grahītā ca artha antara phala vādin idam aniṣṭam evam sati prasajyate iti āha yadi artha antare api ityādi sva adhigame tu jñānasya ityādi anena etat darśayati ātma dṛṣṭāntena na artha antare prameye viśeṣaṇa jñānam ubhayathā sidhyati dṛṣṭānta dārṛṣṭa antikayoḥ vaiṣamyāt kim tu sva adhigamaḥ eva jñāsya ubhaya bhāvaḥ sva adhigame ca jñānam ubhayathā pramāṇam prameyam ca mayā iṣyatas eva tat ca tvayā ātma nidarśanena samarthitam iti 
[I,116,ii]	evam tarhi ityādinā yathā pradīpasya andhakāra nivṛttiḥ phalam artha antaram evam jñāna ādi nivṛttiḥ phalam bhaviṣyati iti darśayati viṣaya bhedaḥ api atra na asti iti upanyāsaḥ na sarvatra iti phala vyavasthānasya avyāpi tvam āha kutas etat na sarvatra iti āha kvacid ityādi ābhoga mātreṇa jñānam utpadyate na tatra tasya ajñānam asti tat yathā kasyacid prājñasya kvacid śilpa viśeṣe utpadyate ca kvacid jñeye lokasya ābhoga mātreṇa jñānam vyāpaka viruddham āha 
[I,116,iii]	nivṛttiḥ na asatī phalam iti ajñāna ādi a bhāvaḥ hi ajñāna ādi nivṛttiḥ na ca abhāvasya kiñcana kartavyam asti nirupākhya tvā akriyamāṇaḥ ca prasiddhiḥ bhavitum arhati na pramāṇa phalam bhavitum arhati iti arthaḥ yat asat na tat pramāṇa phalam atyanta abhāva vat asatī ca nivṛttiḥ viruddha vyāptaḥ pradīpasya api na andhakāra nivṛtti mātram phalam kim tu ghaṭa ādi avabhāsanam atas tad avasthaḥ pramāṇa phala bhāva doṣaḥ iti 
[I,117,i_I,117,ii]	kenacid sambandhena iti vṛtti kāra mata bhedena aneka sambandhāḥ tatra kvacid sambandhe pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam idam sūtram na sambhavati iti atas kenacid sambhandhena iti āha tatra kenacid sambandham āhuḥ prasiddhi liṅgaḥ ātmā prasiddhiḥ jñānam iti anartha antaram tasyāḥ ca prasiddheḥ guṇa tvam anitya tvam ca śabda vat draṣṭavyam iti āha anityā ced buddhiḥ anityam ca kāraṇa vat bhavati tasmāt asyāḥ api kāraṇam vācyam anya tvam ca jñātuḥ anena hetunā iti ucyate ātma indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt yat niṣpadyate tat anyat yadi atas niṣpadyate tat tatas anyat tat yathā turya ādibhyaḥ paṭa ādiḥ tathā ca ātma ādibhyaḥ jñānam niṣpadyate tasmāt tat api tebhyaḥ anyat kāraṇam api anena eva darśitam ātma ādi asmin sambandhe pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam idam sūtram na upapadyate 
[I,118,i_I,118,ii]	apare sambandham ācakṣate laiṅgikam pramāṇam uktam atas āha kim laiṅgikam eva evam pramāṇam na iti ucyate ātamendriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt yat niṣpadyate tat anyat pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti vākya śeṣaḥ atra sambandhe pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam idam sūtram vyākhyāyate asautram api bhāṣya kāra uktam asti indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣam ātmanaḥ sannikarṣaḥ vā iti atas sautram iti āha dravya grahaṇena guṇa karmaṇoḥ api sautram pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam aparam asti iti darśayati tat punar guṇa karmasu sannikṛṣṭeṣu jñāna niṣpatteḥ dravyam kāraṇam kāraṇa kāraṇam ca iti atat sva āśrayeṇa anabhivyakteṣu guṇa karmasu jñānam na upajāyate tasmāt tad āśrayaḥ dravyam guṇa karmāṇi abhivyañjayat tad jñānasya kāraṇam bhavati guṇa karma jñānasya kāraṇam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ tasya kāraṇam dravyam ghaṭa ādi kāraṇa kāraṇam iti ucyate atra ca prādhānyāt eka artha samaveta kāraṇa tvāt ca ātmanaḥ sannikarṣāt utpadyate indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāḥ tu tasya anugrāhakāḥ 
[I,118,iii_I,119,i]	kecid tu iti jñānasya hi pramāṇa tve phalam anyan syāt tathā hi adhigamaḥ phalam na ca jñānāt adhigamaḥ artha antaram atas śrāyaka ādayaḥ sannikarṣam icchati asādhāraṇa kāraṇa tvāt iti itare hi sannikarṣāḥ smṛti ādi jñāna sādhāraṇāḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ tu pratyakṣasya eva kāraṇam prādhānyāt iti ātama manasoḥ prādhānyāt tad sannikarṣasya api prādhānyam atas sārasvata ādayaḥ tam icchanti tatra ātmahaḥ prādhānyam jñāna kartṛ tvāt tad liṅga tvāt phala upabhoktṛ tvāt ca manasaḥ api sarva viṣaya tvāt jñānena eka artha samavāyāt ca 
[I,119,ii^1]	evam ca ityādinā śāstra virodham āha yathā hi ātmanaḥ agni ādi samanusmṛtimataḥ pratyakṣam liṅgam ālocya apratyakṣe bhavati anumānam arthe tathā asya eva viśeṣa smṛtimataḥ sāmānya mātra ālocanāt viśeṣeṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ iti tulyā laiṅgikena saṃśayasya niṣpattiḥ yathā ca bhūta artha sambandha vaśena ayam arthasya svabhāvaḥ iti utpadyate pratyakṣam tathā bhūta artha sambandha vaśena ayam eva na anyaḥ iti utpadyate nirṇayaḥ iti pratyakṣam tulya asya niṣpattiḥ iti yat uktam tat virudhyate vicāra pūrvaka tvāt nirṇayasya iti sambandhaḥ sāmānya pratyakṣiṇaḥ saṃśaye sati vicārayataḥ viśeṣa rūpeṇa arthau adhāraṇam yadā tadā gauḥ eva ayam 
[I,119,ii^2]	na gavayaḥ iti nirṇayaḥ utpadyate viṣaya ālocana artha tvāt iti viṣaya anubhava prayojana tvāt iti arthaḥ viṣaya ālocana mātra artham hi iti mātra śabdaḥ adhika vyavaccheda arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati na viśeṣaṇa adhyāra upādau vyāpriyate iti tat ca nirvikalpaka tvāt yasya ca viṣaya anubhava mātram prayojanam tad vicāra nirapekṣam pravartate tat darśayati tatra kutas vicāraḥ iti tatas ca vaidharmyāt na tena nirṇayasya tulya utpattiḥ yathā anumānena syāt etat vidyamāna artha sambandha vaśāt utpatti mātram atidiśyate iti tat ayuktam viśeṣa atideśān arthaka tva prasaṅgāt saṃśaya anumāna ādibhiḥ api evam utpattiḥ tulyā prāpnoti teṣām api sāmānya ādi bhūta artha abhisambandha vaśena utpatteḥ anatideśaḥ eva iti jñānam tasya api sādharmyasya abhāvāt 
[I,120,i]	sarvathā grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti sarvaiḥ ākāraiḥ bāhuleya tva ādibhiḥ api grahaṇam syāt yatra aṃśe śaktiḥ tasya eva grahaṇam bhaviṣyati iti āha sarva ātmanā ityādi niravayavat tvāt na asti eva saḥ aṃśaḥ yaḥ indriyeṇa na sannikṛṣeṇa tatas ca arthāt vyatirikta tvāt tad viśeṣāṇām arthavat teṣu api grahaṇa utpādana śaktiḥ syāt nanu yaḥ eva aṃśaḥ jighṛkṣitaḥ saḥ eva gṛhyate iti āha kim etat ityādi yadā parān paśyataḥ dṛṣṭvā pūrvam eva artha darśanāt kim etat iti aviśeṣeṇa jighṛkṣāyām satyām tatra gatvā paśyati tadā ayam doṣaḥ āpadyate sannikarṣa vādinaḥ ca imam doṣam udbhāvayata ayam arthataḥ jñāna vādinaḥ api udbhāvitaḥ eva bhavati tathā hi sannikarṣaḥ artha grahaṇa hetuḥ iti eṣa doṣaḥ udbhāvyate jñāna pramāṇa vādinā api ca saḥ eva jñānasya hetuḥ iṣyate iti samānaḥ doṣaḥ tathā hi imam eva doṣam anumāne abhidhāsyati 
[I,120,ii]	yadi indriya artha sambandhe sati sarva ātmanaḥ grahaṇam prasajyate tadā bhavataḥ api tribhiḥ indriyaiḥ sambandhyamāne viṣaye kim iti na sarva ātmanā grahaṇaṇam bhavati iti ced na asmābhiḥ tasya sannikarṣaḥ hetuḥ iṣyate tasya adravya sattvāt api ca asmākam cakṣuḥ ādinā api sarvathā gṛhyate arthaḥ iti matam kevalam na bhavati iti avyavahāra yogya tvāt agṛhīta kalpaḥ eva saḥ iti uktam etat yadi punar paraḥ api evam brūyāt na arhati saḥ evam vaktum yat sākṣāt ālocanam arthānām yathā gauḥ eva ayam aśvaḥ eva ayam iti tad pratyakṣam iti vacanāt tathā bhūta artha sambandha vaśena ayam asya svabhāvaḥ iti utpadyate pratyakṣam iti vacanāt tathā yā iyam indriyāṇām artheṣu prasiddhiḥ śabdaḥ ayam rūpam idam rasaḥ ayam sparśaḥ ayam iti vacanāt yatas niścaya ātmakam paraḥ pratyakṣam icchati 
[I,121,i^1]	iyam eva niścayānām sva artha pratipattiḥ yat tat niścayanam tat ced ākāra antara vat aniścitam katham taiḥ gṛhītam katham idānīm aniścīyamānam pratyakṣeṇa tadā api gṛhītam nāma na pratyakṣam kasyacid niścaya ātmakam tat yat api gṛhṇāti tat na niścayena kim tarhi tad pratibhāsena tat na niścaya aniścaya vaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇa agrahaṇe na evam niścayasya kiñcid niścinvataḥ api anyatra aniścayena grahaṇa agrahaṇam tasmāt tat eva asya grahaṇam 
[I,121,i^2]	yaḥ niścayaḥ anyathā eka ākāre api tat na syāt kim punar sarvāt manāḥ gṛhīte api tathā niścayaḥ na bhavati sahakāri vaikalyāt anubhavaḥ hi yathā vikalpa abhyāsam niścayān janayati yathā rūpa darśana aviśeṣe api kuṇapa kāminī bhakṣya vikalpān tatra buddhi pāṭavam tad vāsanā abhyāsaḥ prakaraṇam iti ādayaḥ anubhavān niścaya utpatti hetavaḥ teṣām eva tu tāratamya ādi viśeṣāt paurvāparyam yathā janaka adhyāpakatva aviśeṣe api pitaram āyāntam paśyataḥ pitā me āgacchati iti prāgniścayaḥ bhavati na upādhyāyaḥ iti saḥ api bhavat niścayaḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe bhavati tasmāt na anubhūtaḥ iti eva sarva ākāra niścayaḥ 
[I,122,i]	yadi tarhi paraḥ sa vikalpam pratyakṣam icchati katham tat uktam viṣaya ālocana mātra artham hi catuṣṭaya sannikarṣa jam iti pramāṇa siddham indriya jñāsya avikalpaka tvam iti vastu vaśāt ācāryeṇa tat uktam asmābhiḥ tu para abhyupagama vaśāt evam uktam iti avirodhaḥ yadi parasya niścaya ātmakam pratyakṣam iti abhyupagamaḥ katham pratyakṣeṇa nirṇayasya tulya utpattiḥ iti etat yujyate na hi tena eva tasya tulya utpattiḥ iti yuktam abhyupetum ayam aparaḥ tasya doṣaḥ astu yaḥ evam icchati iti alam iti prasaṅgena 
[I,122,ii]	viṣaya bhedaḥ api iti pramāṇasya ātma manaḥ viṣaya tvāt phalasya ca artha viṣaya tvāt nanu jñānam api ātmani samavāyāt tad viṣayam eva na etat asti jñānasya hi jñeyam viṣaya tvena abhimatam na samavāyi kāraṇam anyathā sarva jñānānām ekaṣaya tā syāt ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ tu anālambanaḥ tasya samavāyi kāraṇāt kaḥ anyaḥ viṣayaḥ syāt iti anuttaram etat viṣaya bhede kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha na hi ityādi 
[I,123,i]	api ca ityādinābhyupeta bādhām āha śāstre uktam sāmānya viśeṣa apekṣam dravya guṇa karmasu pratyakṣam dravya guṇa karma apekṣam ca dravyeṣu iti atra sāmānya grahaṇena mahāsāmānyam sattā gṛhyate viśeṣa grahaṇena dravya tva ādīni śeṣāṇi sāmānyāni viśeṣāḥ ca apekṣyāḥ bhavanti tatra sāmānya apekṣam dravye sat dravyam iti viśeṣa apekṣam dravyam pṛthivī ghaṭaḥ ityādi dravya guṇa karma apekṣam daṇḍī śuklaḥ gacchati iti 
[I,123,ii]	kutas na yujyate iti āha yasmāt ityādi sva artha mātra grāhika tvāt iti etat viṣaya ālocana artha tvāt iti asya vivaraṇam sandhānam yojanam tasya svarūpam darśayati idam asya ityādinā avaśyam iti anyathā yaḥ api viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca na gṛhṇāti tayoḥ ca sandhānam na karoti saḥ api tathā gṛhṇīyāt iti manyate matu blopāda bheda upacārāt eva iti yathāsambhavam draṣṭavyam tathā hi guṇa vacanebhyaḥ matubh lopaḥ abheda upacāraḥ api na sarvatra na hi kriyā dravya rūpeṇa āśraya tītiḥ asti matubarthaḥ tu yatra gamyate saḥ eva matublopena lakṣyate 
[I,124,i]	yadi indriya buddhau tat na upapadyate kva tarhi tat iti āha tat ca ityādi prāc viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca gṛhītvā loka vyavasthām ca anusmṛtya anusandhānam śakyate kartum na anyathā tadā ca indriya jñānam cira niruddham iti smārtena ākṛṣya viśeṣaṇam manasā eva yojanam kriyate atas tatra eva tat upapadyate anyathā hi iti yadi smārta ākṛṣṭa tvam viśeṣaṇasya na iṣyate tat anena yat viśeṣaṇa apekṣam jñānam na tat pratyakṣam mānasam eva vā tat tat yathā surabhi madhuram iti jñānam yathā ukta prakāram ca gauḥ gacchati iti vyāpaka viruddham dvitīya sādhya apekṣyā tu svabhāvam āha na ca arhati iti dṛṣṭānte sādhya vaikalpa āśaṅkām apakāroti bhinna indriya grāhya tvāt iti dṛṣṭānte gandha rasayoḥ ghrāṇa rasana grāhya tvāt dravyasya ca cakṣuḥ sparśana grāhya tvāt tat etat uktam bhavati yat bhinna indriya grāhya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya viṣayam jñānam na tat pratyakṣam mānasam eva vā tat tat yathā rūpam amlam iti jñānam tathā ca surabhi madhuram iti etat jñānam iti pūrvavat dhetu bhedaḥ yojyaḥ 
[I,124,ii]	idānīm dravyam eva na kiñcid asti rūpa ādi samudāye tat upacārāt tat kutas tatra pratyakṣam bhaviṣyati iti dravye vicāram ārabhate yadi ca ityādi asya ayam arthaḥ yat aneka indriya grāhyam na tat ekam rūpa ādi vat tathā ca dravyam iti vyāpaka viruddhaḥ prasaṅgaḥ aneka indriya grāhya tvam tu dravyasya darśanam sparśanam ca dravyam iti abhyupagamāt 
[I,125,i]	rūpa ādi abhedaḥ vā iti etat darśayati rūpa ādiṣu api bheda vyasthāyāḥ aneka indriya grāhya tvam nibandhanam yadi ca sati api tasmin dravye bhedaḥ na iṣyate rūpa ādiṣu api sa na syāt iti grahaṇa bhedāt rūpa ādīnām aneka tva vyavasthā iti ced bhavatu tatas api na asmābhiḥ bhinna indriya grāhya tvāt eva bhedaḥ iti avadhāryate api ca bhinna indriya grāhya tvena grahaṇa bhedaḥ api ākṣiptaḥ eva avaśyam hi bhinna indriya grāhya tve grahaṇa bhedena bhāvyam nanu dravye sati api bhinna indriya grāhya tve na bhavati grahaṇa bhedaḥ na tasya eva dravyasya vicāryamāṇa tvāt rūpa ādiṣu api tulya paryanuyogāt ca 
[I,125,ii]	dṛṣṭam ca indriya ādinā pratyakṣa siddham dravyasya ekatvam rūpa ādeḥ ca aneka tvam tat katham tat anumānena anyathā śakyate kartum iti darśayati bhāva guṇa tvayoḥ iva iti anena api bhāva guṇa tvābhyām anekāntam āha bhāga guṇa tvayoḥ āśrayāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ sārva indiryāḥ tatas tayoḥ api sārva indriya tvam yathā uktam etena guṇa tve bhāve ca sārva indriyam jñānam vyākhyātam iti abheda jñānam punar yat eva mayā dṛṣṭam tat eva spṛśāmi iti na indriyeṇa tat iti parihāraḥ akṣa aneka tva vaiyarthyāt iti aneka indriya kalpanāyāḥ nirnimitta tvāt iti arthaḥ ekam indriyam anekam artham sakalam na alam avagantum iti indriya antaram parikalpyate yadi punar tat indriya antara arthe api pravartate indriya bahutva kalpanā nirnimittā syāt etat uktam bhavati kārya bhedena indriya bhedaḥ avasīyate indriya kāryam ced ekena eva kriyate na indriya antare pramāṇam asti iti tat na kalpanīyam syāt iti apārthikā iti nirnimitta iti arthaḥ 
[I,126,i^1]	atha api syāt iti evam manyate anekam indriyam ekakm artham paricchettum samartham na punar ekam anekam artham aneke ca rūpa ādayaḥ tatas na asti indriya bahutva kalpanā vaii artham iti sva arthe bhinne api ityādi yadi hi ekam indriyam indriya antara arthe api pravarteta tatas sarve eva sa tasya sva arthaḥ syāt sva arthe ca bhinne api nīla ādi vat tasya śaktiḥ syāt eva iti aparihāraḥ saṅkhī ā ādi bhedena ca iti saṅkhyā parimāṇāni pṛthaktvam saṃyoga vibhāgau paratva aparatve karma ca rūpi samavāyāt cākṣuṣāṇi iti siddhāntāt na tu indriya antara arthaḥ iti etena yaḥ cakṣuḥ indriya arthaḥ na tatra tvac indriyasya sāmarthayam 
[I,126,i^2]	rūpa ādi vat tathā ca dravyam iti vyākapa viruddham prasaṅga sūcayati indriya antara artha tvena eva ityādi rūpa sparśatoḥ hi san api bhedaḥ yāvat bhinnena indriyeṇa na avasīyate tāvat na śakyate jñātum yadi punar ekena indriyeṇa grahaṇam syāt tadā yathā nīla ādīnām cakṣuḥ gocara tvena abhedaḥ tathā rūpa sparśayoḥ api syāt tatas ca sparśaḥ api cakṣuṣā gṛhyeta yatas cakṣuṣā agrahaṇam iti bheda kṛtam indriya antara agrahaṇam darśayati tat etena yatra sparśana indriyasya sāmarthyam na sa cakṣuḥ indriya arthaḥ sparśa vat sparśana indriyasya sāmarthyam ca dravyaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddham prasaṅgam āha 
[I,127,i]	asya eva sādhya viparyaye aniṣṭam prasaṅgayan āha tat yadi ityādi yadi punar cakṣuḥ sparśana grāhyam api dravyam gṛhṇāti iti iṣyate tadā indriya antara arthe api cakṣuṣaḥ sva arthaḥ iti abhyanujñātam syāt dravya vat tatas ca sva artha tvāt tasya sparśa rasa ādi bhedena bhinnasya api nīla ādeḥ iva cakṣuṣā grahaṇam iti atas na bhinna tvam aneka indriya grāhya tve hetuḥ na aneka indriya kalpanāyām hetuḥ iti arthaḥ yatas bhinnaḥ api sva arthaḥ ekena eva indriyeṇa paricchidyate tatas ca tat ayuktam āpadyate yat uktam bhinna tvāt aneka indriya grāhyāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti kim tarhi indriya antara arthaḥ indriya antareṇa na śakyate grahītum evam anekam indriyam śakyate kalpayitum iti darśayati tat evam sthitam etat na dravyam aneka indriya grāhyam asti 
[I,127,ii]	punar asya eva spaṣṭīkaraṇāya dravyasya aneka indriya abhyupagame abhyupeta bādhā prāpnoti iti darśayan āha yadi ceyādi yadi abhinnam artham anekam indriyam gṛhṇīyāt tatas sva viṣaya niyamaḥ syāt indriyāṇām atas ca rūpa ādīnām sārva indriya tvam pratyekam syāt dravya vat sārva indriya grahaṇam ca atra eka indriya grāhya tā niyama nirāsa param yat āha evam hi rūpa ādayaḥ aneka indriya grāhyāḥ prāpnuvanti iti na niyamena eka indriya grāhyāḥ syuḥ iti arthaḥ 
[I,128,i_I,128,ii]	sva viśeṣa niyāmākāḥ iti sva viśeṣe niyāmakāḥ indriya buddhīnām iti sanmbandhīyam na hi dravya saṅkhyā ādi karmasu iti ādi grahaṇāt bhāva guṇa tva pṛthaktva ādayaḥ gṛhyate na syāt ityādi dravyasya sparśanena cakṣuṣā ca grahaṇam na syāt śeṣāṇām cakṣuṣā iti yojanīyam evam tarhi iti anyathā niyāmaka tvam āha evam ca iti atra pakṣe anantara uktaḥ doṣaḥ na avatarati iti darśayati yasya yatra niyama kāraṇam na asti na tatra tasya niyamaḥ tat yathā iccha mātra vṛttīnām kvacid arthe hasta ādi sañjñānām na asti ca niyama kāraṇam indriyāṇām dravya ādiṣu kāraṇa abhāvaḥ sūtra virodhaḥ iti abhyupeta bādhām āha 
[I,129,i_I,129,ii]	yuktyā api ityādi yaḥ abhāvaḥ na asau kriyate kha puṣpa vat abhāvaḥ ca indriya antareṇa agrahaṇam vyāpaka viruddhaḥ anye sūtram anyathā vyācakṣate tad grahaṇena sva viśeṣa vyatiriktam viśeṣa antaram abhipretam tad abhāvāt sparśa tva ādi abhāvāt rūpe cakṣuḥ indriyam pravartate tena ca sparśa tva ādi abhāvena rūpa tva bhāvaḥ lakṣyate avyabhicāraḥ indriya antareṇa agrahaṇām iti tat api yukti api ca ityādinā eva nirakṛtam yukti anuvidhāyi tve hi sati tathā avyākhyānam śobheta yukti virodhe tu kaṣṭa kalpanā kalpanā eva api ca sva viśeṣāṇām prakṛta tvāt tat śatrutyā teṣām eva grahaṇam yuktam na viśeṣa antarāṇām aprakṛta tvāt tad abhāvena ca bhāva upādānam ayuktam iti asāram etat 
[I,129,iii_I,129,iv]	pūrvake tu vyākhyāne na asti ayam doṣaḥ yatra hi yasya hetuḥ na asti na tat tatra bhavati iti yuktam yat āha syāt tu ityādi yadi tarhi dravyam na asti yat aham adrākṣam tat eva as prākṣam iti asya abheda jñānasya kaḥ viṣayaḥ na ca aviṣayam eva etat iti śakyate vaktum deśa ādi niyamena utpatteḥ abhimata pratyakṣa vat iti matvā āha yat tarhi ityādi 
[I,129,v]	anya gocaram ityādi dravyāt anyaḥ eva asya kalpitaḥ viṣayaḥ iti darśayati bhinnam viṣayam ityādi rūpam sparśam ca parasparataḥ vyāvṛttam viṣayam upalabdhavataḥ tat utpadyate tena yadi api kalpita viṣayam tathā api sati rūpa ādi upalambhe tasya bhāvān marīcikā ādau jala jñāna vat eśā ādi niyamena eva tat utpadyate iti sūcayati tad sahacara samudāya viṣayam iti sa cakṣuḥ sparśana upalabdhaḥ bhinnaḥ viṣayaḥ sahacaraḥ asya iti tad guṇa saṃvijñānaḥ bahuvrīhiḥ punar tad sahacaraḥ samudāyaḥ viṣayaḥ asya iti bahuvrīḥ eva evam rūpa sparśayoḥ sahacara upalakṣaṇa tve api sati na gandha ādi samudāya mātra viṣaya tā uktā bhavati smārtam abheda jñānam iti yeṣu rūpa ādiṣu anubhava puraḥsaraḥ ghaṭaḥ iti saṅketaḥ tad samudāye punar uttara kālam rūpam sparśam ca upalabdhavataḥ smārtam saḥ eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti abheda jñānam utpadyate 
[I,130,i]	yaḥ tu āha samudāyaḥ avastu tvāt na kenacid jñānena anubhūyate tat katham tatra smṛtiḥ iti tasya idam acodyam samudāyaḥ hi kalpitaḥ yaḥ ca kalpitaḥ padārthaḥ sa vijñānasya grāhya aṃśa tayā ātma bhūtaḥ iti sva saṃvittyā eva anubhūyate anyathā katham sā eva iyam mahatī prāsāda mālā iti smaraṇam syāt kutas etat samudāya viṣayam tat na punar vastu saddhaṭa ādi dravya viṣayam iti āha rūpa ādi agrahe tad buddha bhāvāt iti yaḥ yat agrahe sati upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ na upalabhyate na sa tatas vyatiriktaḥ asti tat yathā kāṣṭha ādibhyaḥ ṣaṇṇagarī prāsāda mālā vā rūpa ādi agrahe na upalabhyate ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam ghaṭa ādi dravyam iti svabhāva anupalabdhim āha yatra āloka āgrahaḥ tatra rūpam dṛśyam eva na bhavati vinā api ca alokena kaiścid prāṇibhiḥ tasya grahaṇāt na tena anekāntaḥ 
[I,131,i]	tathā viśeṣyān ityādi bhāva guṇa tvābhyām yaḥ prāk anekānte uktaḥ tad parihārāya upanyāsaḥ viśeṣyāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ tān bhinnān sat guṇaḥ iti ca anena viśeṣaṇena asambaddhān eva prāk upalabdhavataḥ tatas artha antara vyavaccheda viṣayam asat guṇa vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yat sāmānyam tat viṣayam iti yāvat abhedena sarvatra iti tat dhi mānasam sāmānya ākāra anuraktam jñānam santam api teṣām bhedam antardhāpya su a ākāram ca abhinnam eṣu pratyasya eka tvam iva apādayat tān abhedena sarveṣu teṣu upajāyate na ekatra eva na bhāva guṇa tvayoḥ pratyakṣam iti atas na anekāntaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tasya anupalakṣaṇāt iti bhinna padārtha viṣayam prāk anubhava jñānam tatas tat pūrvakam mānasam sāmānya jñānam iti asya bhedasya anupalakṣaṇāt 
[I,131,ii]	tulya gocarateṣṭā ced iti anaikāntika tva samarthanāya upanyāsaḥ tulya gocara tve hetum āha tad agre tad buddha bhāvāt iti na agṛhīta viśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiḥ pravartate iti arthaḥ tatas ca rūpa ādīnām viśeṣyāṇām sārva indriya tvāt tad viśeṣaṇayoḥ api bhāva guṇa tvayoḥ sārva indriya tvam sidhyati ye hi viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhūtāḥ te tulya indriya viṣayāḥ tat yathā daṇḍaṇḍinaḥ tathā ca sattva tadvantaḥ guṇa tva tadvantaḥ ca svabhāva pratirūpakaḥ 
[I,132,i]	aniṣṭam anuṣajyate iti prasaṅga vyājena anaikāntika tvam āha dravyavanti ityādi dravyam eṣām āśrayaḥ asti iti dravyavanti atra dravyavān guṇaḥ viśeṣyaḥ dravyam viśeṣaṇam tatas ca yathā guṇaḥ pāñca indriyaḥ tathā dravyam api syāt tathā eka dravya tvāt ityādi dravyam hi adravyam aneka dravyam ca iṣyate na tu eka dravyam dravyam tatra adravyam dravyam yasya dravya antaram āśrayaḥ na asti yathā paramāṇu ākāśa ādikam aneka dravyam tu dravyam yasya anekam dravyam āśrayaḥ yathā ghaṭaḥ sa hi anekatra samavetaḥ atra api ekam dravyam bhāvasya sārva indriyasya viśeṣaṇam iti dravyam api sārva indriyam syāt na ca iṣyate tasmāt anekāntaḥ 
[I,132,ii_I,133,i]	dravya vṛtteḥ ityādi dravya vṛttiḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ tasya ekam dravyam viśeṣaṇam na ca asau sārva indriyaḥ kim tarhi guṇa vṛttiḥ tatas ayam aprasaṅgaḥ kutas etat abhinnaḥ bhāvaḥ dravya ādi bhāve na pratiṣidhyate na punar bhinnaḥ iti āha tathā hi uktam ityādi bhāvasya dravya svabhāva pratiṣedhe kṛte guṇaḥ tarhi syāt karma ca iti āśaṅka apanodāya idam uktam guṇa karmasu ca bhāvān na karma na guṇaḥ iti atas prakṛtasya eva bhāvasya dharmaḥ caśabdena smuccīyate anyathā samuccayāya cakāraḥ na yujyate dravya vṛtteḥ ca guṇa karmasu avṛtteḥ guṇa karma svabhāva nirāsaḥ na syāt yadi ca ityādi yadi ayam viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ iṣyate tatas bhinnaḥ syāt tatas ca ayam anantara uktaḥ doṣaḥ syāt etat ca sūtram virudhyate sat liṅga aviśeṣāt viśeṣa liṅga abhāvāt ca ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ yadā ca ityādi yadā ayam cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭa agniṣṇaḥ ayam iti gṛhṇati tadā sparśaḥ api agni viśeṣaṇa tvat cākṣuṣaḥ syāt na ca evam iti 
[I,133,ii_I,134,i]	atas pi anekāntaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi iti anena arthāpatti samām jātim upanyasyati anantareṇa api ca ityādinā bhinneṣu api nīla ādiṣu indriya bheda abhāvam darśayantaru cā aitanye svāpa vat dvitīyām upalabdhi samām grahaṇa bhedāt iti ca hetu antara upadarśanāt prathamām anyathā uktam ityādinā arthāpatti samām nirasyati syāt etat anekāntaḥ iti anena na hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ uktaḥ kim tarhi pratijñā doṣaḥ yatas tvayā bhinna indriya grāhya tvāt eva iti avadhārayatā hetu antaram na asti iti pratijñātam bhavati tat ca ayuktam hetu antarasya api sadbhāvāt iti atas āha na ca ityādi na ca atra anekāntaḥ iti na ayam niyamaḥ vyabhicāri iti arthaḥ 
[I,134,ii_I,134,iii]	na sarvam sādhyam ityādinā dvitīyām upalabdhi samām apākaroti na buddhi bhedaḥ api anyatva ityādinā hetu antare api sādhyasya vṛttim darśayan sādhya vyabhicāra pradarśanāt prathamām bhede abhedaḥ kutas anyathā iti grahaṇa bhedāt kevalāt anyathā indriya bhede grahaṇa bhede ca sati abhedaḥ na eva iti yāvat yatra ca ityādinā yadi kevalāt grahaṇa bhedāt nīla ādiṣu bhedaḥ evam sati yatra indriya bhedaḥ grahaṇa bhedaḥ ca asti tatra sutarām bhedaḥ sidhyati indriya abheda kṛtāyāḥ abheda āśaṅkāyāḥ abhāvāt iti darśayati 
[I,135,i]	etena iti dravye pratyakṣa nirākaraṇa nyāyena guṇa ādiṣu iti ādi śabdena karmasu apeditam pratyākhyātam katham iti āha tat api hi ityādi sva ādhāram guṇa karmaṇoḥ sva sāmānyam guṇa tvam karma tvam ca sve ādhāraḥ yasya tat sva ādhāram tad sambandha dvāreṇa utpadyate iti anena saha sambandhaḥ viśeṣaṇa sambandha dvāreṇa utpadyate iti yāvat tatas ca yat viśeṣaṇa apekṣam na tat pratyakṣam ityādi pūrvavat sādhanam vācyam kim ca tat api catuṣṭaya ādi sannikarṣāt eva utpadyate iti idam darśanam ādi śabdena traya sannikarṣāt dvaya sat nikarṣāt ca yathāsambhavam tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha yathā ca na sarvatra ityādi tatra catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt ātma manā aindriya dravya sannikarṣāt rūpa ādiṣu karmasu ca traya sannikarṣāt śabde tatra dravyeṇa saha indriyasya sambandhaḥ na asti vyomnaḥ śrotra tvāt tatra eva ca samvāyāt śabdasya dvaya sat nikarṣāt ātma manaḥ sannikarṣāt sukha ādiṣu tat evam guṇa karmasu asat nikṛṣṭeṣu jñāna niṣpatteḥ dravyam kāraṇa kāraṇam ca iti yat uktam tat api dūṣitam iti 
[I,136,i_I,136,ii]	kāpilānām ityādi tatra uktam kim anumānam eva ekam pramāṇam na iti ucyate śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ ca pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti śeṣa śrotra tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇānām manasā adhiṣṭhitā vṛttiḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandheṣu yathākramam grahaṇe vartamānā pratyakṣam pramāṇam manasā iti manaḥ vṛttyā prakṛti vikārayoḥ abheda upacārāt evam uktam adhiṣṭhāna arthaḥ tat yathā rāja puruṣeṇa adhiṣṭhiḥ pravṛttaḥ tena saha iti gamyate 
[I,136,iii]	anye tu āhuḥ manasā adhiṣṭhitā iti manasā saṃviditā yathā uktam bāhyeṣu artheṣu indriyam vyavasāyam kurute tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute iti anena hi grantena indriya vṛttiḥ eva bāhya viṣaya ākārā manaḥ vṛttyā saṃvedyate na tu indriya vṛtti sahitayā bāhyaḥ arthaḥ iti pratipāditam tasmāt yā śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ manaḥ vṛttyā gṛhyate sā tayā adhiṣṭhitā iti uktā 
[I,136,iv]	vṛttiḥ indriyāṇām sva viṣaya sānnidhye tad ākāreṇa pariṇāmaḥ jñeyaḥ sā punar dvi prakārā sa pratyayā ca apratyayā ca pratyayaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ bodhaḥ ucyate caitanya rūpaḥ viṣaya anubhava svabhāvaḥ etat ca ātmanaḥ svarūpam na anyasya kasyacid acetana tvāt tena pauruṣeyeṇa pratyayena saha yā sampṛktā tad eka rūpa tām iva āpannā sā sa pratyayā yathā tapta avasthāyām ayogolakaḥ tejaḥ samparkāt atat svabhāvaḥ api tejaḥ svabhāva tām iva āpadyate tathā vṛttiḥ ananubhava rūpā api caitanya saṃsargāt caitanya rūpa tām iva āpadyate yā punar vṛttiḥ pradīpa prabheda kevalam viṣaya pralāśikā na tu caitanya samparkāt āsādita tad rūpā iva sā apratyaya iti ucyate tatra apratyaya vṛtti nivṛttye grahaṇe vartamānā iti āha śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām yathākramam iti anena sva viṣaya viniveśa vacanāt niyata viṣaya tvam 
[I,137,i]	nanu śrotra ādi vṛttteḥ eva śabda ādīnām grahaṇam tatra kā anyā vṛttiḥ yā grahaṇe vartate kecid āhuḥ indriya viṣaya antarāla vartinī kaśā abhighāta vat ūrdhva ākṣipta jala vat vā viṣaye svasmin apratiṣṭhitā vṛttiḥ ucyate pratiṣṭhitā tu viṣaya ākāreṇa partiṇāmena pariniṣpannā grahaṇam iti yatra api ca antarālam na asti ghnāṇa ādau tatra api indriyasya viṣaya saṃyoga anantaram vikriyā upajāyamānā viṣaya ākāra tvena apariniṣpannā vṛttiḥ jñeyā tathā pariniṣpanna antargaṇam iti 
[I,138,i]	anye tu āhuḥ vṛttīnām nirvikalpa tva upadarśana artham etat bhedena uktam śabda ādīnām grahaṇe vartamānā iti etat uktam bhavati svarūpa grahaṇa mātre vartamānā pratyakṣam pramāṇam na anyathā iti yadi api vikalpane asyāḥ sambhavaḥ na asti tathā api jaiminīya ādibhiḥ vikalpakam pratyakṣam kalpitam tad apekṣayā etat viśeṣaṇam sarvā eva tu vṛttiḥ grahaṇa mātre vartate na vikalpane iti grahaṇe vartamānā iti tad svabhāva iti arthaḥ
