[I,138,ii_I,138,iii]	anye tu apratyayām eva vṛttim pramāṇam icchanti sa pratyayām tu phalam grahaṇe vartamānā iti ca evam varṇayanti grahaṇe phale kartavye grahaṇa nimittam pravṛttā iti arthaḥ indriyānavasthā iti ānantyam indriyāṇām prasajyate iti arthaḥ katham iti āha taiḥ hi ityādi yathā uktam badhiraḥ satsu indriyeṣu navasu śabdam na śṛṇoti tasmāt śrotram eva śabda viṣayam anena tu aga ādīnām sva viṣaya viniveśaḥ boddhavyaḥ iti 
[I,138,iv_I,139,i]	trayaḥ guṇāḥ traiguṇyam trailokya vat utkarṣaḥ ādhikyam apakarṣaḥ nyūna tā mātra śabdaḥ svabhāva bheda vyavacchedāya na hi śabda ādīnām sattva ādi guṇa svabhāvānām svarūpa bhedaḥ asti tatas ca śānta ghora mūḍha ṣaḍja ādi bhedena ānantyāt anantam indriyam syāt yathā hi śabda ādi jāti bhedaḥ guṇa utkarṣāt bhavati tathā ṣaḍja ādi bhedaḥ api atas etat uktam bhavati ye guṇa utkarṣa bheda bhinnāḥ te bhinna indriya grāhya jāti samanvitāḥ śabda sparśa ādi vat tathā ca dhaivatā ādayaḥ śabda viśeṣāḥ iti svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca abhyupeta bādhaḥ atha ityādi yadi utkarṣa apakarṣa bhedeṣu api ṣaḍja ādiṣu śrotra indriya grāhya eka traiguṇya jāti mat tvam iṣyate prāptam ekam eva indriyam sarvatra traiguṇyasya abhedāt ye abhinna traiguṇya jāti avitāḥ te śrotra indriya grāhyāḥ ṣaḍja ādi vat tathā ca śabda sparśa ādayaḥ saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,139,ii]	nanu karma vaśāt indriya abhinirvṛttiḥ na grāhya vaśāt tatra katham idam codyate anantam ekam vā indriyam prāpnoti iti asmākam karma vaśāda acintyaḥ ca karmaṇaḥ vipākaḥ iti manam paraḥ tu puruṣa autsukkya nivṛttaye pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ iti manyate tatra yadi ekena eva indriyeṇa puruṣa arthaḥ sampadyeta eka indriya ātmanā eva prakṛteḥ yuktaḥ pariṇāmaḥ anyathā anyathā iti yuktam codyam syāt etat na brūmaḥ traiguṇyam eva śrotra indriya grāhyam api tu tasya eva pariṇāmaḥ buddhi anugama nimittam sādṛśyam nāma jātiḥ sā ca sarva śabda bhedeṣu anuvartamānāḥ vyāvartate sparśa ādibhyaḥ sā eva śrotra indriyeṇa gṛhyate tena na kaścid doṣaḥ iti āha na hi traiguṇya vyatirekeṇa ityādi 
[I,140,i]	katham na astīy āha asti eva saṃsthāna akmikā jātiḥ traiguṇya abhede api hi traiguṇya saṃsthāna amātra bhedāt śabda ādi jātayaḥ bhidyante tathā hi uktam śabda sparśa rūra sagandhāḥ pañca trayāṇām sukha duḥkha mohānām sanniveśa viśeṣāḥ iti tasmāt śabda ākāra pariṇatāḥ sukha ādayaḥ yena samavasthitāḥ saṃsthāna bhedena tatas saṃsthāna antareṇa samavasthatāḥ sparśa ādayaḥ iti vyapadiśyante tatas niyata indriya grāhya tā na ca indriya ānantyam pañcatvāt saṃsthānānām 
[I,140,ii]	saṃsthānam dvi grāhyam iti nanu saṃthānam adravyasat tat kutas tasya dvi grāhyatā na eṣa doṣaḥ para abhiprāyeṇa evam uktam paraḥ hi rūpi indriya vijñāna anvayena manaḥ vijñānena saṃsthānam upalabhya tayoḥ vijñānayoḥ sūkṣmatara kāla bhedasya duravadhāra tvāṭ tat eva idam cakṣuḥ sparśana vijñānam dīrgha ādi saṃsthāna grāhi iti yathā manyate tathā idam uktam etat darśayati bhavatu nāma saṃsthānam vastutas tat dvi grāhyam dṛṣṭam iti sva viṣaya viniveśa vyāghātaḥ iti 
[I,140,iii_I,140,iv]	śabda ādayaḥ ca iti abhyupeya bādhām āha atha vā prasaṅga viparyayeṇa yaḥ yat dharmaḥ na bhavati na asau tad ātmakaḥ tat yathā caitanyam apradhāna dharmakam na tad ātmakam na bhavanti ca śabda ādayaḥ saṃsthāna dharmāṇaḥ iti vyāpaka abhāvam saṃsthānam na tri gocaraḥ iti sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvam āha saṃsthāna kṛtam ca ityādi vīṇā paṇava ādi śabda jātīnām hi para sparataḥ bhinnānām śabda jāti anatikrameṇa avasthānāt samāna deśa tvam syāt tat ca ayuktam na hi dīrgha hrasva ādi saṃsthānam eka deśam dṛṣṭam iṣṭam ca iti abhyupeta bādhā 
[I,141,i_I,141,ii]	tulya saṃsthāneṣu ca ityādi saṃsthāna bheda kṛtam jāti bhedam icchataḥ suvarṇa ādi mayeṣu dhaṭa ādiṣu tulya saṃsthāneṣu saṃsthāna svabhāva tvāt jāti bhedānām saṃsthānasya ca teṣu tulya tvāt āpannam eka tvam suvarṇa ādi jātīnām tad kāraṇānām ca śabda ādīnām tad kāraṇānām ca satva ādīnām nanu mātrā ādīnām eva tulya saṃsthānānām yuktam eka tvam suvarṇa ādīnām tu katham tat avyatirekāt te api sama saṃsthānāḥ iti acodyam etat sva viṣaya vṛtti abhāvaḥ iti cakṣuṣā ghaṭa ādi grahaṇe śabda ādīnām grahaṇāt prasaṅga viparyayeṇa ca yaḥ yat abhede api bhidyate na asau tad ātmakaḥ yathā caitanya abhede api bhidyamāhaḥ sattva ādayaḥ na tad ātmakāḥ saṃsthāna abhede api ca bhidyante suvarṇa ādayaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddham āha 
[I,141,iii]	jāti mātra grāhikā vā iti saṃsthāna mātra grāhikā mātra śabdaḥ sukha ādi grahaṇa vyavaccheda arthaḥ jāti viśiṣṭa sukha ādi grāhikā vā iti saṃsthāna viśiṣṭa sukha ādi grāhikā artha svabhāva agrāhaṇam iti śanda ādīnām sukha ādi svabhāva agrahaṇam syāt eta saṃsthānāt avyatirekāt artha svabhāvasya tad upalabdhau saḥ api upalabdhaḥ eva iti āha yasmāt dṛṣṭa ityādi etena yasya saṃsthāna mātra upalabdhiḥ na tasya svabhāvaḥ upalabhyate tat yathā manda prakāse pradeśe gavādeḥ upalabhyamānasya saṃsthāna mātrasya saṃsthāna mātra upalabdhiḥ ca indriya vṛttyā śabda ādīnām iti viruddha vyāptam āha 
[I,142,i_I,142,ii]	artha bheda āgrahaḥ iti śabda ādeḥ arthasya viśeṣa upalabdhiḥ na syāt tatra saṃsthāna antara abhāvāt iti śaba ādayaḥ hi saṃsthāna ātmakāḥ jātayaḥ na ca tatra apara saṃsthānam asti yena vīṇā śabdaḥ iti grahaṇam syāt iti abhyupetahānam atha mā mūdeṣa doṣaḥ iti śabda jāteḥ api saṃsthāna antaram viśeṣaḥ kauśika ādiḥ iṣyate evam tarhi ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate iti darśayan āha arthe vā ityādi arthaḥ sva viṣayaḥ tatra vikalpikā syāt kutas iti āha sva artha viśiṣṭasya ityādi śabda jāti viśiṣṭasya tad viśeṣasya kauśika ādeḥ grahaṇāt iti arthaḥ niyogataḥ ca viśeṣaḥ śabda jāti viśiṣṭaḥ grāhyaḥ anyathā śabdasya ayam viśeṣaḥ iti na gṛhyeta na ca jāti viśiṣṭa tad bheda grahaṇa abhyupagame jāti mātra grāhikā iti api pakṣaḥ hīyate yatas mātra śabdena sukha ādi vyavacchidyate na śabda ādi jāti viśeṣaḥ tat etat uktam bhavati yā viśeṣaṇa vyavacchinna artha grāhiṇī buddhiḥ sā sa vikalpikā tat yathā citra gurayam iti buddhiḥ tathā ca śabda ādi viśeṣa viṣayā buddhiḥ iti svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,142,iii_I,143,i]	atha ityādinā pakṣa antare api tam eva doṣam āha sukha ādīn ca iti sukha ādayaḥ eva śabdāt ātmanā sanniviṣṭāḥ iti atas paśnaḥ na tāvat pratyekam ityādi ekaikasya sukha ādeḥ grahaṇe hi indriya vṛttīnām sva viṣayaḥ eva niveśaḥ na syāt sarvatra sukha ādīnām aviśeṣāt sa ca iṣyate tasmāt na pratyekam sukha ādi grāhyam kim tarhi śabda ādi te eva tarhi pratyekam pariṇatāḥ śabda ādi svabhāvāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti āha na hi ityādi pañca trayāṇām sanniveśa viśeṣāḥ iti abhyupagamāt na etat samasti tat etat uktam bhavati yat śabda ādi svabhāvam na bhavati na tat śrotra ādi vṛtti grāhyam caitanya vat na bhavati ca pratyekam sukha ādi śabda ādi svabhāvam iti vyāpaka abhāvaḥ na ananya tvāt iti asiddhim āha yat śabda ādibhyaḥ ananyat tat śrotra ādi vṛtti grāhyam śabda ādi vat tathā ca sukha ādi svabhāvaḥ 
[I,143,ii]	na anyat ced ityādi yat śabda ādeḥ ananyat na tat tasya kāraṇam śabda ādi vat tathā ca sukha ādi iti viruddha vyāptam āha tatas ca abhyupeta bādhā yat uktam ityādinā hetu tva abhyupagamam āha sattvam śabda kāryam pratyākhyāya śabda ātmanā vyavatiṣṭhamānam rajaḥ tamasoḥ śabda bhāvāya vṛttim khyāpayati rajaḥ śabda kāryam pratyākhyāya ityādi sarvam pūrvavat ayam tu viśeṣaḥ rajaḥ sattva tamasoḥ śabda bhāvāya pravṛttim karoti tamaḥ sattva rajasoḥ śabda bhāvāya pravṛttim vyavasthāpayati iti 
[I,144,i]	atha ananya tve api kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iṣyate evam sati aniṣṭam idam āpadyate iti darśayan āha sattva ādīnām vā ityādi yat ekasmāt śabdāt abhinna svabhāvam tat abhinnam śabda svarūpa vat tathā ca sattva ādayaḥ yat anekasmāt sattva ādeḥ abhinna svabhāvam tat anekam sukha ādi vat tathā ca śabdaḥ iti svabhāvau prasaṅgau tad viparyayeṇa tu yat anekam na tat ekasmāt śabdāt abhinna svabhāvam yathā bahavaḥ pumāṃsaḥ tathā ca sattva ādi yat ekam na tat sattva ādibhyaḥ abhinna svabhāvam yathā ekā caitanya vyaktiḥ tathā ca śabdaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddhau tatas ca abhyupetam hīyate vikalpa arthaḥ vā aśabdaḥ iti kārya kṛt na vā iti atra yaḥ vā śabdaḥ 
[I,144,ii_I,144,iii]	ananya tve api na grāhyam iti anekāntam āha tad paramāṇuḥ iti śabda paramāṇuḥ tanmātra ādi vā iti śabda tamna atra ādi ādi śabdena ahaṅkāraḥ mahān pradhānam ca gṛhyate na ca ityādinā api anekāntam āha yatas kāryatva kāraṇa ādayaḥ na indriya viṣayāt bhidyante na ca indriya dhiyā avasīyante sarvā syāt citra ākāra iti yā api acitra ākāra iṣyate sā api citra tvāt sattva ādi samudāyasya na bhinnaḥ ityādinā sādhya abhāve hetoḥ abhāvam āha tad vaśena ityādi yat ākāram viṣaye jñānam utpadyate tad ākāraḥ sa viṣayaḥ pratīyate dṛṣṭam ca ityādinā hetum āha yat abhinna ākāram grahaṇam na tad citra viṣayam caitanya grahaṇam vyāpaka viruddhaḥ 
[I,145,i_I,145,iii]	viṣaya antaraḥ iti indriya antara viṣaya tvena abhimate nanu ca ityādi sarvatra abhede api sukha ādi jāteḥ na eka indriya tva prasaṅgaḥ yatas saṃsthāna viśiṣṭān sukha ādīn gṛhṇāti tat ca saṃsthānam viṣaya antare na asti aneka saṃsthāna bhedena iti nīla pīta ādi saṃsthāna bhedena na eka saṃsthāna anuvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā iti anena anuvṛttim adeka saṃsthāna abhāva vyavahārāya svabhāva anupalambham āha saḥ eva ityādi yatas saṃsthāna bhedāt bhinna indriya grāhya tvam śabda sparśa ādi jātīnām iṣṭam ekasyām eva ca rūpa jātau anekam saṃsthānam iṣṭam atas tat eva indriyān antyam prasajyate 
[I,145,iv]	na eva hi śabda lakṣaṇebhyaḥ iti pūrveṣām kāpilānām eka rūpāḥ eva sarvatra sukha ādayaḥ mādhavaḥ tu sarvatra teṣām bhedam icchati ye sukha ādayaḥ śabda ātmanā riṇamanti na sparśa ādi ātmanā te śabda lakṣaṇam trikam iti ucyante evam ye sparśa ātmanā eva pariṇamanti na artha antarātmanā te sparśa lakṣaṇam trikam iti evam anyatra api jñeyam nanu trayāṇām saṅghaḥ trikam tatra eka vacanena bhāvyam tat katham trikebhyaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ pratiśabdam anyat anyatrikam atas bahu tvātrikāṇām bahuvacanam anye tu anyathā trikāṇi vyācakṣate śabda paramāṇuḥ eva ekaḥ trikaḥ tri dravya ātmakaḥ sukha ādīnām eka tvena piṇḍībhūta tvāt īdṛśāḥ sarve śabda paramāṇavaḥ tathā sparśa ādi paramāṇavaḥ indriya paramāṇavaḥ ca veditavyāḥ te eva āsañcitāḥ prāk sṛṣṭeḥ pradhānam iti ucyante yadā tu sṛṣṭi kāle saṃhanyante tadā vikāra vyapadeśam bhajante ete ca śabda ādi lakṣaṇāḥ trikāḥ śrotra ādi lakṣaṇāḥ ca para sparataḥ bhinna jātīyāḥ eva iti mādhavasya matam 
[I,146,i]	anye api ca tasya prakriyā bhedaḥ yathā uktam rūpa ādimat pradhānam sa avayavam karma pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāraḥ ca anādiḥ vyākhyā bhedaḥ sva yūthyaiḥ mataḥ iti pūrveṣām kapila śiṣyāṇām pradhānam na rūpa ādimat śakyā ātmanā tatra rūpa ādayaḥ vyavasthitā na vyakti ātmanā niravayavam ca na ca karma pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ api tu pradhāna pūrvikā saṃsāraḥ ca śakya ātmanā prāk sṛṣṭeḥ na te vyakti ātmanā mādhavena tu sarvam anyathā abhyupagatam atas eva asau sāṅkhya nāśakaḥ na eva hi ityādinā eka indriya prasaṅgam pariharati ye sattva ādayaḥ śabde hebhyaḥ anyaḥ eva rūpa ādi ātmanā pariṇamanti iti kṛtvā 
[I,147,i_I,147,iii]	sa ca abhinnaḥ ityādinā ānantya prasaṅgam spaṣṭatareṇa iti sva arthaḥ eva tarap pratyayaḥ alpāt taram iti yathā kutas etat mādhava ukta kramasya dūṣya tvena aspaṣṭa tvāt tulya jātīye ca pratiyogini prakarṣa pratyaya vidhānāt atha vā para parikalpita spaṣṭa tva apekṣayā prakarṣa pratyayaḥ ekaika rūpāḥ iti kecid sukha svabhāvāḥ eva kecid śabda rūpāḥ eva evam kriyā ādi paramāṇavaḥ veditavyāḥ te ca sarvatra deśe kāle ca etena pradhāna dharmaka tvam āha pṛthak iti asaṃhatāḥ samāna jātīyaiḥ asambaddhāḥ viprakīrṇāḥ iti arthaḥ te evaṃvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pradhānam iti ucyante jātitaḥ sarva gatānām iti na ekam eva paramāṇu dravyam sarva gatam asti kim tu te eva paramāṇavaḥ aparisaṅkhyātāḥ sarvatra santi eka jātīyāḥ teṣām pradhānam iti ākhyātāḥ kariṣyante iti darśayati 
[I,147,iv]	yadi evam te paramāṇavaḥ atīndriyā na ca taiḥ vyatiriktam kāryam ārabhyate tat katham kārya rūpāḥ lakṣyante iti āha kārya rūpāḥ tu ityādi yathā paraspareṇa asambaddhāḥ tuṣāra leśāḥ viyataḥ patantaḥ na upalakṣyante paraspara saṃyuktāḥ tu harita patra ādau patitāḥ pratyakṣībhavanti tathā paramaṇavaḥ samprayoga viśeṣāt iti viśeṣa grahaṇam dvi paramāṇu ādikasya samprayogasya vyavaccheda artham sva jāti anatikrameṇa iti śabda ādi jāti anatikrameṇa iti śabda paramāṇavaḥ eva hi saṃhatāḥ śrotra indriya grāhyaḥ śandaḥ bhavati tathā sukha paramāṇavaḥ eva sampiṇḍitāḥ sva saṃvedyam sukham bhavati na tu saṃhatāḥ vijātīya kārya rūpa tām pratipadyante 
[I,148,i_I,148,ii]	syāt etat trirūpa tve api paramāṇūnām eka ākārā buddhiḥ pariṇāma viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati iti āha aṇūnām tu ityādi sukha ādi vyatirekeṇa iti sukha ādi a ākāram antareṇa iti arthaḥ yābhid na iti eka rūpā kutas na yujyate iti āha aneka svābhāvyaḥ iti atha vā bhinnam anekam svābhāvyam asya iti bahuvrīhiḥ svabhāvaḥ eva svābhāvyam vartamāna sāmīpya vat jñāna ākāra vaśena hi viṣaya svabhāvaḥ avadhāryate yadi punar anyathā sthite api viṣaye tad upagrāhi jñānam anya ākāram iṣyate na tad vaśena viṣaya avadhāraṇam syāt tat ca iṣṭam tat etena yat eka ākāram jñānam na tad bhinna aneka svabhāva viṣayam caitanya jñāna vat tathā ca śabda jñānam iti vyāpaka viruddham āha 
[I,149,i]	kim kāraṇam iti trayaḥ saṃyuktāḥ eka svābhāvyena pariṇaṃsyanti atas siddha sādhanam iti abhiprāyaḥ vijāti pariṇāmaḥ vilakṣaṇa aneka svabhāvānām abhinna eka svabhāva āpattiḥ jāti bhedāt iti kārya kāraṇa jāti bheda prasaṅgāt iti arthaḥ tatas ca asat kārya vādaḥ syāt iti abhyupeta hāniḥ atha vā jāti bhedāt sukha ādīnām na hi te bhinnāḥ samprayoge api eka svabhāva tayā pariṇantum arhanti sva jāti anatikrameṇa kārya ārambhāt nanu ca bhinnāḥ api guḍa udaka ādayaḥ pānaka ādi eka svabhāva tām pratipadyante iti āha eka śabda vācyā aḥ tu ityādi pānaka ādayaḥ api na eva paramārthataḥ santi kevalam vyavahāra lāghava artham te eva guḍa ādayaḥ ekena śandena vyapariśyante 
[I,149,ii_I,149,iii]	yat utkaṭam iti yathā su alpa saktuḥ pracura lavaṇa saṃsarge lavaṇa rasaḥ eva gṛhyate jighṛkṣitam vā iti yathā śvabhiḥ pramamātanau bhakṣya svabhāva tvam eva upalabhyate tathā śabda ādau api veditavyam śabda grahaṇa nirapekṣa iti śabdaḥ hi na eka guṇa ātmakaḥ kim tarhi triguṇa ātmakaḥ tathā ca na gṛhṇāti iti tat nirapekṣā 
[I,150,i]	saḥ eva na ātmā ekaḥ asya iti śabdasya eka deśena viṣaya tve aneka ātmaka tva nivṛttim asambhāvayan pṛcchati kim kāraṇam iti indriya arthe viśiṣṭaḥ hi iti kāraṇam āha aneka rūpe hi iti śabda tva guṇa tva sattva ādi rūpa bhedena sa ca ekaḥ eva iti sukha ādīnām anyatamaḥ tat etena yat śrotreṇa na gṛhyate na sa tasya arthaḥ caitanya vat sāmānya dharma jñeya tva ādi vat ca tathā ca rūpa dvayam iti vyāpaka abhāvam āha evam indriya antare api vācyam saktu lavaṇa saṃsarge tu gṛhyate eva saktu rasaḥ tathā hi anyādṛśaḥ kevalasya lavaṇasya rasaḥ upalabhyate anyādṛśaḥ saktu saṃsarge samānaḥ ca sparśa ādiṣu iti tulyaḥ etena tam eva eka indriya prasaṅgam āha 
[I,150,ii_I,151,i]	katham punar asmin api pakṣe doṣaḥ yāvatā śabda ādiṣu guṇānām bhedaḥ abhyupetaḥ satyam abhyupagataḥ sa tu vyakti bhedaḥ na svabhāva bhedaḥ sarvatra sukha ādīnām prakāśaka tva ādi rūpasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt na ca vyakti bheda mātreṇa indriya antara grāhya tvam yuktam mā bhūt śabda ādīnām vyakti bhedena ānantyāt anantam indriyam iti nanu śabda ādi bhāvena api bhedaḥ na etat asti trikāṇām hi śabda ādi bhāvena bhedaḥ na tu sukha ādīnām trirūpa tva abhyupagamāt iti āha ayuktaḥ ityādi tasmāt varam ityādi nanu siddhānta vyāpādāt ayam api duṣṭaḥ eva pakṣaḥ mādhava pakṣāt alpa doṣa tvāt asya iti abhiprāyeṇa evam uktam iti doṣaḥ 
[I,151,ii_I,151,iii]	vṛtti pramāṇasya avidhānataḥ iti bāhyeṣu artheṣu indriyam vyavasāyam kurute tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute yathā ca indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute evam mānasam vyavasāyam indriyam saṃvedayate iti anena granthena paraspara saṃvedanam vṛtti dvayasya uktam tasya pratyakṣa tvena avidhānataḥ na sarva prameya viṣayam pramāṇam uktam iti avyāpitā lakṣaṇasya syāt etat āgama anumānabhyām tad ubhaya saṃvedanam atas ayam adoṣaḥ iti āha antareṇa ityādi yadā sva santati patitām vṛttim saṃvedayate tadā liṅga ābhāt na anumānam upadeśa abhāvāt na āgamaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣam eva idam yuktam iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[I,152,i_I,152,ii]	nanu śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ ca iti atra caśabdaḥ manaḥ vṛtti saṅgraha arthaḥ iti atas manaḥ vṛtteḥ tāvat pratyakṣe antarbhāvaḥ indriya vṛttayaḥ tu na eva manaḥ vṛtti saṃvedikāḥ śāstreṇa uktāḥ tathā hi yathā ca indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute evam mānasam vyavasāyam indriyam saṃvedayate iti vedayatiḥ ayam lābha arthaḥ curādau paṭhyate yathā ca indriya vyavasāyam manaḥ vyavasāyaḥ jānāti evam mānasam vyavasāyam indriya vṛttiḥ prāpnoti iti arthaḥ na etat asti caśabdaḥ tāvat iha pramāṇa antara samuccaya arthe anumānam pramāṇam śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ ca iti manaḥ vṛtti samuccaya arthe tu caśabde aviśeṣeṇa sarvasyāḥ manaḥ vṛtteḥ pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa anupādānāt yaḥ api āha manasā adhiṣṭhitā iti manasā saha śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam iti arthaḥ iti tasya api eṣaḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,152,iii]	prāpti arthe api anyaḥ saṃvedanāt ayuktaḥ prāptiḥ hi abhinnaka ālayeḥ eva bhavati na bhinna kālayoḥ tatra yadi prāpti prasiddhi artham indriya vyavasāyena manaḥ vyavasāyasya yaugapadyam iṣyate tasya viṣayaḥ bāhya arthaḥ syāt indriya vyavasāyaḥ vā yadi pūrvaḥ dvāra dvāri bhāvaḥ na syāt saha utpannasya upakāri tvā yogāt anupakāriṇaḥ ca dvāra bhāva anupapatteḥ anyathā manaḥ vyavasāyaḥ api indriya vyavasāyasya dvāram syāt yadi ca manasaḥ bāhye arthe sākṣāt vṛttiḥ evam sati itareṣām indriyāṇām tatra vṛttiḥ apārthikā prāpnoti manasā eva puruṣa arthasya sampādita tvāt artha indriya vyavasāyaḥ tasya viṣayaḥ evam api aviṣaya nimittaḥ viṣayī syāt tat ca ayuktam na nimittasya viṣaya tvam upapadyate anyathā manaḥ vyavasāyaḥ api indriya vyavasāyasya viṣayaḥ syāt 
[I,153,i_I,153,ii]	yaḥ tu manaḥ vṛttyā api indriya vṛtteḥ saṃvedanam icchan āha na eva idam paraspara saṃvedanam anubhava ātmakam uktam kim tarhi prāpti svabhāvam yathā indriya vyavasāyaḥ manaḥ vyavasāyena saṃvedyate prāpyate evam mānasam vyavasāyam indriyam saṃvedayate prāpnoti tena saha saṅgacchate iti arthaḥ iti saḥ api anena eva nirākṛtaḥ kim ca tasya apratyakṣa upalambhasya artha dṛṣṭiḥ api na prasidhyati yathoktam prāk tasmāt ayuktā prāpti artha kalpanā 
[I,153,iii]	yaḥ api āha śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ bāhye arthe pratyakṣam pramāṇam tasmin tu indriya vyavasite arthe manaḥ paścāt vyavasāyam kurutaḥ iti arthaḥ anyathā yadi indriya vṛttau eva mānasaḥ vyavasāyaḥ syāt anu śabda prayogaḥ anarthakaḥ syāt insriya vṛtteḥ kenacid prāk ananubhūta tvāt atideśaḥ api upakāra mātra atideśāt upapadyate etat uktam bhavati yathā indriya upakāra apekṣam bāhye arthe manaḥ pravartate evam mana aupakāra apekṣam indriyam api iti tasya api etat apratyakṣa upalambhasya na artha dṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati iti anena eva apāstam tasmāt paraspara saṃvedanam eva atra arthāt 
[I,154,i]	na eṣa doṣaḥ iti na eva idam vṛtti saṃvedanam pramāṇam iṣyate smārtam hi tat yathā kāma krodha dveṣa bhaya ādayaḥ smaryante tathā indriya vṛttayaḥ manaḥ vṛttiḥ ca manasā granthaḥ ca evam nīyate bāhyeṣu indriyam vyavasāyam kurute pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurutaḥ iti anantaram smārtam yathā ca indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute anantara uktam evam mānasam vyavasāyam indriyam saṃvedayate smārayati iti arthaḥ aneka artha tvāt dhātūnām dvitīyaḥ ca hetu maṇṇit iha veditavyaḥ indriyam hi smaraṇa anukūlam manasaḥ upakāram kurvat tat prayuṅktaḥ iva iti smaraṇena eva ca vṛtti viṣayīkaraṇe artha dṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati iti manyate tat evam vṛtti grahaṇasya apramāṇa tvāt na tasya asaṅgrahān nyūna tvam 
[I,155,i_I,155,ii^1]	yathā uktam iti vṛtti saṃvedanasya smārta tva jñāpakam āha smṛti pratyakṣa vyavasāya viśeṣaḥ iti viśeṣa śabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambadhyate nanu ca anya arthaḥ eva ayam granthaḥ śāstre upanyastaḥ tat katham anena smārta tvam jñāpyate tathā hi kim indriyam anobhyām saha eva bāhyeṣu artheṣu vyavasāyāḥ kriyante āhosvit saha na eva kriyante iti saṃśayaḥ idam uktam bāhyeṣu artheṣu indriyam vyavasāyam kurute tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute kasmāt asti hi ayam smṛti pratyakṣa vyavasāya viśeṣaḥ iti etat uktam bhavati smṛti pratyakṣa vyavasāya viśeṣaḥ asti na ayam prasiddhataraḥ apahnotum śakyate na ca ubhayoḥ bāhya artha pravṛttau ayam upapadyate yadi hi bāhye arthe manaḥ pravartate na indriya vṛttiṣu 
[I,155,ii^2]	tadā tāḥ manaḥ vṛttibhiḥ anadhiṣṭhitāḥ pauruṣeyeṇa caitanyena asampṛktāḥ apratyayāḥ syuḥ tatas ca katham pratyakṣam pramāṇam ucyeran na hi apratyayāḥ vṛttayaḥ pratyakṣam pramāṇam bhavanti pratyakṣa abhāvāt ca smṛtiḥ api tad pūrvikā na syāt yadā tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute tadā smṛti pratyakṣa vyavasāya viśeṣaḥ upapadyate tathā hi sāmprate kāle bāhyeṣu artheṣu indriya vyavasāyam pravṛttam anvadhyavasyati manasi indriya vyavasāyaḥ sva viṣaya ābhāsaḥ manaḥ vyavasāyena sampṛktaḥ pauruṣeṇa pratyayena sa pratyayaḥ bhavati evam pratyakṣa vyavasāyaḥ tasya indriyasya bhavati pratyakṣa tvam tasya indriya vyavasāyasya bhavati iti arthaḥ kevalasya tu pratyakṣa vyavasāyāt paścāt smṛti vyavasāyaḥ manasaḥ bhavati iti tathā ca uktam kevalam tu atīta anāgatayoḥ kālayoḥ pravartate iti 
[I,156,i^1]	nanu ca indriya vyavasāya sahitasya bāhye api arthe pravṛttasya sāmprate kāle manasaḥ pratyakṣa vyavasāyaḥ bhaviṣyati kevalasya tu paścāt smṛti vyavasāyaḥ na etat asti evam bāhya artha grahaṇe sati dvayoḥ api eka artha kāri tvāt ānarthakyam indriyāṇām syāt tathā hi uktam na eka artha kāriṇoḥ indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam iti yatas evam smṛti pratyakṣa vyavasāya viśeṣaḥ bāhya arthe pravṛttau manasaḥ na upapadyate tasmāt tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute na bāhyeṣu artheṣu iti tat evam na indriya m anobhyām saha bāhyeṣu artheṣu vyavasāyāḥ kriyante iti asya arthasya pratipādānāya asti hi ayam iti ādiḥ granthaḥ upanyastaḥ 
[I,156,i^2]	na tu vṛtti saṃvedanasya smārta tva pratipādānāya tat katham tat smārta tva jñāpaka tvena uktaḥ iti na ca idam vṛtti saṃvedanam sāṅkhyasya smārtam jñānam abhīṣṭam anubhūta pūrvam hi smaryate vṛtti saṃvedanam ca idam aprūva ca idam apūrvaḥ eva anubhavaḥ tat katham idam para abhiprāyeṇa uktam smārtam hi tad vṛtti saṃvedanam iti parasya gati antara abhāvāt tathā hi vṛtti upalabhyaḥ tāvat niyatam abhyupeyaḥ anyathā tad anupalambhe artha upalambhaḥ api na syāt iti andhamūkam jagat syāt na ca vṛtti saṃvedanam pratyakṣa ādiṣu antarbhavati atas gati antara abhāvāt idam api asat uttaram brūyāt iti āśaṅkya evam uktam 
[I,157,i_I,157,iii]	indriya vṛttau tu anataram iti indriya vṛtti grahaṇena manaḥ vṛttiḥ api gṛhyate smārtaḥ na ananubhūta tvāt ityādinā yat ananubhūtam na tatra smārtaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati tat yathā santāna antarīyeṣu ananubhūteṣu ananubhūtāḥ ca indriya vṛttayaḥ iti kāraṇa viruddham āha yugapad dve ityādi yadi smārta tva prasiddhaye hetoḥ asiddha tvam iṣyate evam hi saha bhūbhyām indriya manaḥ vyavasāyābhyām parasparam saṃvedane tāsu smārtaḥ pratyayaḥ sambhavati anantaram 
[I,158,i]	evam ca iti viṣayaḥ indriya vyavasāyaḥ grāhyaḥ viṣayiṇaḥ grāhakasya manaḥ vyavasāyasya manaḥ vyavasāyaḥ api viṣayaḥ grāhyaḥ viṣayiṇaḥ grāhakasya indriya vyavasāyasya paraspara saṃvedane hi tayoḥ apekṣayā viṣaya tvam ca bhavati viṣaya tvam ca tayoḥ nimitta nimitti bhāvaḥ iṣyate parasparam na hi anyathā viṣaya viṣayi tvam sambhavati na ca yugapad utpannayoḥ nimitta nimitta tvam upapadyate 
[I,158,ii^1]	sa ca iti abhyupeti doṣa antaram āha yaḥ asau indirya vṛtti anubhavaḥ yat pūrvakaḥ smārtaḥ pratyayaḥ sa pramāṇam na uktaḥ iti sā eva nyūna tā kāma ādiṣu tarhi katham smārtaḥ iti āha sva saṃvedya tvāt ityādi etena etat sūcayati kāma ādi upanyāsaḥ sva bādhāya kṛtyā utthāpanam tathā hi asmākam sva saṃvedya tvena kāma ādīnām abhyupagamāt tatra smārtaḥ sambhavati bhavataḥ tu tathā teṣām anabhyupagamāt tad asambhavaḥ eva atha sva saṃvittiḥ abhyupeyate sā api tarhi lakṣaṇena asaṅgṛhīta iti sā eva nyūna tā nanu ca śāstreṇa smārta tvam pratipāditam iti āha andha padam eva etat iti yathā andha padasya adarśana pūrvaḥ vinyāsaḥ tathā asya api pramāṇena aparicchidya abhidhānāt atha vān dhāni padāni anunmīlita arthāni yatra vākye 
[I,158,ii^2_I,159,i]	tat tathā uktam tathā hi ityādinā andha padha pada tvam darśayati indriya arthe api smārtaḥ na sambhavati yaḥ anubhūtaḥ kim punar vṛttiṣu ananubhūtāsu iti api śabdasya arthaḥ syāt etat tasmin tu indriya vyavasāye sati bāhyaḥ eva arthe manaḥ anuvyavasāyam kurute iti śāstra arthaḥ tatas ananubhūta tvam asiddham iti āha hāniḥ vā ityādi hāniḥ śāstrasya anya darśane smaraṇam indriya vṛttyā anubhūta tvāt manasā ca smaryamāṇa tvāt tat ca ayuktam na hi devadatta anubhūtam yajñadattaḥ smarati sva mate tarhi katham indriya jñāna anubhūtam manasā smaryate iti ced parasya eva ayam doṣaḥ yasya idam matam na anyena anubhūtam anyaḥ smarati iti asmākam tu eka santatau jñāna antara anubhūtam api smaryate iti samayaḥ iti adoṣaḥ ananubhūte vā smārtaḥ iti atha manasā eva anubhūtasya smaraṇam iṣyate evam sati ananubhūte arthe smaraṇam syāt tasya mansā pūrvam ananubhūta tvāt dvitīye kṣaṇe mānasaḥ iṣyate iti atas indriya vṛtti sahajaḥ iti āha 
[I,160,i]	yat uktam ityādi śātraḥ uktam kim bāhyeṣu artheṣu indriyam anobhyām saha vyavasāyāḥ na iti ucyate kasmāt na eka artha kāriṇoḥ indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam iti etat uktam bhavati yadi indriya m anobhyām dvābhyām api bāhyasya arthasya grahaṇa lakṣaṇam kāryam eka artha kāri tvam iṣyate evam sati sāmarthyam indriyāṇām na syāt arthavat tā na syāt iti arthaḥ tayoḥ api bāhya artha grahaṇam atra ekārtha kāri tvam bāhya artha grahaṇāt ca dvābhyām api indriyāṇām arthavat tā na syāt katham yadi tāvat viṣaye pravartamānam manaḥ indriya vṛtti kṛtam anugraham na apekṣate evam sati indriyāṇām sarvathā eva ānarthakyam syāt manasā eva bāhya artha upasaṃhārāt puruṣasya upabhoga siddheḥ indriya vṛttayaḥ ca bāhya artha ābhāsāḥ mānasaiḥ avyavasāyaiḥ anadhyavasitāḥ taiḥ asampṛktāḥ apratyayāḥ syuḥ 
[I,160,ii]	yat ca idam dvāra dvāri vicāre paṭhyate manasi ekībhūtān indrita vyavasāyān puruṣaḥ cetayate na tu indriya vyavasāyaiḥ manaḥ vyavasāyān iti tasmāt manaḥ eva dvāri dvārāṇi indriyāṇi iti tat api vyāhanyate yugapad eka artha kāri tve dvayoḥ api dvāra dvāri tva prasaṅgāt andha ādīnām api ca rūpa ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam syāt 
[I,160,iii]	atha api indriya kṛtam anugraham apekṣya bāhye arthe manaḥ pravartate na kevalam asāmarthyāt iti ucyate evam api na eva indriyāṇām sāmarthyam syāt yasmāt evam iṣyamāṇe sa pratyayāyāḥ vṛtteḥ asambhavaḥ syāt indriya vṛttau pradīpa prabhāyām iva hi sahakāri tvena avasthatāyām manaḥ eva bāhye arthe grahaṇāya pravartate tatra yathā pradīpa prabhāyām satyām cakṣuṣaḥ vṛttiḥ pradīpa prabhā tu sahakāriṇi eva kevalam tathā indriya vṛttau manasaḥ bāhye arthe grahaṇāya vṛttiḥ indriya vṛttiḥ tu sahakāriṇi eva sā ca manaḥ vṛttyā gṛhyamāṇā sampṛktā tayā apratyayā eva sarvadā syāt indriya vyavasāyānām ca manasi ekībhāvāt arthavat tvam uktam na anyathā tena te yadi manaḥ vyavasāyaiḥ anuvyavasīyante evam manasi ekībhavantaḥ pauruṣeṇa saṃvedyante tatas ca tena sampṛktāḥ tad rūpa tām iva āpannāḥ prāmāṇyam pratipadyante anyathā teṣām prāmāṇyam eva na syāt 
[I,161,i_I,161,iii]	yeṣām api apratyayā vṛttiḥ prāmāṇyena abhimatā sa pratyayā tu phalam teṣām api yathā uktena prakāreṇa sa pratyayāyāḥ vṛtteḥ asambhavāt phala abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt ca pramāṇasya api abhāvaḥ na hi niṣphalam pramāṇam yuktam iti eke cakṣuḥ manasoḥ dvāra dvāri bhāvāt na ete eka artha kāriṇī kalpayitum asmākam sāmarthyam asti yugapad eka artha kāri tve dvayoḥ api dvāra dvāri tva prasaṅgāt iti anye na eṣa doṣaḥ ityādinā etat pratipādayati na iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ tena na saha vyavasāya kriyā mātram pratiṣidhyate kim tu niyamavatī yā saha vyavasāya kriyā sā pratiṣidhyate manasaḥ smārta adhika vyavasāya pradarśana artham na saha eva api tu paścāt api smārtaḥ vyavasāyaḥ adhikaḥ manasā kriyate iti 
[I,162,i]	saha tu siddhaḥ eva ityādinā etat āha niyama rahitām saha vyavasāya kriyām prati praśnaḥ eva na upapadyate tasyāḥ prāk eva jñāta tvāt tasmāt gamyate kim saha eva kriyante pṛthakkriyante eva iti evam ayam praśnaḥ pravṛttaḥ na tu kim saha kriyante āhosvit na saha kriyante iti kutas etat saha tu siddhaḥ eva vyavasāye paśnaḥ iti āha sāmprate kālaḥ ityādi śāstre śnotra ādīnām sva viṣaya viniveśam sāmprata kāla vṛtti tvam ca pratipādya evam uktam tathā manaḥ sarva artheṣu traikālyam pravartate bāhyeṣu artheṣu sāmprate kāle kenacid indriyeṇa yuktam yadā manaḥ bhavati tadā pratyayavatī vṛttiḥ indriyasya bhavati kevalam tu atīta anāgatayoḥ ityādi prāk uktam paścāt ayam paśnaḥ kṛtaḥ atra kenacid indriyeṇa yuktam yadā iti vacanāt siddhaḥ pūrvam eva saha vyavasāyaḥ tatas niyamavatīm saha vyavasāya kriyām ārabhya paśnaḥ pratyuttaram api ca na eka artha kāriṇoḥ indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam asti iti tat pratiṣedham eva prati iti gamyate tatas na śāstra hāniḥ 
[I,163,i_I,163,ii]	tasya vyāghātaḥ iti katham kṛtvā yatas yathā ca indriya vyavasāyaḥ ityādinā paraspara vṛtti saṃvedanam pratipāditam avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam artha antara kalpane hi yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt tatas ca na kalpayitavyam indriya pravṛtti sahajaḥ bāhye arthe manasaḥ anubhavaḥ paścāt smārtaḥ iti apārthikā prāpnoti iti doṣa antaram āha manasā ityādinā atra eva hetum tri kāla viṣayam sarva artham ca manaḥ iti uktam tat ced abāhya arthe sākṣāt pravartate tena eva puṃsaḥ arthaḥ kṛtaḥ iti śrotra ādīnām vaiyarthyam syāt tatas ca na eva tad ātmanā prakṛteḥ pariṇatiḥ syāt pauruṣa autsukya nivṛttaye hi tasyāḥ pariṇāmaḥ iṣyate anyathā prāpta kaivalye api puṃsi syāt iti 
[I,163,iii_I,164,i]	sat samprayogaḥ ityādi asya sambandhaḥ atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti prastuti āha tasya nimitta parīṣṭiḥ tasya dharmasya upalabdhi nimittāni pramāṇāni parīkṣyante tatra pratyakṣeṇa tāvat dharmaḥ na upalabhyate iti darśayan āha sat samprayogaḥ ityādi sataḥ satā vā samprayogaḥ iti vigrahaḥ sampragrahaṇam samprati utkarṣeṇa ca yaḥ yogaḥ tasya jñāpana artham evam ca ātmā ādibhiḥ api yaḥ yogaḥ sa saṃskāraḥ upagṛhītaḥ bhavati anyathā sat yogaḥ iti etāvat eva brūyāt samprayogaḥ indriyāṇām arthena sambandhaḥ sannikarṣaḥ vyāpāra atiśayaḥ vā yatra utpanne buddhiḥ utpadyate sat samprayogaḥ iti asya indriyāṇām iti anena sambandhaḥ puruṣasya iti asya api buddhi janma iti anena indriya śabdena manaḥ api gṛhyate tena ātma manaḥ samprayogāt yat ātma viṣayam buddhi janma tasya api pratyakṣa tvam vihitam bhavati buddhi janma iti ca karmadhārayaḥ ṣaṣṭhī tatpuruṣaḥ vā yadā karmadhā arayaḥ tadā janma viśiṣṭā buddhiḥ pratyakṣam buddhiḥ hi janmanā eva viṣayam prakāśayati na tu janma vyatirekeṇa vyāpāra antaram tasyāḥ samasti kṣaṇika tvāt iti jñāpana artham janma grahaṇam yadā tu ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ tadā buddhi viśiṣṭam janma pratyakṣam 
[I,164,ii_I,165,i]	tatra sat iti asat vyudāsāya ityādinā yat samprayogāt gamyate na tasya pratyāyanāya sat śabdaḥ upādeyaḥ samprayoga vat tathā ca adat vyudāsaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddham āha sataḥ eva iti dvi ṣaṭha tvāt tasya anyatara abhāve asambhavāt nanu sataḥ eva iti eva kārāt eva niyamasya gata tvāt niyamāt iti na vācyam atha etat ucyate eva śrutiḥ apārthikā syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ niyamasya eva hi svarūpam eva śabdena dyotyate vākya bhedam ca kṛtha evam vyākhyeyam sataḥ eva iti yaḥ ayam niyamaḥ asmāt niyamāt sataḥ eva samprayogaḥ bhavati iti atha ca niyamān na sat prayogaḥ yuktaḥ iti sambandhaḥ kartavyaḥ na eva sat prayogaḥ yuktaḥ iti evam vā 
[I,165,ii]	pratiyogi atha ityādi anyathārtha tvāt sat śabdasya siddha sādhanam āha kim artham punar prāk sataḥ eva iti bruvatā ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ darśitaḥ idānīm tu kena samprayogaḥ iti tṛtīyā samāsaḥ samāsa antare api eṣa doṣaḥ iti sūcanā artham tathā hi śabareṇa sati samprayoge na asati iti bruvatā karmadhārayaḥ ayam iti vyākhyātam tatra api ca ayam anivāryaḥ doṣaḥ yat saptam yeṣā nimitta arthā syāt yasya ca bhāvena bhāva lakṣaṇam iti anena vā na ca asataḥ nimitta tvam lakṣaṇa tvam ca sambhavati tatas ca yadi samprayogena samittena buddhi janma bhavati tad bhāvena vā tādbhāvaḥ lakṣyate evam sati samprayogaḥ san iti etat gamyate eva 
[I,165,iii]	syāt etat satyam gamyate tathā api yeṣām pareṣām asat kalpanā atīta an āgata viṣayam yogi jñānam asatī api samprayoge bhavati iti tat nirākaraṇa artham sat grahaṇam iti ayuktam etat saptam yat tena eva samprayoga śabdena sat artha avyabhicāriṇā asyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ nivārita tvāt api ca asmākam yogi jñām sat viṣayam eva prāk eva ākhyātam 
[I,166,i^1]	yat api atīta anāgata viṣayam yoginām jñānam ucyate tasya api upacārāt atīta anāgata viṣaya tvam abhyupeyate paramārthataḥ tu tat api vartamāna viṣayam eva katham kṛtvā pratyutpannaḥ hi bhāvaḥ atītānām hetu pratyayānām sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā upakāryaḥ yat anantaram yasya utpādaḥ tasya sākṣāt yebhyaḥ tu vyavadhānena teṣām pāramparyeṇa anāgatānām ca asau bhāvānām upakārakaḥ ye anantaram tatas bhavanti bhāvāḥ teṣām sākṣāt tat uttara kāla bhāvinām tu pāramparyeṇa yat ca asya atīta upakārya tvam anāhata upakāri tvam ca vyavahitam itarat ca saḥ asya svabhāvaḥ tam ca pratyutpannam bhāvam bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta jena jñānena yoginaḥ paricchindantaḥ sarva ātmanā eva paricchin danti tasya niravayava tvāt evam paricchinne tasmin samādhi vyutthitānām yoginām ye tasya bhāvasya upakārakāḥ upakāryāḥ ca arthāḥ atīta anāgatāḥ 
[I,166,i^2]	tat pratyavamarśīni jñānāni avisaṃvādīni bhāvanā āmaya jñāna viśeṣa balāt upajāyante yaiḥ atīta anāgata padārtha vyavasthā kriyate tat evam atīta anāgara artha viṣayam pratyavamarśa jñānam yogi jñānasya kāryam iti kāraṇe kārya upacārāt tat api atīta anāgata viṣayam iti ucyate bhavatu nāma tat nirviṣayam eva paramārthataḥ atīta anāgatayoḥ asattvāt tathā api tasya sphuṭa atīta anāgata artha pratibhāsasya avikalpa tvāt avisaṃvādi tvāt ca pratyakṣa tvam aviruddham eva yathā hi bhavadbhiḥ codanā janitāyāḥ buddheḥ anāgata dharma viṣayāyāḥ rūpāgrahe api avisaṃvādāt prāmāṇyam iṣyate tathā asmābhiḥ api yathā uktāt kāraṇāt tasya pratyakṣa tvam sphuṭa atīta ādi artha pratibhāsi tvam punar tasya nirvikalpa tvam avisaṃvādi tvam ca yoga balāt karma devatā ādi adhiṣṭhāna balāt satya svapna darśana vat tatas niṣprayojanam sat iti etat akāryam eva 
[I,168,i^1]	nanu ca na eva idam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam kim tu dharmaḥ kaiścid yogi jñāna pratyakṣa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ uktaḥ tat pratiṣedha artham idam uktam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ dharmaḥ na pratyakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ kutas yasmāt tat īdṛśam pratyakṣam bhaviṣyan ca dharmaḥ na jñāna kāle asti tatas animittam atīndriyasya arthasya avabodhane vidyamāna upalambhana tvāt tasya tat pūrvaka tvāt ca anumāna ādi api dharmasya animittam bhavati tasmāt codanā lakṣaṇaḥ eva arthaḥ dharmaḥ iti etat atra pradhānam vidheyam na tu pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa pradhānam idam pratyakṣa sūtram pratyakṣasya siddha tvāt anuvāda mātram eva idam kriyate iti tat ayuktam 
[I,168,i^2]	asiddha tvāt pramāṇānām etat ca prāk eva pratipāditam api ca yadi siddha tvāt pratyakṣasya na anena lakṣaṇam vidhīyate kim tadi iti etāvat eva dharmasya animitta tvam evam sati pratyakṣam animittam vidyamāna upalambhana tvāt iti etāvat eva vaktavyam syāt etat svarūpa nirdeśe sati evaṃlakṣaṇam pratyakṣam iti svarūpa vijñānāt tasya animitta tvam sidhyati na anyathā iti yadi svarūpa nirdeśam antareṇa tasya svarūpam na jñāyate na tarhi tat siddham tatas ca tasya lakṣaṇa vidheḥ eva āśritaḥ iti na dūṣaṇāt mucyase 
[I,169,i_I,169,ii]	viśiṣṭaḥ akṣasya kathyatām iti indriyasya hi viśiṣṭaḥ eva viṣayaḥ pratiyogī yathā cakṣuṣaḥ rūpam iti evamādi atas evam vaktum yuktam rūpa ādi samprayogaḥ iti atha api syāt iti ātma indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt jñānam utpadyate sa ca rūpa ādi śabdaiḥ na śakyate vaktum atas tat pratītaye sat grahaṇam iti indriyāṇām iti tu vacanam upalakṣaṇa artham kākebhyaḥ dadhi rakṣyatam iti yathā iti manyate 
[I,170,i_I,170,ii]	sat mātram ityādinā pūrvakam eva sādhanam sūcayati syāt etat asati tasya āvṛttiḥ iti asat etat tathā hi asatām api mṛgatṛṣṇā ādīnām samprayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tatas ca asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti āha ye api hi ityādi pratyakṣa ābhāsa viṣaya tvāt pratyakṣa ābhāsāḥ atas eva asantaḥ tatas na taiḥ saha kasyacid samprayogaḥ tatas ca na tat niṣedhāya sat grahaṇam yuktam iti 
[I,170,iii]	syāt etat asati sat grahaṇe dvi candra ādi jñānasya api bhrāntasya pratyakṣatā syāt atas tat nivṛttaye sat grahaṇam iti na etat asti tasya samprayoga grahaṇena eva nivarta tvāt iti uktam etat yadi tarhi taiḥ na samprayogaḥ katham jala ādi pratibhāsam vijñānam iti āha deśa viśeṣe tu ityādi maru jāṅgala ādau deśa viśeṣe tatra api na sarvadā kim tarhi yadā sūrya raśmibhiḥ santāpitāḥ bhavanti tadā kāraṇam bhavanti na anyadā yat āha sūrya upatāpāt iti avyapadeśyāḥ iti sva lakṣaṇasya avyapadeśya tvāt krameṇa iti prāk indriya jñānam tatas sādṛśya avasayī manaḥ vikalpaḥ tatas jala ādi sadṛśa vastu smaraṇam tad antaram tat eva idam iti bhrāntam manaḥ vijñānam sāmānya ālambi bhavati vinā api tad arthena iti jala ādinā kalpitena samanantara pratyaya viśeṣa vaśena eva utpatteḥ 
[I,171,i_I,171,ii]	atha ityādinā viśiṣṭaḥ eva vyutpatti samāśrayeṇa kathitaḥ iti darśayati yaḥ vā yasya iti praśaṃsāyām api sat śabdaḥ vartat sat puruṣaḥ iti yathā tat sīdati anyat api atra iti yathā hi asti arthaḥ sat śabdaḥ indriya artha vyabhicārāt na alam indriya artha pratyāyanāya tathā sadana arthaḥ api tathā hi inndriya antara arthāḥ api rajaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ indriye sīdanti prabhṛti śabdena karṇāt imālā ādayaḥ gṛhyante añjana ādīnām api ca upakāri tvāt praśasta tā vidyate atas tat samprayoge api pratyakṣatā syāt 
[I,171,iii]	nanu yaḥ yasmin indriye sīdati anyatra āvṛtteḥ iti vacanāt tasya eva indriyasya viṣaya bhāva upagamana lakṣaṇam sadnam atra vivakṣitam praśaṃsā arthaḥ api atra yogya tvena uktaḥ yogya tvam ca iha indriyasya viṣaya bhāva upagamana sāmarthyam eva vaktum iṣṭam na ca evam prakāram sadana ādi rajaḥ prabhṛtīnām asti tat kutas ayam prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,172,i]	uktam atra asti arthaḥ iva sat śabdaḥ sadana ādi arthaḥ api na alam viśeṣa pratipādanāya iti yadi ca evam prakāram iha sadana ādya abhipretam tatas samprayoga śandena na arthaḥ sati yat abuddhi janma tat pratyakṣam iti etāvatā eva samprayogasya api labdha tvāt na hi tena vinā evaṃvidham sadana ādi tvam atyā sambhavati tasmāt saṃśleṣaḥ sadanam upakāri tvam ca praśasta tvam eṣṭavyam tatas ca rajaḥ prabhṛtiṣu prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,172,ii]	kim punar atra aniṣṭam yadi hi rajaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi indriya samprayogāt rajaḥ prabhṛti viṣayā buddhiḥ na upajāyate na eva ayam doṣaḥ buddhi janma pratyakṣam iti vacanāt yat ca tat samprayogāt vijñānam jāyate tad viṣayam tat iṣyate eva pratyakṣam na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi atra rajaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ samprayogāt tat viṣaya indriya jñānasya utpannasya pratyakṣatā prasajyate kim tarhi pratyakṣa jñānasya utpattiḥ etat uktam bhavati yadi yaḥ indriye sīdati tasya vā praśastaḥ saḥ indriya arthaḥ rajaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ api evaṃvidhāḥ tat tat samprayoge api pratyakṣam jñānam utpadyeta iti 
[I,172,iii]	na evam bhaviṣyati ityādinā sat śabdaḥ indriya arthaḥ eva rūḍhaḥ tat vyutpattau viśiṣṭasya eva artha sambandhinaḥ sadana ādeḥ āśrayaṇāt yathā go śabdaḥ go jātau eva ananya sādhāraṇam gamanam āśritya vyutpāditaḥ iti darśayati viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ iti dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ vaiṣamyāt rūḍhi balena hi viśeṣam āśritya vyutpattiḥ kriyate na ca sat śrutiḥ indriya arthe rūḍha iti asat etat 
[I,173,i]	tat nairantaryasya bādhakam iti samprayogaḥ nairantaryam yadi hi ityādinā sarva artha samprayoga śruteḥ artham āha nanu ca samprayoga śrutyā vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ pratyāyyate tat kutas ayam doṣaḥ kaḥ punar indriyasya vyāpāraḥ yadi grahaṇam cakṣuḥ vijñānam antareṇa api cakṣuḥ vijñānasya sadbhāvāt atha prakāśanam cakṣuṣaḥ eva taijasa tvena abhimata tvāt tasya eva prakāśanam syāt na śeṣāṇām śrotrasya vā ākāśa svabhāvasya niṣkriya tvāt kutas vyāpāraḥ samprayoga grahaṇam ca vyartham avaśyam hi buddhi janmani karaṇānām vyāpāreṇa bhāvyam na ca loke samprayoga śrutiḥ vyāpāra arthā pratītā prasiddha artha grahaṇam ca sūtre abhyupetam tena ayam pakṣaḥ atyantam ayuktaḥ iti sannikarṣa pakṣaḥ eva āśrayaṇīyaḥ tatas ca yathoktam aniṣṭam prasajyate iti 
[I,174,i]	vṛtti kāraḥ buddhi janma iti sa upaskāram vākyam vyācaṣṭaḥ iti atas idam āha buddhi kāraṇa sāmagrīm ityādi sā iti guṇa bhūtā api buddhiḥ parāmṛṣyate na tu sāmagrī tad vyatiriktasya strī liṅgasya upanyāsāt vṛttau ca tathā avivaraṇāt saṃskāraḥ dharma adharmau ātma guṇaḥ vā jñāna jaḥ jñāna hetuḥ saṃskāra viśeṣeṇa jñāna viśeṣa utpādāt anyat ityādinā yat asat na tat pratyakṣam kha puṣpa vat tathā ca sāmagrī vyatiriktaḥ hetuḥ iti vyāpaka abhāvam āha 
[I,174,ii_I,175,i]	buddhi janma iti kim punar iti anena api yat anarthakam na tat kartavyam tad anya anarthaka vat tathā ca buddhi janma grahaṇam iti vyāpaka viruddham syāt etat asati tasmin abuddhi janma hetoḥ api samprayogasya pratyakṣatā syāt atas samprayoga viśeṣaṇa artham tat kartavyam iti asat etat na hi sannikarṣasya buddhi janma ahetu tvam sambhavati kāryeṇa hi tasya astitvam anumīyate tat abhāve kutas tasya avagatiḥ jaiminīyaiḥ kriyā anumeyā iṣyate kim punar atīndriyāṇām indriyāṇām katham ca bhinna vibhakti viśeṣaṇam samāna adhikaraṇam syāt samprayoge buddhi janma iti atha vyadhikaraṇam viśeṣaṇam rājā iva puruṣasya tadā samprayogaḥ eva buddhi janmanaḥ viśeṣaṇam syāt iti asāram etat kim ca ityādinā yat akṣam prati na vartate na tat pratyakṣam abhimata apratyakṣa vat tathā ca yathā uktā sāmagrī iti vyāpaka abhāvam āha saṃskāravān iti saṃskāra sahitaḥ 
[I,175,ii]	manaindriya sannikarṣaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ ca akṣam prati vartate iti atas sā eva iti āha yaḥ api hi kalpayet iti tasya abhiprāyaḥ indriya sannikarṣaḥ eva jñānasya asādhāraṇam kāraṇam atas saḥ eva yatas buddhi janma iti atra sarva nāmnā hetu tvena parāmṛṣṭaḥ tasya ca akṣam prati vṛtteḥ pratyakṣa vyapadeśaḥ yujyate iti tasya api dviṣṭha tvāt iti indriya viṣaya varti tvāt dviṣṭha tvam anena ca tasya na indriyam eva asādhāraṇam kāraṇam iti darśitam tathā hi dviṣṭha tvāt tasya yathā indriya antaram na kāraṇam evam viṣaya antaram api yathā ca viṣayasya anyenān indriyeṇa api yogaḥ evam indriyasya api anyena aviṣayeṇa api iti aviśeṣaḥ asādhāraṇena ca loke vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti uktam prāk tatas na indriyeṇa eva vyapadeṣṭavyam iti āha akalpanā iyam iti 
[I,175,iii]	yatas yat niścayaḥ ityādi yatas buddhi janma tat pratyakṣam iti asya idam bhāṣyam etat uktam bhavati yatas indriya ādi samprayogāt niścaya jñānam jāyate gauḥ eva ayam ityādi tat pratyakṣam iti tat api ayuktam iti indriya ādi samprayogāt asambhavāt evaṃvidha jñānasya katham iti āha go tva ādi yogāt ityādi caśabdaḥ hetau yasmāt go tva ādi viśeṣaṇa sambandhāt arthaḥ go tva ādi tvena niścīyate na ca indriya dhiyaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya yojane sāmarthyam atas asambhavaḥ lakṣaṇasya iti ayuktam 
[I,176,i]	tvat matyā iti yatas pareṇa go tva ādayaḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca dravyam vastu tvena abhyupetam atas tad viśeṣayata indriya buddheḥ āśakyeta anusandhāne tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vastu satoḥ api na indriya dhiyaḥ śaktiḥ tathā hi gandhaḥ rūpi indriya viṣayaḥ dravyam ca para matena tathā api na tayoḥ paraspara anusandhāne tasyāḥ sāmarthyam abhyupeyate surabhi dravyam iti hi yadi cakṣuḥ vijñānam etat na gandha viṣayam atha ghnāṇa vijñānam dravya viṣaya tva anupapattiḥ sva matena tu jāti dravyayoḥ api asattvāt asat ālocanam iti darśanāya tvat matyā iti uktam 
[I,176,ii_I,177,i]	nanu ca kaṇa bhuj parīkṣāyām uktaḥ eva ayam arthaḥ viṣaya ālocana artha tvāt na sandhānam viśeṣaṇaiḥ iti tat kim punar kutas tasya eva spaṣṭatarīkaraṇāya sva saṃvedyam ityādinān antaram vakṣyamāṇena nyāyena syāt etat vinā api sambandhena niścayaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha na ca ityādi tasmāt mānasaḥ iti yasmāt evam indriya jaḥ na yujyate iti abhiprāyaḥ abheda upacāraḥ viśeṣaṇa abhidhāna rūpeṇa viśeṣya abhidheya pratipattiḥ abhidhāna abhidheyayoḥ ca iti grahaṇam dṛṣṭānta artham yat abheda upacāra jñānam tat mānasam abhidhāna abhidheya abheda upacāra vikalpavat tathā ca gauḥ eva ayam ityādi jñānam svabhāvaḥ 
[I,177,ii_I,177,iii]	kim kāraṇam iti vyāptim asambhāvayan pṛcchati sva saṃvedyam hi ityādinā hetum āha etat ca dharmiṇaḥ aneka rūpasya iti atra antare vyākhyātam asādhāraṇena iti sādhāraṇasya kvacid anupayogāt iti uktam tat etena anirdeśyam eva sva lakṣaṇam indriya dhiyaḥ viṣayaḥ na nirdeśyam sāmānyam atas na tena abheda upacāram kartum sā samartha iti sūcitam yaḥ yasya aviṣayaḥ na sa tena abheda upacāram kartum samarthaḥ tat yathā cakṣuḥ vijñānam śabdena aviṣayaḥ ca go tva ādi sām anyam indriya budheḥ vyāpaka viruddhaḥ tatas ca mānasam eva idam iti sthitam 
[I,177,iv]	atha punar iti asiddha tām āśaṅkate sarvathā iti jñeya tva ādi ākāreṇa api iti arthaḥ tatra kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha sarvathā ityādi sarvathā artha vijñāne sthitā sarva prakāreṇa artha adhigame vartamānā satī na pratyakṣa dhīḥ bhavet iti sambandhaḥ na pratyakṣa śabda vācyā syāt iti arthaḥ kutas etat iti āha pratyakṣa śabdaḥ hi ityādi yatas bhāṣya kāram atena pratyakṣa śabdaḥ triṣu eva vartate pramāṇe mukhyaḥ iti sannikarṣe pratyakṣa pramita tvāt iti prastha pramite prastha upacāra vat jñānaḥ iti phale akṣam prati vṛtteḥ iti anena sādharmyeṇa pramāṇa tulya tvāt pratyakṣa upacāraḥ yuktaḥ yathā siṃhaḥ māṇavakaḥ iti 
[I,178,i_I,179,i]	yadi ca ityādinā sarvathā artha vijñāne sthitā iti etat vyācaṣṭe sa ityādinā tu na pratyakṣa dhīḥ bhavet iti etat indriya nirapekṣā iti sāmānya buddhīnām atīta ādau api bhāvāt andha ādīnām ca abheda upacāra pravṛttā iti abheda upacāra buddhayaḥ api evam prakārāḥ eva asatā api vā abheda upacāram kurvanti yathā pradhānayaḥ sāṅkhya puruṣaḥ ayam iti na ca evaṃvidham indriya ādi sannikarṣa jam jñānam iṣyate pratipāditam ca na sāmānyam indriya dhiyaḥ viṣayaḥ iti na akṣa paratantrā syāt iti sāmarthyāt pratyakṣa śabda abhidhānam prati iti gamyate tathā hi pratyakṣa śabda abhidheya tā pratipādya tvena prastutā avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam anyathā indriya nirapekṣa akṣa paratantrā ca iti virodhaḥ syāt tat etat uktam bhavati jñānasya utpattau akṣapāratantryam pratyakṣa sādharmyāt pratyakṣa upacāraḥ vā pratyakṣa śruteḥ pravṛtti nimittam asati tasmin sā na pravartate iti yasyāḥ naimittikyāḥ śruteḥ yatra nimittam na asti na sā tatra pravartate tat yathā daṇḍi śrutiḥ na asti ca nimittam pratyakṣa śruteḥ yathā ukte jñāne kāraṇa abhāvaḥ sarvathā ca ityādinā doṣa antaram āha guṇa tva ādīnām sāmānya dharmāṇām rūpa śabda ādau sarvatra bhāvāt yathā cakṣuṣā grāhya tvam tathā śrotra ādibhiḥ api iti indriya antara viṣaye api indriya antaram pravartate tatas aneka indriya kalpanāyāḥ vaiyarthyam syāt 
[I,179,ii]	phalam anyat na labhyate iti adhigamaḥ hi jñānasya phalam sa ced pramāṇam phala antara abhāvaḥ na ca hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhayaḥ phalam iti kalpayitum yuktam udaka ādi smṛti antarita tvāt vyavahita avyavahiyoḥ ca avyavahitam eva phalam nyāyyam bhinna viṣaya tvāt ca ayuktam tāsām phala tvam pratyakṣam hi rūpa ādi sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam tāḥ tu hāna ādi kriyā viṣayāḥ 
[I,180,i]	buddheḥ ca ityādi buddhi janma sūtre pratyakṣam uktam tat ca buddheḥ anyat anyat vā syāt tatra yadi anyat iṣyate tat eva pramāṇam syāt janma ca kaṇabhujām ātmani sva kāraṇe buddheḥ samavāyaḥ sattā guṇa tva buddhi tva samavāyaḥ vā jñāne kārye mīmāṃsakaiḥ api tat matam eva āśritam sa vā yasmāt bhāṣya kṛtaḥ matena samavāyaḥ pratyakṣam prāpnoti na ca yuktam tasya pratyakṣa tvam artha vyabhicārāt tathā hi nitya tvāt artha abhāve api saḥ asti yat artha vyabhicāri na tat pratyakṣam mithyājñāna vat tathā ca samavāyaḥ viruddha vyāptaḥ atha vṛtti kāram atena yatas buddhi janma tat pratyakṣam evam api nitya tvāt samavāyaḥ na kutaścid utpadyate iti nirviṣayam lakṣaṇam tasmāt ubhayathā api yadi sūtrakāra matena yadi vṛtti kāra matena atha vā yadi sva kāraṇe kāryasya samavāyaḥ buddheḥ janma iṣṭam yadi sattā ādīnām jñāne kārye samavāyaḥ ubhayathā api pratyakṣa tvam na yujyate 
[I,181,i_I,181,ii]	atha ityādi ananya tve buddhiḥ eva janma iti janma grahaṇam mata dvaye api apārthakam nanu ca janma grahaṇasya prayojanam uktam jāyamāna avasthāyāḥ eva buddheḥ prāmāṇya jñāpana artham iti tat ayuktam uktam tathā hi kṣaṇika tvena uttara kāle anavasthānāt abuddheḥ jāyamānāyāḥ eva prāmāṇyam na ūrdhvam iti uktam tadā ca buddha bhāvāt eva prāmāṇya abhāvaḥ iti kim janma grahaṇena atha janma uttara kālam asti buddhiḥ evam api aviśiṣṭa tvāt tasyāḥ prāgvat tadā api prāmāṇyam anivāryam iti kim janma grahaṇena buddhi viśiṣṭasya tu janmanaḥ akṣam pratyavṛtteḥ pūrva uktāt ca kāraṇāt pratyakṣa tva abhāvaḥ 
[I,181,iii]	sarve tīrthyāḥ ātmānām pramātāram icchanti atas tam vicārayitum āha buddhi janmani ityādi iha eva kim vicārayati iti ced kva punar vicāra ārambhe na idam ca udyam avatarati api ca iha lakṣaṇa vākye puruṣasya iti vacanāt ātma adhikṛtaḥ iti yuktam atra eva vicārayitum pūrva avasthām vikṛtya iti apramātṛ avastha upamardena iti arthaḥ evam sati anityaḥ iti yat vikāri tat anityam ghaṭa vat tathā ca ātmā svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,182,i_I,182,ii]	atha avikṛtiḥ ityādinā yaḥ yadā pramātṛ avasthāyāḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ na tadā pramātā yathā saḥ eva pumān prāk yathā uktaḥ ca buddhi utpāde api saḥ iti viruddha vyāptam prasaṅgam āha anena eva ca nitya pramāṇa nivṛttaye pramāṇa bhūtāya iti atra yat bhūta grahaṇam tatra yuktiḥ sūcitā vakṣyamāṇasya ca svabhāva hetoḥ vyāpti siddhau evam tu ślokaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ vastunaḥ artha kriyā kāle vikṛtiḥ yadi anitya tā na ced sā asti na tat vastu sarva sāmarthya varjitam iti prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ 
[II,1,i_II,1,ii]	dve eva pramāṇe pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti uktam tatra pratyakṣam vyutpāditam samprati prāpta a asaram anumānam vyutpādayitum āha anumānam dvidhā ityādi sva artham yena svayam pratyeti para artham yena parān pratyāyayati nanu para arthasya lakṣaṇam pṛthak avācyam eva gamaka lakṣaṇa vidhānena eva hi pratipipādayiṣoḥ vacana anukramaḥ darśitaḥ eva anyathā abhidhāne gamaka dharmāt yotanāt na hi ye yathā yam artham vidanti vacana jñāḥ te tad pratipādane punar upadeśa antaram apekṣante 
[II,1,iii_II,2,ii]	satyam etat tathā api bāla vyutpādana arthaḥ ayam ārambhaḥ yathāvastu pratipādyamānāḥ api hi anyathā nigadantaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ upayoginaḥ api avinābhāvasya avacanāt anupayoginām api ca sādhya upanaya nigamanānām prayogāt trirūpāt iti hetau pañcamī abhighātāt śabdaḥ iti yathā atha vā lya blope yathā prāsādam āruhya prekṣate prāsādāt prekṣate tathā trirūpam liṅgam dṛṣṭvā artha darśanam tri rūpāt liṅgataḥ artha dṛś iti nanu tri rūpa grahaṇam anarthakam atri rūpasya āliṅga tvāt kim ca līnaḥ arthaḥ liṅgyate anena iti liṅgam tat ca trairūpyam vinā na sambhavati atas api gata artha tvāt tri rūpāt iti na vācyam na eṣa doṣaḥ atri rūpam api kecid liṅgam icchanti atas tad vipratipatti nivṛttaye tri rūpa grahaṇam 
[II,2,iii]	tatra āhrīkaḥ āha anyathā anupapanna tvam yasya asau hetuḥ iṣyate eka lakṣaṇakaḥ saḥ arthaḥ catur lakṣaṇakaḥ na vā iti anyathā iti sādhyena vinā iti arthaḥ anupapanna tvamaklṛptiḥ asambhavaḥ nanu ca avinābhāvi tvam eva idam syāt na iti ahrīkaḥ avinā abhāvi tvam hi sādhyāt bahis iṣyate anyathā anupapanna tvam tu dharmiṇī eva sādhyaḥ eva iti ślokam api āha vinā sādhyāt adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭānte hetutā iṣyate paraiḥ mayā punar dharmiṇya sambhūṣṇoḥ vinā amunā iti etat ca ekam eva rūpam sati va trairūpye anyathā anupapanna tvam caturtham rūpam eṣṭavyam trairūpya mātre hi sa deśa antara gataḥ śyāmaḥ caitra putra tvāt iti asya api hetu tvam syāt iti 
[II,3,i]	tatra yat uktam avinā abhāvi tvam hi paraiḥ sādhyāt bahis iṣyate iti eṣaḥ adhyāropaḥ sarva upasaṃhāreṇa hi yatra yatra sādhana dharmaḥ tatra tatra sādhya dharmaḥ iti aṣāḥ vyāptiḥ avinā abhāvi tvam atas sādhye api tat iṣyate eva yadi ca sādhya dharmiṇī eva yaḥ sādhya dharmeṇa avinābhāvī sa hetuḥ iṣyate evam sati yasya bahis api sādhyena āvinābhāvaḥ tasya hetu tvam na syāt vyabhicārī api ca hetuḥ syāt tasya api dharmiṇi anyathā anupapanna tvasya sambhavāt tasmāt ayuktam etat atas eva asya ayukta tvāt na catur lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ upapadyate 
[II,3,ii_II,4,i]	yat punaruktam trairūpya mātre hi sa syāmaḥ caitra putra tvāt iti asya api hetu tvam syāt iti tat ayuktam svabhāva kārya anupalambha viśeṣāṇām eva hi trairūpyam upapadyate na anyeṣām na ca ayam teṣu antarbhavati tatas kutas sa prasaṅgaḥ anyaḥ tu dvi rūpaḥ hetuḥ iti darśayan āha ajñātaḥ dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ dharme san ā iva yatra hi jñāyate jñāpyate ca eṣa hetuḥ vidhi niṣedhavān iti ajñātaḥ dharmaḥ jijñāsitaḥ anitya tva ādiḥ dharmiṇaḥ śabda ādeḥ yatra jñāyate kṛtaka tva ādau dharme jñāta tvam sāmarthya labhyam san ā iva iti pramātrā ghaṭa ādiṣu svayam smaryate paraḥ va smāryate para artha anumāne san ā iva na āsan ityetau vidhi niṣedhau yasya staḥ sa vidhi niṣedhavān hetuḥ etena dharmi dharma tvam sat sādhya dharma tvam ca iti etat dvairūpyam uktam 
[II,4,ii_II,5,i]	atra sādhya dharmaḥ yatra san ā iva na āsan iti bruvatā tat eva anvaya vyatirekavat tvam uktam bhavati yasmāt evam sa tatra san ā iva bhavati yadi tad abhāve hetuḥ na bhavati eva tatas ca traiḥ upyam eva ākāra antareṇa uktam iti na dvi rūpaḥ hetuḥ ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti aparaḥ trīṇi ca etāni abādhita viṣaya tvam vivakṣita eka saṅkhya tvam jñāta tvam ca iti tatra ābādhita viṣaya tvam tāvat na rūpa antaram bādhāvinā bhāvayoḥ virodhāt avinā abhāvaḥ hi hetoḥ sādhya dharme sati eva bhāvaḥ katham ca sa tad lakṣaṇaḥ dharmiṇi hetuḥ syāt na ca atra sādhya dharmaḥ bhavet tet na bādhāvinā abhāvayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ tena na ābādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram 
[II,5,ii]	vyavacchedya abhāvāt vivakṣita eka saṅkhya tvam api na lakṣaṇa antara tvena vācyam tat viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ hetu tva prasaṅga nivṛtti artham ucyate sva lakṣaṇa yuktayoḥ ca hetvoḥ ekatra virodhinoḥ upanipāte viruddha avyabhicāri tvam bhavati na ca yathā ukta lakṣaṇānām kārya svabhāva anupalambhānām pratyanīkaḥ hetuḥ sambhavati katham hi nāma ekaḥ sva sādhya bhāvaḥ eva bhāvāt tena avyabhicārī tatra eva ca anyaḥ api tad bādhakasya bhāvaḥ eva bhāvāt viruddhaḥ tena sambhavet api ca sa hetuḥ yadi svabhāvataḥ eva tad dharma bhāvī tadā artha antara upanipāte api katham anyathā syāt na hi vastūnām svabhāvānyathā bhāvasya viruddha svabhāva dvayasya ca sambhavaḥ atha svabhāvataḥ atad dharma bhāvī evam satyanyadā api na sādhanam kasyacid tasmāt svabhāvataḥ eva sva sādhya avinābhāvinaḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ pratihetuḥ na sambhavati iti alakṣaṇam eka saṅkhyā vivakṣā viruddha avyabhicārya vacana prasaṅgaḥ iti ced vastu bala pravṛttam liṅgam pratīṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ viṣayaḥ ca asya parastāt nivedayiṣyate 
[II,6,i]	jñānam punar aliṅga dharmaḥ katham liṅgasya lakṣaṇam syāt kiṃrūpāt liṅgāt arthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ iti cintāyām pratipattuḥ avisaṃvādakasya rūpam ucyate yad darśana āt ayam sādhana asādhane pravivecya tasya iṣṭa artha sādhana pratyayāt pravartate tatra yat asya liṅgasya ātma rūpam tat lakṣaṇam na para rūpam pratipatti janmani upayoga mātrāt tad lakṣaṇa tve ati prasaṅgāt evam hi prameya puruṣa ādīnām api tad lakṣaṇa tvam syāt na hi teṣu api asatsu liṅgini jñānam bhavati tasmāt jñānam api na liṅga lakṣaṇam eṣṭavyam iti sthitam etat trirūpaḥ eva hetuḥ iti 
[II,7,i_II,7,ii]	pūrvavat phalam iti yathā pratyakṣe dvidhā phalam uktam viṣaya saṃvittiḥ sva saṃvittiḥ ca tathā iha api pratyakṣa vat a vyatiriktam anumānasya adhigama ātmakam phalam iti bruvata anumānam api adhigama svabhāvam iti uktam bhavati atas pṛcchati yadi dvayam api ityādi arthaḥ tu rūpam ca atulyam etayoḥ iti tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ etat eva dvayam atulyam adhigama rūpa tā tu tulya iti nanu ca adhigamaḥ tayoḥ rūpam tat ced abhinnam tat kim anyat rūpam yat ucyate rūpam ca atulyam etayoḥ iti yat tad viṣaya sārūpyam pramāṇam vyavasthāpitam tat atulyam iti uktam tathā hi tat pratyakṣasya spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam tu anumānasya 
[II,7,iii]	viṣayaḥ hi ityādi viṣaya śabdena atra ālambanam vivakṣitam na tu prāmāṇyasya viṣayaḥ anumānasya api hi avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam vastu viṣayam eva tasmāt ālambana bhedāt pramāṇayoḥ viṣaya bhedam āha katham punar ālambana bhedaḥ pratibhāsasya bhinna tvāt na hi tau ekasya vilakṣaṇau ākārau yujyete bhinnaḥ iti ca abhinna pratiṣedhaḥ eva draṣṭavyaḥ na tu nānā viṣaya tā anumāna vikalpasya nirviṣaya tvāt tat ca anumānasya sammataḥ yaḥ viṣayaḥ tasya tattvataḥ apariniṣpanna tvāt 
[II,8,i]	tad ākāra viśeṣāt ca iti tat iti pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ viṣayaḥ parāmṛśyate tasya ākāraḥ svabhāvaḥ ākriyate paricchidyate iti kṛtvā tad ākārasya viśeṣaḥ bhedaḥ iti arthaḥ viśeṣa grahaṇam ca aviśeṣa pratiṣedha pratipādana param veditavyam na tu nānā svabhāva tā anena pratipadyate sāmānyasya vikalpita tvena asattvāt tat etat sūcitam bhavati yasmāt pratyakṣasya bahis viṣayaḥ asti yatas tasya spaṣṭaḥ viṣaya pratibhāsaḥ bhavati na tu anumānasya yaḥ tu tasya asphuṭaḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ sa sva bīja balāt eva jāyate tasmāt pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ yathā uktam svarūpam bhinnam iti atha vā pratyakṣasya sva lakṣaṇam sākṣāt spaṣṭasu a ākāra janakam prameyam sva rūpeṇa anumānasya tu tat eva pāramparyeṇa asphuṭa viṣaya ākāra janakam para rūpeṇa prameyam pratyakṣasya api para rūpeṇa iti apare tat evam yatas pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ bhinnaḥ viṣayaḥ atas tad svabhāva viśeṣāt spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa viṣaya ākāra tayā svarūpam api bhinnam iti 
[II,9,i_II,9,ii]	atha kasmāt iti kim kāraṇam sva artha para artha bhedena anumānam eva dvidhā bhidyate na tu pratyakṣam iti avadhāraṇena darśayati etat uktam bhavati svayam pratyakṣīkṛtasya arthasya para avabodhanāya yat vacanam tat para artham pratyakṣam dvitīyam kasmāt na iṣyate iti yasmāt ityādi anumānasya hi sāmānyam viṣayaḥ tatra ca yādṛśam anumānam ātmanaḥ tādṛśam eva para santāne vācā kriyate iti yuktam tasya dvaividhyam pratyakṣasya tu sva lakṣaṇam viṣayaḥ na ca tatra yādṛśam ātmanaḥ pratyakṣa jñānam tādṛś śabdena santāna antare janayitum śakyate tasya anirdeśya tvāt anyathā andha ādīnām api śabdāt tathā avigham eva sphuṭa pratibhāsi jñānam syāt kasmāt tad anirdeśyam iti āha grāhya bhedāt iti pratyakṣasya hi asādhāraṇam grāhyam na ca tat śakyate nirdeṣṭum tasya pūrvam adṛṣṭa tvāt anumānasya tu tad viparītam tasmāt tasya eva grāhyam nirdeśyam na pratyakṣasya 
[II,9,iii_II,10,i]	sva ātma vat iti anena etat sūcayati pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ svarūpam bhinnam pratyātma vedyam etat sarvasya na ca abhinna viṣaya tve sva viṣaya ākāram anukurvatoḥ tat upapadyate tasmāt yathā tayoḥ svarūpam bhinnam tathā viṣaya bhedaḥ api draṣṭavyaḥ tatas na anumāna vat pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ nirdeśyaḥ iti anye tu āhuḥ vṛtta bhaṅga bhayāt atra yat paścāt vaktavyam tat pūrvam uktam tasmāt evam atha granthaḥ vijñeyaḥ kasmāt anumānam eva dvidhā bhidyate na pratyakṣam iti pṛṣṭe kāraṇam āha grāhya bhedāt ityādi yadi grāhya bhedāt anumānam dvi ghā bhidyate evam sati pratyakṣam api dvidhā bhidyeta iti āha sva lakṣaṇam anirdeśyam iti etat uktam bhavati īdṛśam idam pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ grāhyam iṣyate yatra ekam nirdeśyam anyat anirdeśyam iti tasmāt anumānam eva dvidhā bhidyate yasya viṣayaḥ vācā parasmai pratipādayitum śakyate na tu pratyakṣam iti 
[II,10,ii_II,10,iii^1]	nanu ca arthaḥ tu rūpam ca atulyam etayoḥ iti anena prāk eva pramāṇayoḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ pratipāditaḥ tad bhedāt ca svarūpa bhedaḥ tat kim idam upanyastam bhinnam hi pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ sva ātma vat grāhyam ityādi pūrvam anya arthaḥ ayam arthaḥ uktaḥ idānīm anya arthaḥ iti adoṣaḥ yadi ca ityādinā sva lakṣaṇasya anirdeśya tvam pratipādayati sa tena eva śabdena anumeyaḥ syāt iti saḥ eva pratyakṣa grāhyaḥ arthaḥ tatas śabdāt pratīyeta iti arthaḥ na ca evam mā bhūt andha ādeḥ api pratyakṣeṇa eva tasya arthasya darśanam iti paraḥ tu jāḍyāt imam doṣam anavagacchan svayam abhyupagata pramāṇa eka viṣaya tvasya dṛṣṭa anuvidhāyitām darśayat iṣṭam evam me tat iti nanu ca ityādinā sūcayati sparśaḥ hi pratyakṣasya arthaḥ saḥ eva ca rūpeṇa anumīyate iti manyate kadācid iti yadā sparśaḥ indriyeṇa na spṛśyate 
[II,10,iii^2]	tadā iti arthaḥ na tu yathā pratyakṣam iti pratyakṣam hi bheda antara vimarśa vivekena pratiṣṭhitena eva rūpeṇa sparśam paricchinatti anumānam tu smārta ākṛṣṭa pūrva anusandhānataḥ saḥ ayam mayā pūrvam anena rūpeṇa saha prāk upalabdhaḥ iti sparśa sāmānyam asparśa vyāvṛttam tat yathā iti pūrva dṛṣṭa anusandhāne dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā rūpam na pratyakṣataḥ gṛhyate iti eva sva lakṣaṇa ākāreṇa liṅgam bhavati viśeṣasya ananvayāt api tu sāmānya ākāreṇa eva pūrva dṛṣṭa anusaṃhitena tathā na sparśaḥ pūrva pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītaḥ iti eva sva lakṣaṇataḥ anumeyaḥ kim tu sāmānya ākāreṇa eva anumāna yogyena iti darśayati 
[II,12,i_II,12,ii]	katham dṛṣṭa ādi vyavahāraḥ iti yadi yathā anubhūtam ācakṣate evaṃvyavahārāḥ āryāḥ yujyante tvad matena tu sva lakṣaṇam upalabhya anyat eva kathayatām vyavahārāḥ anāryāḥ syuḥ tatas ca abhyupeta bādhā dṛṣṭam ityādinā etat kathayati darśana ādi kriyā nimittāḥ dṛṣṭa ādi śabdāḥ te ca sati svasmin nimitte āryaiḥ prayujyante nāsati iti āryāḥ vyavahārāḥ abhyupeyante na tu sva lakṣaṇa abhidhānāt iti na abhyupeta bādha iti 
[II,12,iii]	yat tarhi ityādi śāstra virodham āha nanu ca na eva cakṣuḥ vijñāna anubhūtaḥ eva kṣaṇaḥ manaḥ vijñānena anubhūyate kim tarhi kṣaṇa antaram iti uktam prāk tat katham evam uktam na eṣa doṣaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñāna anubhūtam eva artham iti sva lakṣaṇa upalakṣaṇa param etat sva lakṣaṇam eva iti yāvat tulya jātīya tvāt ca pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ abheda vivakṣayā evam abhihitam syāt atha vā anuśabdaḥ ayam saha arthe vartate bhūta śabdaḥ api utpanne tatas ca cakṣuḥ vijñānena saha utpannam eva artham vijānāti iti ayam atra arthaḥ iti adoṣaḥ yadi yat tad manaḥ vijñāna anubhūtam sva lakṣaṇam tat anirdeśyam katham manaḥ nīlam ca vijānāti nīlam iti ca āviṣṭa abhilāpam tat eva tatra api iti śāstre 
[II,13,i_II,13,iii]	ākāra antaravirdeśya nāma jña tvāt ityādi sva lakṣaṇa ākārāt ākāra antaram sāmānya ākāraḥ tena nirdeśyam na sva lakṣaṇena tasya nāma nīlam iti iyam sañjñā tat ca vijānāti na kevalam sva lakṣaṇam tasmāt dvidhā śāstre manaḥ iṣyate anīla vyudāsena iti tam ākāra antaram darśayati vyavahartṝṇām abhiprāya anurodhāt anīla vyudāsena iti uktam te hi tattva adhyavasāyena vyavaharanti iti uktam etat anyathā paraspara vyāhatam etat syāt tathā hiyadya ākāra antareṇa manaḥ nirdiśati na tarhi tena cakṣuḥ vijñāna anubhūtam eva nirdiṣṭam bhavati atha tat eva sva lakṣaṇam nirdiśati na nāma ākāra antareṇa iti asāmānye api iti api śabdāt sāmānye api anitya tva ādau 
[II,13,iv]	vāyu ādi svabhāvaḥ iti ādi śabdena ākāśa ādayaḥ apratyakṣāḥ gṛhyante yathā aha iti kaṇādaḥ asya sūtrasya sambandhaḥ kṣiti jala ānana vat agrahaṇāt sparśa mātram vāyuḥ iti pareṇa akte tad parihārāya āha adṛṣṭasya api liṅgataḥ samadhigamam kariṣyāmaḥ kim punar tasya liṅgam iti tat ucyate sparśaḥ ca na ca dṛṣṭānām sparśaḥ iti adṛṣṭa liṅgaḥ vāyuḥ iti sparśaḥ ca samupalabhyate śīta uṣṇa tva viśeṣa rahitaḥ caśabdāt śabda dhṛti kampāḥ ca nirvṛkṣa kṣupe deśe śuka śukā śabdaḥ samupalabhyate tṛṇa ādinām ca dhṛtiḥ teṣām dravya antareṇa asati pratibandhe guru tvāt pātaḥ syāt sthitiḥ ca viyati lakṣyate latā ādīnām ca kampaḥ na ca ayam dṛṣṭānām kṣiti ādīnām caśabdāt na ca adṛṣṭānām ākāśa ādi nāma atas dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭeṣu adṛṣṭa tvāt sparśa viśeṣaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ saḥ asya liṅgam iti adṛṣṭa liṅgaḥ vāyuḥ na ca asau pūrvam dṛṣṭaḥ tat prathamatas sparśa viśeṣeṇa grahaṇa āditya sāmānya viṣayam anumānam 
[II,14,i_II,15,ii]	na tad sāmānya sūcanāt iti tad śabdena sparśaḥ eva sambadhyate na tu vāyuḥ atas eva āha na hi tat vāyu ādiṣu ityādi sparśasya sāmānyam āśrita tvam guṇa utvena sūcyate yaḥ guṇaḥ saḥ āśritaḥ gandhavat guṇaśa ca sparśaḥ svabhāvaḥ atha vā tad śabdena vāyuḥ eva sambadhyate iti darśayan āha na vā vāyu ādi svabhāveṣu ityādi asya arthaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa dravya āśritaḥ gandhavat guṇaḥ ca sparśaḥ iti svabhāvaḥ sparśasya guṇa tvāt dravya āśrita tve anumite dravya tva mātram arthataḥ sidhyati tat yathā cakṣuḥ ādīnām pārārthye siddhe paraḥ api arthataḥ sidhyati iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[II,15,iii]	pariśeṣāt iti pariśeṣa siddhiḥ anumānam eva liṅga ja tvāt iti manyate yathā āha ityādi na ayam sparśaḥ pṛthivyāḥ gandha ādi asahacāri tvāt na aptejasoḥ anuṣṇa aśīta tvāt na api ākāśa ādīnām adṛṣṭānām teṣām hi sparśavat tvāt ghaṭa ādīnām tatra pratighātaḥ syāt na manasaḥ anumeya guṇa tvāt aṇu tvam eka tvam ca asya anumeyau guṇau ayam tu pratyakṣaḥ na ca nirāśrayaḥ guṇaḥ samasti tasmāt pariśeṣāt vāyoḥ eva ayam sparśaḥ iti eṣā pariśeṣa siddhiḥ 
[II,16,i_II,16,ii^1]	na tad sattva āsiddheḥ iti tad śabdena vāyuḥ sambadhyate yasmāt nyeṣām yasya asambhavaḥ tatra siddha sattāke tasya astitvam sambhāvyate yasya tu sattvam eva asiddham katham tatra pariśeṣāt saḥ asti iti sambhāvyate na hi yadā anyena tatra sannihitena puruṣeṇa idam kāryam na kṛtam iti sambhāvyate tadā vandhyā sutena pariśeṣāt kṛtam etat iti yuktam sambhāvayitum teṣu eva tu kena idam kṛtam iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati pratiṣedha tulya tvāt ca iti siddhe api tasya sattve pratiṣedhasya tulya tvāt na yuktam anumānam yathā eva ayam sparśaḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu na dṛṣṭa caraḥ iti teṣām na bhavati tathā vāyau api prāk na dṛṣṭaḥ iti tasya api mā bhūt katham tarhi vāyoḥ pariśeṣa siddhiḥ iti āha 
[II,16,ii^2]	siddhe hi ityādi yathā utpattimatām ghaṭa ādīnām sattvam siddham tathā yadi vāyu ādīnām jijñāsitānām sattvam siddham bhavati evam sati hetoḥ siddhatvam labhyate na anyathā pratiṣedha asambhave citi siddhe api teṣām sattve yadi sa dharmaḥ pramāṇena bādhyate agnau iva śaityam evam api asiddhaḥ eva hetuḥ syāt viparyayāt tu siddhaḥ iti evam yathā hetoḥ siddhatvam janyate tathā darśitam guṇa viśeṣa sambandhāt iti guṇa viśeṣaḥ dharma viśeṣaḥ hetu tvena abhimataḥ tasya sambandhaḥ sādhyena avinābhāvaḥ guṇa sāmānyam ujjhitvā iti dharma sāmānyam vyabhicāri hitvā guṇa viśeṣeṇa iti yathā uktena sādhya dharmiṇi siddha sattākena anvaya vyatirekavatā dharmeṇa dravya viśeṣa anumānam kriyate iti pariśeṣāt vāyuḥ anumīyate iti arthaḥ tatra api sāmānya ākāreṇa iti veditavyam na tu svarūpeṇa yasmāt prāk eva anumānasya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvam niṣiddham viśeṣa grahaṇam tu pṛthivī ādi dravya nirāsa artham tatra ayam prayogaḥ 
[II,16,ii^3]	yaḥ yatas siddha sattākāt anyeṣām na sambhāvyate vastu dharmaḥ tatra ca pramāṇena ābādhitaḥ sa tasya bhavati tat yathā utpatti madbhyaḥ siddha sattākebhyaḥ anyeṣām asambhāvyamānam anitya tvam vastu dharmaḥ tatra pramāṇena ābādhitam bhavati vāyoḥ siddha sattākāt anyeṣām na sambhāvyate anuṣṇa aśīta sparśaḥ vastu dharmaḥ tatra ca pramāṇena ābādhitaḥ iti svabhāvaḥ evam sparśasya pariśeṣāt vāyu sambandhi tve siddhe vāyuḥ kvacid deśa viśeṣe kāla viśeṣe vā sidhyati tvad matena tu eṣām pariśeṣa siddhiḥ na bhavati iti darśayan āha sattvam tu asiddham ityādi yasmāt sattvam asiddham tulyaḥ ca pṛthivī ādibhiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt guṇa viśeṣa abhāvaḥ trairūpyavataḥ dharmasya abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ tatas guṇa viśeṣa abhāvāt tatra kutas anumānam na eva evam tāvat dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedham abhyupetya anumāna abhāvaḥ uktaḥ 
[II,18,i]	samprati pratiṣedhaḥ eva ayuktaḥ iti darśayan āha yadi adarśana mātreṇa ityādi mātra grahaṇena upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yat adarśanam tatas eva abhāvaḥ sidhyati iti sūcayati nanu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ sparśasya yuktaḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ dṛśya tad svabhāva mātrā pratiṣedhāt pṛthivī ādi sāmānyam gṛhītvā bhavān pratiṣedham āha tatra ca tūla upala pallava ādiṣu tad bhāve api sparśa bheda darśanāt kvacid viśeṣasya api sambhavāt śaṅkayā bhāvyam iti sarvatra adarśana mātreṇa ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ 
[II,18,ii]	adṛṣṭebhyaḥ api na yuktaḥ iti darśan āha na hi adṛṣṭebhyaḥ ityādi hi śabdaḥ samuccaya avadhāraṇe vā amurtimatām anabhighātāt iti abhighātasya vā ayam pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tad viparītasya vā vastunaḥ vidhiḥ yadi pratiṣedhaḥ abhighāta sparśa viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ vā vācyaḥ yatas hetu vyāpakau eva nivartamānau sva pratibaddhe kārya vyāpye nivartayataḥ anyathā ati prasaṅgāt kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvau ca na sidhyataḥ vinā api abhighātena sparśa viśeṣasya bhāvāt artha antara tvāt ca atha amūrtimatām anabhighātāt iti anena anabhighāta ākhyam vastu eva ucyate paryudāsa vṛttyā tasya tarhi vyoma ādhibhiḥ sambandhaḥ sādhyaḥ sparśa viśeṣeṇa ca virodhaḥ anyathā katham tad asambaddham aviruddham ca tena etat tatra bādhata atiprasaṅgaḥ vā 
[II,19,i]	tatra tāvat sambandhaḥ na sidhyati tathā hi teṣu tasya vṛttiḥ vā sambandhaḥ syāt tat janyatā vā na tāvat vṛttiḥ sidhyati teṣām atīndriya tvāt n hi atīndriyeṣu kasyacid vṛttiḥ upalabhyate na ca vinā upalambhena atra idam vartate iti śakyate niścetum na api tad janyatā sidhyati vyatireka asiddheḥ na hi anvaya mātrāt kāraṇasya sāmarthyam gamyate api tu vyatirekāt api sa ca iha na asti nitya tvāt sarva gata tvāt ca vyoma ādinām tad abhāve tad abhāva asambhavāt tat evam anabhighāta ākhyam ākāśa ādi sambandhi vastu eva na sidhyati 
[II,19,ii_II,20,i]	kutas punar tasya sparśa viśeṣeṇa virodhaḥ tathā hi ātapa ādiṣu ghaṭa ādinām anabhighātaḥ asti atha ca te sparśavantaḥ tasmāt na tatas pratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati guṇa anumeya tvāt ca iti tatpuruṣaḥ ayam manasi ca guṇa upajanita vyatireka nibandhanā ṣaṣṭhī na anumeya apekṣā manasaḥ guṇānām anumeya tvāt iti vākya arthaḥ guṇasya guṇa apekṣāyāḥ nitya tvāt sāmarthya abhāva doṣaḥ api na asti ayam api ahetuḥ avirodhāt tathā hi yathā ātmanaḥ vibhu tvam nāma guṇaḥ anumeyaḥ atha ca sukha ādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ tathā manasaḥ api aṇu tvam eka tvam ca anumeyam etat guṇa dvayam syāt ayam ca sparśaḥ pratyakṣaḥ guṇaḥ syāt iti na kaścid virodhaḥ idānīm yat atra yuktam tat pratipādayitum āha kim tarhi ityādi caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ katham punar dṛṣṭeṣu ca dṛṣṭa tvāt iti etat uktam yāvatā sa sparśa viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭeṣu api na eva dṛṣṭaḥ 
[II,20,ii]	na eṣa doṣaḥ dṛṣṭeṣu tāvat sparśa sāmānyam sambhavat viśeṣam dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭeṣu tu tasya api darśanam na asti yaḥ yatra dṛṣṭa sāmānyaḥ sa tatra sambhavati yathā āmalakeṣu madhuraḥ rasaḥ dṛṣṭa sāmānyaḥ ca dṛṣṭeṣu sparśa viśeṣaḥ atha vā yaḥ yatra dṛṣṭaḥ sa tatra sambhavat viśeṣaḥ yathā āmalakeṣu rasaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca sparśaḥ dṛṣṭeṣu iti svabhāvau ubhayatra ca ābādhake sati iti viśeṣaṇam draṣṭavyam vāyu ādau tu sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhāya anupalambhaḥ vācyaḥ yadi evam niścayena bhavitavyam atra eva ayam sambhavati iti saṃśayaḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt na ayam dṛṣṭeṣu sambhavati iti atas āha teṣām ca ityādi aneka tvāt saṃśayaḥ na tu tatra asambhavāt iti arthaḥ 
[II,20,iii]	taiḥ api vāyoḥ ānu mānika tvam nirastam iti darśayan āha āpta sañjñā vidhānena ityādi na vāyoḥ ānumānika tvam iti atra adhyāhāryam dravya sāmānya anumāne sati iti sparśena guṇena dravya āśritena asti kim api dravyam yat ayam āśritaḥ iti dravya mātra anumānam tat parityajya āpta sañjñā prāmāṇyāt iti yasmāt kṣīṇa doṣaiḥ nava eva dravya sañjñā vihitāḥ tatra pṛthivī ādiṣu aṣṭāsu dravyeṣu aṣṭau sañjñāḥ niveśitāḥ vāyu sañjñā eva avaśiṣyate na ca anyat dravyam asti daśamam tasmāt yasya ayam sparśaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti evam pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ anyasya daśama ādeḥ dravyasya pṛthivī ādeḥ ca anyasya pratiṣedhena vāyu sattvam avagacchati 
[II,21,i]	na bhedasya api sambhavāt iti śābdasya pramāṇa antara tva nirākaraṇāya pramāṇa antara vādī tāvat uttaram dāyikaḥ svayam tu uttaratra dāsyati prasiddhi vaśena iti sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sat asat tve śrotuḥ siddhe iti dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam dṛṣṭānta grahaṇam avayava upalakṣaṇa artham avayavānām anupadeśāt iti yāvat tat etat uktam bhavati yat anupadiṣṭa avayavam tad anumānāt bhinnam pratyakṣa vat tathā ca śābdam iti svabhāvaḥ 
[II,21,ii]	evam api iti vyabhicāram āha dṛṣṭāntasya ekasya iti śeṣa avayava apekṣayā dṛṣṭāntasya eka tvam na tu dṛṣṭānta apekṣayā tatas ca ayam arthaḥ yat dṛṣṭāntasya eva anabhidhānam iti dvayoḥ vā iti vā śabdaḥ ca arthe vartamānaḥ anukta samuccayam karoti trayāṇām caturṇām pañcānām ca iti arthaḥ tena yadā api sādhāraṇam hetum karoti tadā api sva artha anumānena anekāntaḥ bhavati śābda prasaṅgaḥ iti parasya śābdam anumānāt bhinnam pratītam tena śābda vat prasaṅgaḥ anumānāt bhinna tva prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ yathābhūtam śābdam tathābhūtam tat api prāpnoti iti yāvat vinā api hi vatinā tad arthaḥ gamyate iti ukta prāyam 
[II,22,i^1]	anye tu āhuḥ ityādi śabdaḥ hi sva rūpeṇa abhinna rūpam eva artham pratyāyayati na tu evam dhūma ādayaḥ na hi dhūmāt agnim pratiyan pratyāyayan vā dhūma rūpeṇa pratyeti pratyāyayati vā katham arthe anumānam iti arthasya aneka rūpa tvāt tatra kim svarūpeṇa saḥ arthaḥ gamyate uta sāmānya rūpeṇa sarvathā eva anupapattim manyate tathā hi yadi vṛkṣa ādayaḥ śabdāḥ sattva ādibhiḥ sāmānya ākāraiḥ vṛkṣa ādikam artham pratipādayeyuḥ 
[II,22,i^2]	sarva śabdānām ekārtha tā prasajyeta sāmānya ākārāṇām aneka artha sādhāraṇa tvāt atha viśeṣa rūpeṇa tat ayuktam asādhāraṇasya rūpasya pratipādayitum aśakya tvāt iti sarvathā śabda artha tva abhāvaḥ vṛkṣa śabda abhidheyaḥ anyaḥ arthe na bhavati iti yathā eva tava śabda arthaḥ anya apoḍhaḥ sāmānyam tathā mama api etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ mayā tat śabda ākāra uparaktam pratīyate iti abhyupagatam iti darśayati vṛkṣa śabda abhidheyaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ saḥ anyaḥ ghaṭādiḥ na bhavati anya śabda artha abhāvena atra vṛkṣa śabda abhidheyaḥ bhāgaḥ lakṣyate etat uktam bhavati artha antara vyāvṛtti upalakṣitaḥ yaḥ vastunaḥ bhāgaḥ saḥ eva vṛkṣa śabdasya arthaḥ iti tena eva tasya sārūpyāt na tu sattva ādibhiḥ sādhāraṇaiḥ ākāraiḥ asādhāraṇena vā rūpeṇa iti manyate 
[II,23,i]	anyeṣām pāṭhaḥ vṛkṣa śabda abhidheyaḥ anya arthaḥ na bhavati iti vṛkṣa śabda arthaḥ yaḥ sa śabda antarasya arthaḥ na bhavati paryāya śabdānām ekārtha tvena ananya tvam eva iti abhiprāyaḥ atra api vṛkṣa śabda arthasya śabda antarān abhidheya tām darśayatā śabda antara artha vyāvṛtti upalakṣitam vṛkṣa tva mātram vṛkṣa śabdasya arthaḥ iti uktam bhavati iti saḥ eva arthaḥ 
[II,23,ii]	nanu ca dravya śabdena api śākhā ādimān arthaḥ pratyāyyate na ca asau tad rūpaḥ tatas ca asārupye api abhidheya tva darśanāt na śabda sārūpyeṇa artha pratyāyanam iti atas āha yadi api ityādi api śabdena dravya śabdaḥ dravya bhedānām vyabhicārāt avācakaḥ eva abhyupetya tu uttaram ucyate iti artham āviṣkaroti rūpa antaram ākāra antaram tasya eva vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ tena ca saha dravya śabdasya sārupyam asti eva iti abhiprāyaḥ tat punā rūpa antaram adravya nivṛttya upalakṣyate iti darśayitum idam uktam adravya nivṛttya iti 
[II,24,i]	nanu ca ityādi na kevalam dravya śabdena adravya nivṛtti upalakṣitam vastunaḥ rūpa antaram dravya śabda sārupya prāpti yogyam gamyate api tu vṛkṣa śabdena ap tathā hi sāmānādhikaraṇyam dṛśyate dravyam vṛkṣaḥ iti na hi bhinna arthayoḥ tat upapadyate na ca tena saha tasya sārūpyam iṣyate tatas saḥ eva doṣaḥ asārūpye api śabda artha tva darśanāt na abhidhānasya sārūpyeṇa artha abhidhānam iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[II,24,ii]	arthāt na śabdāt iti vṛkṣa śabda arthā deva adravya nivṛtti avinābhāvinaḥ sā pratīyate mūḍhaḥ tu śabdāt eva gamyate iti manyate sāmānādhikaraṇyam tu viśeṣa sahitasya viśeṣe vartamāna tvāt na tu vṛkṣa śabdena adravya nivṛttiḥ abhidhīyate yadi vṛkṣa ādi padāni eva ityādi subantāni eva padāni yadi śabda nibandhane pramāṇaḥ ucyeran na syāt doṣaḥ tathā hi teṣām pariniṣpanna rūpaḥ arthaḥ idam tat iti pratyavamarśa yogyaḥ buddhau sanniviśate iti tena saha abheda upacāraḥ sambhavati śabdasya na tu nāma padāni eva pariniṣpanna artha abhidhāyīni ucyante kim tarhi taṅantāni api yat āha ākhyāta śabdaiḥ api ityādi ākhyāta śabdaiḥ pacati paṭhati iti evamādibhiḥ aliṅga asaṅkhyā pūrva aparībhūta avayavā pariniṣpanna svarūpā kriyā ucyate na ca tathāvidhasya arthasya idam tat iti agṛhītasya buddyā śakyaḥ abheda upacāraḥ kartum na api pariniṣpanna rūpaḥ śabda ātmā śādyamāna ākāra tām pratipadyate 
[II,25,i_II,25,iii]	yeṣām ca vākyam eva śabdaḥ iti tena arthasya śabdanāt yadi vākyam eva śabdaḥ padānām upādānam kimartham iti āha tad adhigama upāyaḥ ca ityādi tad samudāya ātmaka tvāt yathā varṇāḥ padānām iti manyate teṣām na asti ityādi vākya arthaḥ hi bāhyaḥ vā syāt sādhya sādhana sambandha ātmā sādhana śakti niveśa anugṛhītā niravayavā kriyā vā āntaraḥ va pratibhā lakṣaṇaḥ trayam api ca etat asattva bhūtam idam tat iti pratyavamarśa atikrāntam na ca tathābhūtena arthena saḥ ayam iti abheda upacāraḥ śakyaḥ kartum iti viśeṣa leśam iti dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam śabdena ca abheda upacāraḥ viśeṣa leśaḥ 
[II,26,i^1]	yadi tarhi na bhidyate tvayā ca āgamika tvam vāyu ādīnām pratipādayatā sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvam śābdasya pratipāditam evam satya āgama anumānayoḥ abhedāt siddhim sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvam iti āha tatra śabda vinirmuktam ityādi tatra iti śāstre śāstra nimittam iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati bhavatām sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam śāstram iti abhyupagamaḥ tatas yat etat amu mānam sparśaḥ ca na ca dṛṣṭānām sparśaḥ ityādinā upanyastam etat yuṣmad śāstrāt eva nimittāt a sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam uktam āgamika tvam bhavatām eva prasiddham bruvatā na tu sva prasiddhim iti kim sandhāya evam uktam iti āha 
[II,26,i^2]	śabda mi nirmuktam liṅgam abhisandhāya iti śabdena āgama ākhyena tyaktam etat liṅgam sparśa ākhyam tad nirapekṣaḥ eva sa yasmāt vāyoḥ sattām sādhayati tat evam tvad abhyupagata śāstra vaśāt akiñcitkaram liṅgam abhipretya tad jam anu mānam mayā idam asva lakṣaṇa viṣayam uktam na punar svayam āgamika tvam vāyu ādīnām icchata iti acodyam evam tarhi śābdam api yathā sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam na bhavati pratipādyatām iti atas pratipādayitum āha śābdam api tu ityādi sambandha abhāvaḥ iti saṅketa kāle śabda artha sambandha abhijñaḥ hi saṅketa kāla anubhūta artha sāmānyam eva pratipadyate śabdāt na sva lakṣaṇam tasya pūrvam adṛṣṭa tvāt prayoga kāle viśeṣa viṣaya tva āśaṅkā na bhavati eva saṅketa kāle tu pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇam iti sambhavati tad viṣaya tva āśaṅkā atas sambandha abhāvaḥ iti āha 
[II,27,i]	dṛṣṭa artham yatra arthaḥ pratyakṣeṇa dṛśyate adṛṣṭa artham viparyayāt dṛṣṭa arthe sañjñāvyutpattiḥ iti yathā ayam panasaḥ iti atra sambandha vyutpattiḥ eva bhavati na anumānam arthasya pratyakṣa tvāt adṛṣṭa arthe svarga ādau artha vikalpa mātram iti na hi svarga ādi śabdāḥ svarga ādīnām saṅketa kāle anyadā vā sva lakṣaṇam buddha ā arpayanti anatīndriya tva prasaṅgāt kevalam tad pratipādana abhiprāyaiḥ prayuktāḥ śrotarya pratibhā samāna tad svabhāvam artha bimbam arpayanti asti kaścid sura adhivāsa viśeṣaḥ iti evam ādikam na ca evam sva lakṣaṇam pratipannam bhavati pratipāditam vā svarga ādi śravaṇe tad anubhāvinām iva pratibhāsa bheda prasaṅgāt apratipadyamānaḥ api ca tad svabhāvam tathābhūtaḥ eva vikalpa pratibimbe tat adhyavasāyī santuṣyati
[II,28,i_II,28,ii]	tathābhūta tvāt eva śabda artha pratipatteḥ atra ca sambandha abhāvaḥ iti etat na apekṣyate kim tu dṛṣṭa artheṣu eva tatra hi dṛṣṭa tvāt viśeṣasya tasya eva vācya tā āśaṅkyeta tatas tad nivṛtti artham uktam sañjñāvyutpattiḥ iti katham tarhi tasya anumāna tvam iti api nāma āgamāt puruṣa upayoginam artham atīndriyam niścitya yathārham anutiṣṭhan āsādayā iyam iti āgamaḥ mṛgyate tatas ced artha vikalpa mātram bhavati na viśiṣṭa artha pratītiḥ tasya anumāna tvam eva hīyate iti abhiprāyaḥ nanu ca yathā anāpta prayuktānām śabdānām vivakṣā lakṣaṇam yad artha mātram tad vacanāt eva anumāna tvam na tu bāhyasya arthasya abhidhānāt tathā āpta prayuktānām api syāt iti atas āha na hi ityādi evam manyate na āpta vacasaḥ vivakṣā mātre prāmāṇyameṣṭavyam api tu bāhye api arthe anyathā kaḥ tasya anāpta vacanāt viśeṣaḥ syāt tasmāt na āpta prayuktaiḥ svarga ādi śabdaiḥ artha mātram ucyate kim tarhi laukika śabda asā dhāraṇaḥ bāhyaḥ api arthaḥ iti 
[II,28,iii]	na sva lakṣaṇa vacanāt āgamānām anumāna tvam kim tarhi tathāvidham artha vikalpa mātram upajanayatām sāmānya ākāreṇa artha prakāśanāt tatra ca avisaṃvādāt iti darśayan āha āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt ityādi āpta vacasaḥ atyanta parokṣa artha viṣayasya itareṇa pratyakṣa anumāna dṛṣṭa artha viṣayeṇa āptavacanena avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tvam iti vākya arthaḥ 
[II,29,i]	nanu ca śabdānām artheṣu apratibandhāt puruṣa atiśayasya na niścetum aśakyatvāt bāhye arthe prāmāṇyam eva ayuktam satyam etat ayam punar atra abhiprāyaḥ na ayam puruṣaḥ anāśritya āgama prāmāṇyam āsitum śaktaḥ atyakṣa phalānām keṣāñcid mahā anuśaṃsa apāya śravaṇāt tad bhāve virodha adarśanāt ca tat sati pravartitavye varam evam pravṛttiḥ iti atas parīkṣayā prāmāṇyam āha tatra puruṣa arthasya śakyasya ca tad upāyasya yat pratipādana samartham tat śāstram parīkṣā arham iti tat eva parīkṣyeta anyatra avadhānasya eva ayukta tvāt tat yadi na visaṃvāda bhāj bhavati pravartamānaḥ śobheta 
[II,30,i]	āpta vacanam gṛhītvā ityādi āpta vacanam gṛhītvā avisaṃvāda adhigama hetum tasya anumāna tvam uktam kasmāt punar tasya anumāna tvam artha avisaṃvāda tulya tvāt iti vyākhyeyam kaḥ punar asya avisaṃvādaḥ pratyakṣa abhimatānām tathā abhāvaḥ atathā abhimatānām ca apratyakṣatā tathā anumāna viṣaya abhimatānām tathā abhāvaḥ atathā bhūtānām ca ananumeya tā sā iyam śakya pariccheda aśeṣa viṣaya pariśuddhiravi saṃvādaḥ tat sāmānyam anumīyate pratyakṣa anumāna agamye api arthaḥ āpta vacana tvam upalabhya yat ā āpta vacanam tad avisaṃvādi tad anya āpta vacana vat āpta vacanam ca atyanta parokṣa viṣayam kiñcid vacanam svabhāvaḥ tatas ca sva lakṣaṇam aviṣayīkurvatām api āgamānām na tad anya śabda vat vivakṣā mātre prāmāṇyam kim tarhi arthe api 
[II,30,ii_II,31,i]	atha vā anyathā āpta vacanasya avisaṃvādāt anumāna tvam ucyate heya upādeya tad upāyānām tad upadiṣṭānām avaiparītyam avisaṃvādaḥ tathā asya puruṣa artha upayoginaḥ anuṣṭhāna arhasya avisaṃvādāt viṣaya antare api tathā tva upagamaḥ na vipralambhāya anuparodhān niṣprayojana vitatha abhidhāna vaiphalyāt ca vaktuḥ tat etat agatya ubhayathā api anumāna tvam āgamasya upavarṇitam varam āgamāt pravṛttau evam pravṛttīḥ iti na khalu evam anumānam anapāyam anāntarīyaka tvāt arthaiḥ śabdānām iti 
[II,31,ii]	atra ca āpta vacanam gṛhītvā avisaṃvādaḥ anumīyate anumite tasmin paścāt tatas eva avisaṃvādāt āpta vacasaḥ anumāna tvam bhavati anumāna śabdaḥ ca atra liṅge vartate anumīyate anena iti kṛtvā anumiti kāraṇa tvāt vā avisaṃvādaḥ punar āpta vacasaḥ artha kārya tvāt tat punar pratipattuḥ abhiprāya anurodhāt na tu vastu vaśāt
