[II,110,i_II,111,i]	dvividham anumānam iti tatra viśeṣa dṛṣṭam yadā agni dhūma sambandham dṛṣṭvā tena eva dhūmena tasya eva agneḥ punar punar astitvam pratipadyate saḥ eva ayam agniḥ iti sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam yat kvacid dhūma agni sambandham dṛṣṭvā uttara kālam dhūma mātra darśanāt agni sāmānya anumānam etat api sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam anumānam dvividham pūrvavat śeṣavat ca tatra pūrvavat yadā kāraṇam anyūnam dṛṣṭvā bhaviṣyat tvam kāryasya pratipadyate tat yathā megha udayam dṛṣṭvā bhaviṣyat tvam vṛṣṭeḥ śeṣavat yadā kārya nirvṛttim dṛṣṭvā bhūta tvam kāraṇasya pratipadyate tat yathā nava vṛddha jalām nadīm dṛṣṭvā bhūta tvam meghasya tatra pūrvavat anumānam vyabhicāri śeṣavat sa vicāram avyabhicāri teṣām yat etat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam anumānam śeṣavat eṣa hetuḥ atīndriyāṇām bhāvānām samadhigamaḥ iti smṛtiḥ seṣṭā iti atra upapattim āha na hi ityādi anena yat pūrva anubhūtam tat eva idam iti pratyavamṛśati tat smṛtyātmakam yathā saḥ eva ayam dhūmaḥ iti jñānam yathā ukta dharmakam ca viśeṣa dṛṣṭam iti svabhāvam āha 
[II,111,ii]	kārya kāraṇābhyām ityādi sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam eva dvividham iti avadhāraṇasya hi anyat vaividhyava yava chedaḥ phalam tatas ca kārya kāraṇābhyām punar punar anumāna abhāva prasaṅgaḥ punar punar anumānam viśeṣa dṛṣṭam iti kṛtvā iti abhyupeta hāniḥ atha iti evamādinā api abhyupeta hānim eva āha yasmāt sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam dvividham eva iti avadhāraṇasya saṅkhyā antara vyudāsaḥ phalam tatas ca sva svāmi ādi sambandhaiḥ tad prathamam anumāna abhāvaḥ tad prathama grahaṇam punar punar anumāne viśeṣa dṛṣṭa sambhavāt kasmāt sāmānyatas dṛṣṭa abhāvaḥ iti āha na hi eṣu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ asti iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt ca sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam iṣṭam katham viśeṣa dṛṣṭa abhāvaḥ iti āha na viśeṣa grahaṇam iti dvitīya ādiṣu kṣaṇeṣu viśeṣa grahaṇam sambhavati saḥ eva ayam iti tad bhāva ākhyā iti viśeṣa grahaṇāt na tu prathame kṣaṇe 
[II,111,iii]	sambandhāḥ saptavidhā nirdiṣṭāḥ iti sva svāmi bhāva ādayaḥ anumānam dvidhā eva iti sāmānya dṛṣṭa viśeṣa dṛṣṭābhyām anyasya api sambhavāt ekaḥ tuśabdaḥ yasmāt arthe dvitīyaḥ tasmāt arthe yasmāt dvividham eva anumānam tasmāt prathamatas anumeya adhigame sva svāmi ādibhiḥ tribhiḥ yat anumāna trayam tat kva viniveśyatām na eva kvacid tasya antarbhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ traya grahaṇam prakṛti vikāra nimitta naimittika mātra mātrika bhāvānām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva antar bhāvāt 
[II,112,i_II,112,ii]	anugrāhya anugrāhaka tvāt iti upakārya upakāraka tvāt iti arthaḥ na hi upakārya upakāraka bhāvam antareṇa sva svāmi bhāvaḥ sambhavati anyathā hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt anayā diśā sahacari bhāva vadhya vadhaka sambandhayoḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhavaḥ unnīyate iti pṛthak na uktaḥ tathā hi na vinā upakāreṇa saha cari bhāvaḥ asti cakravākayoḥ maithuna sukha upasaṃhāra ādinā paraspara upakāra darśanāt vadhya vadhaka bhāvaḥ api ahi jaya nakula parājayayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva paraspara hetu tvāt sattva ādīnām iva śabda ādi bhāvena pariṇatau 
[II,112,iii]	sambandha antara abhāva prasaṅgāt iti kārya kāraṇa sambandhaḥ eva ekaḥ syāt na sambandha antaram na hi upakārya upakāraka tvena vinā sambandhaḥ sambhavati atiprasaṅgāt katham punar sambandha antara abhāvaḥ iti āhasarvatra ityādi saptabhiḥ api sambandhaiḥ anumāne kartavye pratyāyya pratyāyakābhyām sambandhibhyām kṛtaḥ parasparasya anyatarasya vā yathāsambhavam upakāraḥ vidyataḥ anyathā tayoḥ sambandhaḥ eva na syāt 
[II,113,i]	atha vā anumīyate anena iti anumānam saptavidhaḥ sambandhaḥ tasmin anumāne nimitta arthā saptamī saptavidha sambandhaḥ nimittam pratyāyya pratyāyakābhyām ityādi śeṣam pūrvavat asmin vyākhyāne yat etat codyam nanu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratyāyanāya āśrīyate anyathā vidita sambandhāt api liṅgāt prathama darśane anumānam bhavet tat katham saḥ eva upakāraḥ iti ucyate iti tasya avatāraḥ eva na asti yatas na atra pratyāyanam upakāraḥ abhisaṃhitaḥ kim tarhi sambandhinoḥ ātma bhūtaḥ anugrahaḥ 
[II,113,ii_II,113,iii]	dvidhā doṣaḥ iti ayam eva ubhaya pakṣa bhāvī phala abhāvaḥ iti artha antara vyavaccheda phala tvāt vākyānām kim hi asya ityādinā tam eva phala abhāvam darśayati nanu ca avidita dvaividhya pratipādanam eva vākyasya phalam syāt kim atra artha antara vyavacchedena kartavyam ayuktam etat artha antara vyavacchedena hi tad svarūpam pratīyate svabhāva antara vyāvṛtta rūpa tvāt tasya rūpa antaram cena na vyavacchinnam kutas tad svarūpa pratītiḥ na ca aviditam dvaividhyam kārya kāraṇa anumāna prastāvāt tatra punarvacanam niyama artham vijñāyate 
[II,114,i_II,114,ii]	tat ayuktam iti atra hetum āha sambandhinaḥ vyabhicāri tvāt iti pratibandha ādi sambhavaḥ iti pratibandhaḥ vidhura pratyaya upanipātaḥ ādi śabdāt sahakāri vaikalya sambhave liṅgī ate iti gamyate iti arthaḥ na atra upacāraḥ yuktaḥ iti upacāra nibandhanasya abhāvāt atha ityādi yaḥ hi kiñcid kāraṇam upajanita kāryam dṛṣṭvā anyat api tat jātīyam paśyan sādṛśya skhalita matiḥ etat api niyatam tat kāryam janayiṣyati iti adhyavasyati tasya kāraṇāt kārya jñānam bhavati kadācid iti vacanāt na bhavati api yasmāt bhavati tasmāt anumāna kāraṇa tvāt anumānam ucyate yasmāt kadācid na bhavati tasmāt vyabhicārī iti ucyate evam anumāna tvam vyabhicāri tvam ca uktam iti 
[II,114,iii_II,115,i]	tat na tadā tasya akāraṇa tvāt iti tadā api na eva anumāna upacāraḥ yuktaḥ anumāna kāraṇa tva abhāvāt na eva hi sa tadā anumānam iti yaḥ asau ayatha arthaḥ pratyayaḥ atas tad kāraṇe na anumāna upacāraḥ yujyate yadā api ca yathārthaḥ tadā vyabhicāritva abhāvaḥ atas na asti tat ekam yat anumānam syāt vyabhicāri ca nanu anumā na ābhāsa kāraṇam apyamānam ucyate tathā hi vaktāraḥ bhavanti yat anena anumānam upanyastam tat mayā dūṣitam iti api cavyabhicāri iti etāvataḥ arthasya vivakṣita tvāt adūṣaṇam etat iti āha yadi ca ityādi yadi kārya kāraṇa jñāne sati api punar tatas adhikam vyabhicārya vyabhicāri tvam apekṣyate sambandha antaram āgatam iti abhyupeta hānam 
[II,115,ii_II,115,iii]	yasya eva avyabhicāritā apekṣyate iti yasya eva avyabhicāritā svarūpam apekṣyate iti arthaḥ svarūpam iti etat kutas yatas avinābhauvi tvasya na anya avyabhicāritā asti tasya avyabhicāritā rūpa tvāt sarva anumāneṣu ityādinā punarvacana ānarthakyam āha atha niyama artham tat vacanam evam api sāmānyatas khalu api iti ādeḥ ānarthakyam syāt 
[II,115,iv]	sattve ca asau vicāraṇa iti sattva śabdaḥ atra svarūpa abhidhāyī kārya kāraṇa sambandhe hi anumiti hetu tvena abhyupete liṅga svarūpam eva vicārayitum yuktam kim idam kāryam syāt na syāt iti tat yathā nadī pūraḥ iti tatra hi svarūpa gataḥ eva vicāraḥ kim ayam nadī pūraḥ vṛṣṭi kṛtaḥ āhosvit na iti yadā tu asau phena kalila pāṃsula udaka ādibhiḥ cihnaiḥ niścita svarūpaḥ bhavati tadā na punar avyabhicāri tve vicāram apekṣyate na hi vṛṣṭi kārya tve niścite tatra vyabhicāri tvam āśaṅkyate kāryasya kāraṇa avyabhicārāt etat eva darśayan āha avicaritam api ityādi 
[II,116,i]	tasmāt na yuktam avadhāraṇam iti anyatas api atīndriya artha adhigamāt nanu ca na evam avadhāryate sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam eva atīndriya artha darśana hetuḥ iti katham tarhi sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam atīndriya artha upalabdhi hetuḥ eva iti evam ca anumāna antarasya atīndriya artha samadhi gama hetutva apratiṣedhāt adoṣaḥ na etat asti sarveṣām hi anumānānām apratyakṣa adhigama hetutvāt sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya api tad adhigama hetu tva prāptau punarvacane tad viparīta pratiṣedha rupaḥ niyamaḥ vijñāyate pañca pañcanakhāḥ bhakṣyāḥ iti yadvat anumāna dvayāt ca sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam pṛthakkṛtya atīndriya artha adhigama hetutvena upādīyate tatas api tasya eva tat vijñāyate tat yathā kṛṣṇā gavām sampanna kṣīratam ā iti kṛṣṇāyāḥ eva sampanna kṣīratama tvam 
[II,116,ii]	tad sadbhāvasya eva kāraṇa tvāt iti pradhāna sadbhāvasya eva tad bhāva mātreṇa hi pradhānam bheda hetuḥ na eka tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ evam manyate asataḥ hi upajanaḥ pratiṣidhyate vikāraṇām na idam vyaktam asataḥ utpadyate iti atas pāriśeṣyāt pradhāna sadbhāvāt eva utpadyante bhedāḥ sat rūpa anuvidhānāt ca bhedānām sat rūpam eva kāraṇam sat rūpam ca tasya ātma dhāraṇam svābhāvikam eva na tu sattā saṃsarga kṛtam sattāyāḥ prāk pariṇāmāt asambhavāt tathā hi āha niḥ sattā satta iti yathā ca tadā sattā na asti tathā ekatva ādayaḥ api kutas teṣām kāraṇa tvam pradhāna sadbhāvasya eva ca puruṣa autsukya vinodanāya pravṛttiḥ atas tasya eva kāraṇa tvam iti 
[II,117,i_II,118,i]	yadi evam katham tat uktam na ca kaścid pradhānasya bhedaḥ nirvartakaḥ na ca ityādi tat para abhiprāyeṇa eva evam uktam yadi paraḥ ananya tvam aṅgīkṛtya pradhāna puruṣa artha gatān daśa cūlikā arthān sādhayet sarvathā gatiḥ syāt idam tu sva abhiprāyeṇa tad sadbhāvasya eva kāraṇa tvam yuktam iti kṛtvā tasya ca bhedebhyaḥ eva iti pradhānāstitvasya 
[II,118,ii]	sattvasya bahu tvasya vā ityādinā sarvathā śabdasya artham ācaṣṭe vā śabdāt samuccaya arthāt eka tva ādeḥ bhedena abhedena vā iti sattvena vā ekena akartṛka tva ādibhiḥ vai atha vā ekena vā vītena pañcabhiḥ vai atha vā yadi puruṣāt astitva ādayaḥ bhinā atha api abhinnāḥ sarvathā anavagamaḥ iti abhyupeta hāniḥ yat akāraṇam na tat śeṣa vat anumāna avaseyam atyanta abhāva vat tathā ca puruṣaḥ vyāpaka abhāvaḥ ye tu śabda ākāra pariṇata indriya vṛtti nirbhāsāyām manaḥ vṛttau upajātāyām puṃsaḥ api tad ākāra vṛttiḥ upajāyate tasmāt vṛtti ākāra pariṇāmī puruṣaḥ iti icchantaḥ asiddha tām hetoḥ udbhāvayanti teṣām pradhāna rūpaḥ pumān prapnoti tathā hi manaḥ vṛttiḥ triguṇa ātmakā tad ākārā ca puruṣasya vṛttiḥ tatas ca asau api triguṇa ātmakā eva syāt evam ca vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ ananya tvāt puṃsaḥ api triguṇa ātmaka tvam āpannam triguṇa svabhāva tvāt ca saḥ api pradhānam eva syāt tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ pradhānasya ca eka tvam abhyupetam hīyate iti asāram etat iti 
[II,119,i_II,119,ii]	anumāna ādīni ityādi ādi śabdena śābda upamāna artha āpattayaḥ gṛhyante pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt tadvat eva iti yathā pratyakṣam dharmam pratyanimittam tathā anumāna ādīni api kutas pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt atas eva ca etāni na sūtritāni pratyakṣa ādīni hi pramāṇāni kim artham parīkṣyante codanā lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ na pratyakṣa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti jñāpayitum pratyakṣasya ca dharmam pratyanimitta tve jñāpite anyat api yat pratyakṣa pūrvam tat dharmpari jñāna nimittam na bhavati iti jñāyate eva iti kim tena sūtritena katham tarhi ṣaḍ pramāṇāni mīmāṃsāyām pratītyāni iti āha vṛtti kāraiḥ ityādi 
[II,119,iii]	tatra ityādinā dūṣaṇam āha nanu ca sūtre pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvam asūtrita tve hetu tvena upāttam vṛttau tu pramāṇa tva parijñāne yadi yat pratyakṣa pūrvakam tat pramāṇa tvena vijñāsyate iti abhidhānāt tat katham vṛtteḥ sūtra artha anugamanam sūtre pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvam asūtraṇasya pāramparyeṇa hetu tvena upāttam na sākṣāt tat eva ca pāramparyam darśayitum yadi yat pratyakṣa pūrvakam iti ādikam vivaraṇam kṛtam iti adoṣaḥ yadi punar pramāṇa parijñānam eva asūtraṇa hetuḥ avyavahitaḥ ucyeta pramāṇa parijñāna hetuḥ na uktaḥ syāt tatas ca smṛti icchā dveṣa yatna ādi pramāṇa manuṣajyate iti asya dūṣaṇasya avatāraḥ na syāt tasmāt dūṣaṇa avakāśa dānāya pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt iti uktam 
[II,120,i^1_II,120,i^2]	nanu na eva mīmāṃsāyām pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvena pramāṇa tvam uktam api tu dharmam pratyanimitta tvam eṣām ākhyātam yat āha pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt ca anumāna upamāna artha āpattīnām api akāraṇa tvam iti upavarṣeṇa api prasiddha tvāt na uktāni iti uktam pratyakṣa ādīni hi pramāṇāni prasiddhāni iti na eṣa doṣaḥ iha prasiddha tvam na asti teṣām iti jñāpitam etat bahavaḥ ca vipratipannāḥ iti anena na ca teṣām lakṣaṇam uktam yatas svarūpa avasāyaḥ syāt pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt ca dharmam pratyanimitta tā anumāna ādīnām vijñāyate eva tatas na uktāni iti vṛtti kāraiḥ vākya kāra abhiprāyam udbhāvayadbhiḥ pratyakṣa pūrvam yat tat pramāṇa tvena vijñāyate eva tatas na uktāni iti ayam api abhiprāyaḥ utprekṣitaḥ iti sambhāvyate anyathā pūrvakaḥ api abhiprāyaḥ na syāt na hi avijñāya pramāṇa antarāṇām svarūpam dharmam pratyanimitta tā śakyā vijñātum yatas sva rūpa parijñāna artham vaktavyāni syuḥ na ca uktāni tasmāt nūnam yat pratyakṣa pūrvakam tat pramāṇa tvena vijñāyate eva tatas na uktāni iti ayam api vṛtti kāraiḥ vākya kāra abhiprāyaḥ abhyūhitaḥ iti āśaṅkyate tatas ca smṛti ādīnām api pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt pramāṇa tvam prasajyate iti 
[II,121,i]	anumāna upadeśa ādi iti ādi śabdena upamāna arthāpatti grahaṇam upadeśaḥ dvividhaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ apauruṣeyaḥ ca iha pūrvasya grahaṇam itaraḥ tu pareṣām api na eva pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvena abhimataḥ 
[II,121,ii^1_II,121,ii^2]	asādhāraṇa viṣaya iti uktam iti dharmiṇaḥ aneka rūpasya iti atra pratipāditam indriya dhiyaḥ asādhāraṇa viṣaya tvam sambandhaḥ ca aneka āśrayaḥ ityādinā sādhāraṇa tvam sambandhasya darśayan yat sādhāraṇam na tat pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ sāmānya vat tathā ca sambandhaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddham udbhāvayati sāmānyasya ca adarśana pratipādanam sāmānyam yadi api ityādinā avyāptiḥ atra na aśaṅkanīyā indriya buddhiḥ hi vastu viṣaya iṣyate asādhāraṇam ca vastu na sādhāraṇam sambandhaḥ ca sādhāraṇaḥ tasmāt na vastu tatas na indriya dhiyaḥ viṣayaḥ sambandhinaḥ ca ityādi yadi sambandhinaḥ saṃyogi samavāyi ādi tvena sambandhi rūpeṇa gṛhyante evam anumāna ādi upakāriṇaḥ bhavanti ādi śabdāt upamāna ādi upakāriṇaḥ anyathā yaḥ api anagni sambandhi tvena prathamam avyutpanna agni dhūma sambandhaḥ dhūmam gṛhṇāti tasya api tatas agneḥ anumānam syāt na ca te tathā pratyakṣāḥ iti sambandha apekṣa tvāt sambandhi tvasya sambandhasya ca apratyakṣa tvāt artha ālocana mātra tvāt ca indriya dhiyaḥ sandhānam pratyasāmarthyāt sambandhi rūpeṇa grahaṇam pratyakṣeṇa teṣām na sambhavati 
[II,122,i]	dṛṣṭa sāmānyatodṛṣṭa ādi bhedāt iti dṛṣṭam yatra liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam yatra kvacid sambandha darśanāt tad sāmānya ākāreṇa atīndriya artha adhigatiḥ ādi śabdena pūrvavat ādayaḥ naiyāyika uktāḥ gṛhyante tatra ityādinā samavāya ādīnām tadvatām ca samavāyi ādīnām samavāya sama vāyi ādi rūpeṇa apratyakṣa tva abhyupagamāt para matena api tad āśrayasya anumānasya pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvam na asti iti darśayati tad matena tu iti tad mata grahaṇam sva matena saṃyoga saṃyoginoḥ api apratyakṣa tvāt tat abhyupetya iti tat matam tat śabdena sambadhyate 
[II,122,ii_II,123,iii]	na hetuḥ anumāyāḥ ca iti caśabdaḥ bhinnakramaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ ca draṣṭavyaḥ na eva hetuḥ iti arthaḥ dvayoḥ aviśeṣāt ityādi dvayoḥ api sambandhinoḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ saṃyogaḥ tatas ca ubhayoḥ api agni dhūmayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ syāt sarvathā ca sarva ātmanā saṃyogāt saṃyoginau ca na sva rūpeṇa adhigantavyau iti svarūpam yat avidita sambandhena api gṛhyate dhūma ādi rūpam tena na adhigamana arhau kasmāt iti āha na hi anumānaḥ ityādi sambandhi rūpeṇa tarhi tayoḥ adhigatayoḥ upakāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha na ca ityādi na hi indriya dhiyaḥ yogaḥ viṣayaḥ na api tat yutaḥ iti anena saṃyogi rūpeṇa saṃyoginoḥ pratyakṣatā na bhavati iti uktam 
[II,123,iv]	syāt etat na nāma pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvam anumāna ādīnām lakṣaṇam tu te ṣām yat iṣṭam tad anavadyam yatas tasya pratiṣedhaḥ na ucyate iti āha anumāna upadeśa upamānām ityādi katham punar sva abhiprāyeṇa na uktam iti āha sambandha antarasya anirdeśāt iti na hi vaiśeṣika ādi abhimata sambandhebhyaḥ anyaḥ kaścana sambandhaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ yat api idam śabareṇa sva abhiprāyeṇa kila anumānam uktam anumānam jñāta sambandhasya eka deśa darśanāt eka deśa antare asannikṛṣṭe buddhiḥ tat dvividham pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa sambandham sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca iti tat api vaiśeṣikīya anumānam eva yadi te eva sambandhāḥ vivakṣitāḥ atha anye teṣām svarūpam na nirdiṣṭam iti anirdiṣṭam eva anumānam smṛtiḥ api ca eka deśa darśanāt eka deśa antare pūrva adhigate jāyate iti sā api anumānam syāt sambandhaḥ api na indriya grāhyaḥ iti uktam tat kutas tasya pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa sambandhatā iti ayuktam etat 
[II,124,i_II,124,ii]	artha apatti abhavayoḥ tu pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate iti tayoḥ sva abhiprāyeṇa vidhānāt sthālī ādi adhiśrayaṇa ādi artha gṛhītam iti ekena ādi śabdena cūrṇī darvya ādayaḥ sādhana viśeṣāḥ gṛhyante dvitīyena ca udaka upasaṃhāra ādayaḥ vyāpāra viśeṣāḥ artha gṛhīta tvam tu pākasya tatas utpatteḥ na hi taiḥ vinā pāka niṣpattiḥ bhavati tatas anyathā anupapattyā tat sarvam artha gṛhītam eva katham punar anumānam yāvatā tri rūpāt liṅgataḥ artha dṛś anumānam uktam iti āha pacati liṅgāt eva gamyate iti pākaḥ eva hi sthālī ādīnām avinā bhāva tvāt liṅgam avinābhāvaḥ tu tatas utpatteḥ tatas dhūmāt agni anumāna vat liṅga ja tvāt anumānāt na bhidyate 
[II,125,i^1]	anye tu bhāva abhāvābhyām kārya kāraṇa pratipattim arthāpattim icchanti tām eva anye yukti ākhyam pramāṇa antaram iti yathā sati cakṣuṣi cakṣuḥ vijñānam bhavati asati na bhavati tasmāt cakṣuḥ eva tasya kāraṇam iti na hi idam anumānam yujyate dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati na ca atra pramāṇa antareṇa dṛṣṭānta siddhiḥ tathā hi yat api idam bīja aṅkura ādi dṛṣṭānta tvena iṣyate tatra api anena eva siddhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na ca etat yuktam yena eva sādhyam sādhyate tena eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ api iti
[II,125,i^2]	nidarśana anavasthā prasaṅgāt iti sā api na eva pramāṇa antaram na hi atra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sādhyate sādhya sādhanayoḥ abhedāt na hi bhāva abhāvābhyām anyaḥ hetu phala bhāvaḥ na ca tena eva tasya sādhya tvam upapadyate tasmāt atra mūḍham prati jana na khyātyā pitṛ tva vat viṣaya darśanene viṣayiṇaḥ vṛtta sambandhasya smaraṇāt vyavahāraḥ sādhyate yādṛśe viṣaye tvayā anyatra kārya kāraṇa vyavahāraḥ pravartitaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva ayam tasmāt atra api sa pravartyatām iti vyavahāre ca sādhye sambhavati dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti anumānam eva prayogaḥ tu 
[II,125,i^3_II,126,i]	yatra tad bhāva bhāvi tvam tatra kārya kāraṇa vyavahāraḥ kartavyaḥ tat yathā yatra pūrvam pravartitaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ bīja aṅkura ādau tad bhāva bhāvi tvam ca cakṣuḥ vijñānayoḥ iti svabhāvaḥ śabaraḥ tu āha arthāpattiḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā arthaḥ anyathā na upapadyate iti artha parikalpanā yathā jīvati devadatte gṛha adarśanena bahirbhāvasya adṛṣṭasya kalpanā iti atra go balīvarda nyāyena śabdāt avagatasya śruta śabdena pṛthak upādānāt dṛṣṭa śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara upalabdhe vartate yathā jīvati iti abhāva pūrvikāyāḥ arthāpatteḥ udāharaṇam gṛha adarśanena bahirbhāvasya iti jīvataḥ devadattasya gṛha adarśanam abhāva pramāṇa upalabdham bahis bhāvam antareṇa na upapadyate iti arthaḥ 
[II,126,ii]	atra yadi jīvataḥ devadattasya gṛha adarśanam bahirbhāvāt anyathā na dṛśyate iti anyathā na upapadyate iti ucyate evam sati bahirbhāvauvinābhūtam api tat na dṛṣṭam iti tathā api na upapadyate atha jīvataḥ devadattasya gṛha adarśanam bahis bhāvaḥ eva sati dṛṣṭam tad abhāve ca na dṛṣṭam iti anyathā na upapadyate iti abhidhīyate tadā tad bhāva bhāvi tvam eva anyathā anupapanna tvam uktam syāt tat ca anvaya vyatirekiṇī ā iva arthe bhavati iti na artha āpattiḥ anumānāt bhidyate prayogaḥ tu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ gṛhe na dṛśyate jīvati ca sa bahis bhavati yathā yathā ukta prakāraḥ bahis upalabhyamānaḥ yajñadattaḥ yathā ukta dharmakaḥ ca śabda avagata sattākaḥ devadattaḥ iti svabhāvaḥ 
[II,127,i_II,127,ii]	saṃśaya kāraṇa tvāt iti yat saṃśaya kāraṇam na tat pramāṇam prameya tva vat tathā ca prakrānta arthāpattiḥ iti vyāpaka viruddham āha gehe abhāvāt na caitrasya ityādi na hi gehe abhāva mātreṇa caitrasya bahirbhāva pratītiḥ bhavati anyathā śaśa viṣāṇasya api syāt geha śabdaḥ tu tatra vākye prayuktaḥ tasya bahirbhāvam gamayati 
[II,127,iii]	geha śabdasya prayoge hi vākyam etat niyamavantam abhāvam khyāpayati tathāvidha artha vivakṣāyām eva evaṃvidha vākya prayogāt yat āha yadi tu gehe bahis ca na syāt na asti iti eva ucyeta iti tasmāt vākyam etat ubhayam ākṣipati geha abhāvam ca bahirbhāvam ca ekasya api niyama yoga khyāpakasya dvitīya ākṣepana antarīyaka tvāt na tu kevalaḥ abhāvaḥ bahis bhāvam ākṣipati niyamavān ca na kevalaḥ niyamasya ubhaya rūpa tvāt tasmāt na asti gehe caitraḥ iti na abhavaḥ eva ucyate api tu bahis ca bhāvaḥ tasmāt arthāpattiḥ eva abhāvaḥ iti yathā hi sthālī ādikam antareṇa pākasya niṣpattiḥ na bhavati iti na antarīyaka tvāt sā tadā ākṣipati evam pratiṣedha niyama vivakṣāyām gṛha śabdasya prayogaḥ bahis bhāvam antareṇa na bhavati iti na antarīyaka tvāt sa tam ākṣipati tatas ca yathā pacatiḥ sthālī ādeḥ liṅgam evam evaṃvidha vākya samavāyī geha śabdaḥ api bahirbhāvasya iti tatas eva tad gatiḥ 
[II,128,i_II,128,ii]	śabaraḥ tu āha abhāvaḥ api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ na asti iti arthasya āsat nikṛṣṭasya iti pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa pañcaka abhāvaḥ indriyeṇa āsat nikṛṣṭasya arthasya na asti iti abhāve niścaya hetuḥ bhavati tasmāt abhāvaḥ pramāṇam iti vākya arthaḥ tam eva anye anupalabdhi śabdena vyapadiśantaḥ pramāṇa antara vādinaḥ āhuḥ upalabdhyā yayā yaḥ arthaḥ jñāyate tad abhāvataḥ nāstitvam jñāyate tasya anupalabdhiḥ iyam matā iti atra api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ agṛhītaḥ vastu abhāva grahaṇa kāraṇam na bhavati atha grahaṇa apekṣaḥ sa vastu abhāva grahaṇe vyāpriyate anavasthā syāt yathā hi ghaṭa abhāvaḥ pramāṇa abhāvena gṛhyate tathā pramāṇa abhāvaḥ api apareṇa saḥ api apareṇa iti anavasthitiḥ ekasya api ca agrahaṇe sarveṣām agrahaṇam iti kutas tasya prāmāṇyam agṛhītasya api indriya vat grahaṇa kāraṇa tvam syāt iti ced na abhāvasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt anyathā bhāvaḥ eva syāt artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāvasya iti na abhāvaḥ pramāṇam 
[II,129,i]	tava api tarhi anupalabdhiḥ na syāt pramāṇam yathā uktāt eva doṣāt na etat asti na hi mayā evaṃvidha anupalabdhiḥ iṣyate api tu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ upalambha pratyaya antara sākalyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yaḥ svabhāvaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavati tatra upalabdhiḥ kartṛ sthā vā kriyā syāt karma sthā vā pūrva kalpaḥ upalabhamānasya dharmaḥ jñānam upalabdhiḥ tatas anya upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣya asparśanīya vat yadā tu karma sthā kriyā upalabdhi śabdena ucyate tadā upalabhyamānasya eva dharmaḥ sva viṣaya jñāna janana yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ upalabdhiḥ viṣaya svabhāvaḥ eva yogyatāyāḥ bhāva rūpa tvāt tasmāt anyaḥ upalambha yogyaḥ eva tad eka jñāna saṃsṛṣṭa svabhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ sa ca ayam yathā upavarṇitaḥ dvi prakāraḥ api anupalambhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati iti na asmākam yathā ukta doṣa sambhavaḥ 
[II,130,i]	bhavatu nāma evaṃvidha anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam sā punar katham anumānam katham ca na syāt dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt na hi asyām kaścid dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti pramāṇa siddhaḥ hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati anyathā yadi anupalabdhi siddhaḥ eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ syāt evam sati yathā ghaṭa abhāvaḥ dṛṣṭāntena sādhyate tathā dṛṣṭāntaḥ api nirupākhyam vyoma kusuma ādi apareṇa dṛṣṭāntena sādhyeta saḥ api apareṇa iti anavasthā prasajyeta atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭāntena vinā api sidhyati ghaṭa abhāvaḥ api sidhyet tatas ca pramāṇa antaram eva anupalabdhiḥ syāt dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt iti 
[II,130,ii]	na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi apalambhena abhāvaḥ sādhyate kim tarhi abhāva vyavahāraḥ nimittam hi asat vyavahārasya upalabhya anupalabdhiḥ sā sva sannidhānāt sva nimittam enam sādhayati iti sva nimitta sāmagrī bhāvī sarve atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhe api sādhye dṛśya anupalabdhyā itarayā ca nimitta vaikalya abhāvinaḥ aṅkura ādayaḥ api dṛṣṭāntaḥ na kevalam nirupākhyam eva iti na pramāṇa antara tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[II,130,iii_II,131,ii]	kim punar kāraṇam abhāvaḥ eva na sādhyate bheda abhāvāt tathā hi upalabdhiḥ eva dṛśya ātmanām sattā anupalabdhiḥ ca asattā katham kṛtvā yadā tāvat yathā uktā sva viṣaya jñāna janana yogyatā upalabdhiḥ tadā yogyatāyāḥ svabhāva bhūta tvāt upalabdhiḥ sattā iti siddham etat yadā api kartṛ dharmaḥ jñānam upalabdhiḥ tadā api sā dṛśyasya arthasya sattā nibandhana tvāt tad vyāpti avyatirekābhyām tad svabhāvā viśiṣṭa iti sattāvat upacārāt sattā eva tat evam ubhayathā api upalabdhiḥ sattā tad abhāvaḥ ca asattā paryudāsa vṛttyā pūrvavat sā eva ca anupalabdhiḥ iti na asti sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhedaḥ tat na abhāvaḥ anupalabdhyā sādhyate tasmāt nimitta upadarśanena na asti iti anupalabdheḥ asat vyavahāraḥ sādhyate muḍham prati jana na khyātyā pitṛ tva vat adṛśya anupalambhena api nimitta abhāvāt vyavahāra pratiṣedha ajana nakhyāti ā pitṛtva vat iti yā atra para pakṣa pratiṣedhena ityādi yat uktam bhāṣya kāreṇa para pakṣa pratiṣedhena sva pakṣa siddhiḥ iti tad pratiṣedhaḥ sāṅkhyīya avīta pratiṣedhāt eva kṛtaḥ veditavyaḥ ayam api āvīta prayogaḥ eva iti kṛtvā iti dvitīyaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ
